$app  = \Joomla\CMS\Factory::getApplication();
$user = \Joomla\CMS\Factory::getUser();
$db   = \Joomla\CMS\Factory::getDbo();

\Joomla\CMS\Factory::getDocument()->setCharset('utf-8');

|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
| Workspace Mode Controller
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
| real   = logged-in user sees their real workspace
| demo   = guest sees the real workspace in read-only demo mode
| preview= guest is redirected to the public preview page
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
*/
/*
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
| Workspace Mode Controller
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
| real   = logged-in user sees their real workspace
| demo   = guest sees the real workspace in read-only demo mode
| preview= guest is redirected to the public preview page
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
*/
$__mlePreviewUrl = \Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::base() . 'lottoexpert-preview';
$__mleMode       = 'real';
$__mleDemoUserId = 555; // your demo account user ID

if ($user->guest) {
    $__mleRequestedView = strtolower(trim($app->input->getString('mle_view', 'preview')));

    if ($__mleRequestedView === 'demo') {
        $__mleMode = 'demo';
        $user = \Joomla\CMS\Factory::getUser($__mleDemoUserId);

        if (empty($user->id)) {
            $app->enqueueMessage('Demo workspace is not available right now.', 'warning');
            $app->redirect($__mlePreviewUrl);
            exit;
        }
    } else {
        $app->redirect($__mlePreviewUrl);
        exit;
    }
}

if (!defined('MLE_DEMO_MODE')) {
    define('MLE_DEMO_MODE', $__mleMode === 'demo');
}

/*
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
| Hard fail-safe: never allow user id 0 past the access controller
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
| If the workspace user is still 0 here, do not allow reads, writes,
| saves, deletes, or preference changes to continue.
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
*/
$workspaceUserId = (int) $user->id;
if ($workspaceUserId <= 0) {
    $app->enqueueMessage('Workspace is not available right now.', 'warning');
    $app->redirect($__mlePreviewUrl);
    exit;
}

// --------------------------------------------------
/**
 * User profile prefs (stored in #__user_profiles)
 */
function mylottoexpertGetUserPref($db, $userId, $key, $default = '1') {
    $userId = (int) $userId;
    if ($userId <= 0) {
        return (string) $default;
    }

    $query = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select($db->quoteName('profile_value'))
        ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_profiles'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $userId)
        ->where($db->quoteName('profile_key') . ' = ' . $db->quote('mylotto.' . $key))
        ->order($db->quoteName('ordering') . ' ASC')
        ->setLimit(1);

    $db->setQuery($query);
    $val = $db->loadResult();

    if ($val === null || $val === '') {
        return $default;
    }

    $decoded = json_decode($val, true);
    if (json_last_error() === JSON_ERROR_NONE) {
        return (string) ($decoded ?? $default);
    }

    return (string) $val;
}
function mylottoexpertSetUserPref($db, $userId, $key, $value) {
    $userId = (int) $userId;
    if ($userId <= 0) {
        return false;
    }

    $value = (string) $value;

    $query = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select('COUNT(*)')
        ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_profiles'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $userId)
        ->where($db->quoteName('profile_key') . ' = ' . $db->quote('mylotto.' . $key));

    $db->setQuery($query);
    $exists = (int) $db->loadResult() > 0;

    if ($exists) {
        $query = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->update($db->quoteName('#__user_profiles'))
            ->set($db->quoteName('profile_value') . ' = ' . $db->quote(json_encode($value)))
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $userId)
            ->where($db->quoteName('profile_key') . ' = ' . $db->quote('mylotto.' . $key));
    } else {
        $columns = ['user_id','profile_key','profile_value','ordering'];
        $values  = [
            $userId,
            $db->quote('mylotto.' . $key),
            $db->quote(json_encode($value)),
            0
        ];
        $query = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_profiles'))
            ->columns(array_map([$db,'quoteName'], $columns))
            ->values(implode(',', $values));
    }

    $db->setQuery($query);
    $db->execute();

    return true;
}

/**
 * Format a percentage for labels without unnecessary trailing zeros.
 */
function mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($value)
{
    if ($value === null || $value === '') {
        return '';
    }

    $value = round((float)$value, 1);

    if (abs($value - round($value)) < 0.05) {
        return (string)((int)round($value));
    }

    return rtrim(rtrim(number_format($value, 1, '.', ''), '0'), '.');
}

function mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($value)
{
    $value = strtolower(trim((string)$value));
    $value = preg_replace('/[^a-z0-9]+/', ' ', $value);
    return trim(preg_replace('/\s+/', ' ', $value));
}

function mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($value)
{
    if ($value === null || $value === '') {
        return null;
    }

    $value = (float)$value;
    if ($value < 0) {
        $value = 0.0;
    }
    if ($value > 100) {
        $value = 100.0;
    }

    return $value;
}

function mylottoexpertResolveBlendStrategyLabel($strategyKey, $ai)
{
    $canonicalMap = array(
        'skip pattern boost' => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'skip pattern'       => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'skip forward'       => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'skip heavy'         => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'skip boost'         => 'Skip Pattern Boost',
        'balanced mix'       => 'Balanced Mix',
        'balanced'           => 'Balanced Mix',
        'ai forward'         => 'AI-Forward',
        'ai heavy'           => 'AI-Forward',
        'ai forward blend'   => 'AI-Forward'
    );

    if ($strategyKey !== '' && isset($canonicalMap[$strategyKey])) {
        return $canonicalMap[$strategyKey];
    }

    if ($ai !== null) {
        if ($ai >= 65) {
            return 'AI-Forward';
        }
        if ($ai <= 40) {
            return 'Skip Pattern Boost';
        }
        return 'Balanced Mix';
    }

    return '';
}

function mylottoexpertResolveBlendExplanation($strategyLabel)
{
    if ($strategyLabel === 'AI-Forward') {
        return 'More AI-driven weighting';
    }
    if ($strategyLabel === 'Balanced Mix') {
        return 'Balanced SKAI mix';
    }
    if ($strategyLabel === 'Skip Pattern Boost') {
        return 'More skip-pattern emphasis';
    }
    return '';
}

function mylottoexpertBuildSimpleModeLabel($value)
{
    $value = trim((string)$value);
    if ($value === '') {
        return '';
    }
    $value = str_replace(array('_', '-'), ' ', $value);
    return ucwords($value);
}

function mylottoexpertBuildSimpleBlendLabel(array $blendInfo)
{
    $aiText = mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($blendInfo['ai'] ?? null);
    $skipText = mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($blendInfo['skip'] ?? null);
    $strategy = (string)($blendInfo['strategy_label'] ?? '');

    if ($strategy === 'AI-Forward') {
        return 'AI Forward' . ($aiText !== '' ? ' ' . $aiText . '%' : '');
    }
    if ($strategy === 'Balanced Mix') {
        return 'Balanced' . ($aiText !== '' ? ' ' . $aiText . '%' : '');
    }
    if ($strategy === 'Skip Pattern Boost') {
        return 'Skip' . ($skipText !== '' ? ' ' . $skipText . '%' : '');
    }
    if ($aiText !== '') {
        if ((float)($blendInfo['ai'] ?? 0) >= 65) {
            return 'AI Forward ' . $aiText . '%';
        }
        if ((float)($blendInfo['ai'] ?? 0) <= 40 && $skipText !== '') {
            return 'Skip ' . $skipText . '%';
        }
        return 'Balanced ' . $aiText . '%';
    }
    if ($skipText !== '') {
        return 'Skip ' . $skipText . '%';
    }
    return '';
}

function mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings)
{
    $skip = null;
    $ai   = null;

    if (is_array($settings)) {
        $settingsPairs = array(
            array('skai_blend_skip_pct', 'skai_blend_ai_pct'),
            array('blend_skip_pct', 'blend_ai_pct'),
            array('skip_pct', 'ai_pct')
        );

        foreach ($settingsPairs as $pair) {
            if ($skip === null && array_key_exists($pair[0], $settings) && $settings[$pair[0]] !== '' && $settings[$pair[0]] !== null) {
                $skip = mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($settings[$pair[0]]);
            }
            if ($ai === null && array_key_exists($pair[1], $settings) && $settings[$pair[1]] !== '' && $settings[$pair[1]] !== null) {
                $ai = mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($settings[$pair[1]]);
            }
        }
    }

    if ($skip === null) {
        foreach (array('skai_blend_skip_pct', 'blend_skip_pct', 'skip_pct') as $rowKey) {
            $rowSkip = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $rowKey);
            if ($rowSkip !== null && $rowSkip !== '') {
                $skip = mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($rowSkip);
                break;
            }
        }
    }
    if ($ai === null) {
        foreach (array('skai_blend_ai_pct', 'blend_ai_pct', 'ai_pct') as $rowKey) {
            $rowAi = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $rowKey);
            if ($rowAi !== null && $rowAi !== '') {
                $ai = mylottoexpertClampBlendPercent($rowAi);
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    $strategyKey = '';
    if (is_array($settings)) {
        if (!empty($settings['strategy'])) {
            $strategyKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($settings['strategy']);
        } elseif (!empty($settings['blend'])) {
            $strategyKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($settings['blend']);
        }
    }

    if ($strategyKey === '') {
        $rowStrategy = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'strategy');
        $rowBlend = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'blend');
        if ($rowStrategy !== null && $rowStrategy !== '') {
            $strategyKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($rowStrategy);
        } elseif ($rowBlend !== null && $rowBlend !== '') {
            $strategyKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeBlendKey($rowBlend);
        }
    }

    if ($skip === null && $ai === null && $strategyKey !== '') {
        $presetMap = array(
            'skip pattern boost' => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'skip pattern'       => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'skip forward'       => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'skip heavy'         => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'skip boost'         => array(75.0, 25.0),
            'balanced mix'       => array(45.0, 55.0),
            'balanced'           => array(45.0, 55.0),
            'ai forward'         => array(25.0, 75.0),
            'ai heavy'           => array(25.0, 75.0),
            'ai forward blend'   => array(25.0, 75.0)
        );
        if (isset($presetMap[$strategyKey])) {
            $skip = $presetMap[$strategyKey][0];
            $ai   = $presetMap[$strategyKey][1];
        }
    }

    if ($skip === null && $ai !== null) {
        $derivedSkip = 100.0 - (float)$ai;
        if ($derivedSkip >= 0 && $derivedSkip <= 100) {
            $skip = $derivedSkip;
        }
    }
    if ($ai === null && $skip !== null) {
        $derivedAi = 100.0 - (float)$skip;
        if ($derivedAi >= 0 && $derivedAi <= 100) {
            $ai = $derivedAi;
        }
    }

    $strategyLabel = mylottoexpertResolveBlendStrategyLabel($strategyKey, $ai);
    $aiText = mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($ai);
    $skipText = mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($skip);
    $primary = '';
    if ($strategyLabel !== '' && $aiText !== '') {
        $primary = $strategyLabel . ' - AI ' . $aiText . '%';
    } elseif ($strategyLabel !== '') {
        $primary = $strategyLabel;
    } elseif ($aiText !== '') {
        $primary = 'AI ' . $aiText . '%';
    } elseif ($skipText !== '') {
        $primary = 'Skip ' . $skipText . '%';
    }
    $technical = '';
    if ($skip !== null && $ai !== null) {
        $technical = 'Skip ' . mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($skip) . '% | AI ' . mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($ai) . '%';
    } elseif ($ai !== null) {
        $technical = 'AI ' . mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($ai) . '%';
    } elseif ($skip !== null) {
        $technical = 'Skip ' . mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($skip) . '%';
    }

    return array(
        'skip' => $skip,
        'ai' => $ai,
        'strategy_key' => $strategyKey,
        'strategy_label' => $strategyLabel,
        'explanation' => mylottoexpertResolveBlendExplanation($strategyLabel),
        'primary' => $primary,
        'technical' => $technical
    );
}

function mylottoexpertResolveBlendPair($row, $settings)
{
    $blendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings);
    return array($blendInfo['skip'], $blendInfo['ai']);
}

/**
 * Build a human-readable SKAI share used label from the resolved settings source of truth.
 */
function mylottoexpertBuildSkaiBlendLabel($row)
{
    $settings = mylottoexpertResolveEffectiveSettings($row);
    $blendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings);
    return (string)$blendInfo['primary'];
}

function mylottoexpertNormalizeLotteryKey($value)
{
    $value = (string)$value;
    $value = strtolower(trim($value));
    $value = preg_replace('/[^a-z0-9]+/', ' ', $value);
    $value = trim(preg_replace('/\s+/', ' ', $value));
    return $value;
}

function mylottoexpertIsEuroMillionsLottery($stateName, $gameName)
{
    $stateKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeLotteryKey($stateName);
    $gameKey  = mylottoexpertNormalizeLotteryKey($gameName);
    $comboKey = trim($stateKey . ' ' . $gameKey);

    return ($gameKey === 'euromillions'
        || $gameKey === 'euro millions'
        || $comboKey === 'euromillions'
        || $comboKey === 'euro millions'
        || $stateKey === 'euromillions'
        || $stateKey === 'euro millions');
}

function mylottoexpertBuildEuroMillionsLogoPath($gameName)
{
    $gameName = (string)$gameName;
    $candidates = array(
        '/images/lottodb/us/uk/euromillions.png',
        '/images/lottodb/us/UK/euromillions.png'
    );

    foreach ($candidates as $rel) {
        if ($rel !== '' && is_file(JPATH_ROOT . $rel)) {
            return array(
                'path'   => $rel,
                'exists' => true,
                'alt'    => ($gameName !== '' ? $gameName : 'EuroMillions') . ' logo'
            );
        }
    }

    return array(
        'path'   => $candidates[0],
        'exists' => false,
        'alt'    => ($gameName !== '' ? $gameName : 'EuroMillions') . ' logo'
    );
}

function mylottoexpertIsMillionaireForLifeLottery($lotteryName, $gameId = '', $stateName = '')
{
    $lotteryKey = mylottoexpertNormalizeLotteryKey($lotteryName);
    $gameKey    = mylottoexpertNormalizeLotteryKey($gameId);
    $stateKey   = mylottoexpertNormalizeLotteryKey($stateName);
    $combo      = trim($lotteryKey . ' ' . $gameKey . ' ' . $stateKey);

    return (
        strpos(' ' . $combo . ' ', ' millionaire for life ') !== false
        || strpos(' ' . $combo . ' ', ' millionaire 4 life ') !== false
        || strpos(' ' . $combo . ' ', ' millionaire4life ') !== false
        || $lotteryKey === 'mfl'
        || $gameKey === 'mfl'
    );
}

function mylottoexpertResolveDisplayLocationMeta($stateName, $countryName, $lotteryName, $gameId = '')
{
    $stateName   = trim((string)$stateName);
    $countryName = trim((string)$countryName);
    $lotteryName = trim((string)$lotteryName);
    $gameId      = trim((string)$gameId);

    if (mylottoexpertIsEuroMillionsLottery($stateName, $lotteryName)) {
        $countryName = 'Multi-Country';
        $stateName   = '';
    } elseif (mylottoexpertIsMillionaireForLifeLottery($lotteryName, $gameId, $stateName)) {
        $countryName = 'Multi-State';
        $stateName   = '';
    }

    return array(
        'state'   => $stateName,
        'country' => $countryName,
        'lottery' => $lotteryName,
        'game_id' => $gameId
    );
}

function mylottoexpertBuildLotteryLocationParts($stateName, $countryName, $lotteryName = '', $gameId = '')
{
    $meta = mylottoexpertResolveDisplayLocationMeta($stateName, $countryName, $lotteryName, $gameId);
    $parts = array();

    if ($meta['country'] !== '') {
        $parts[] = (string)$meta['country'];
    }
    if ($meta['state'] !== '' && strtolower((string)$meta['state']) !== 'lottery') {
        $parts[] = (string)$meta['state'];
    }
    if ($meta['lottery'] !== '') {
        $parts[] = (string)$meta['lottery'];
    }

    return $parts;
}

function mylottoexpertFormatLotteryLocationLine($stateName, $countryName, $lotteryName = '', $gameId = '', $separator = ' | ')
{
    $parts = mylottoexpertBuildLotteryLocationParts($stateName, $countryName, $lotteryName, $gameId);
    return implode((string)$separator, $parts);
}

function mylottoexpertIsValidSavedLabel($label)
{
    $label = trim((string)$label);
    if ($label === '') {
        return false;
    }

    return !in_array(strtolower($label), array('default', 'n/a', 'na', '-', '--', 'null'), true);
}

function mylottoexpertFormatPrecisePercent($value)
{
    if ($value === null || $value === '') {
        return '';
    }
    return number_format((float)$value, 2, '.', '');
}

function mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $key)
{
    if (is_array($row)) {
        return array_key_exists($key, $row) ? $row[$key] : null;
    }
    if (is_object($row)) {
        return isset($row->$key) ? $row->$key : null;
    }
    return null;
}

function mylottoexpertNormalizeTargetSession($value)
{
    $value = strtolower(trim((string)$value));
    $value = preg_replace('/[^a-z0-9]+/', '_', $value);
    return trim((string)$value, '_');
}

function mylottoexpertBuildPredictionTarget(array $args)
{
    $timezoneId  = trim((string)($args['timezone_id'] ?? 'America/New_York'));
    $gameId      = trim((string)($args['game_id'] ?? ''));
    $lotteryId   = (int)($args['lottery_id'] ?? 0);
    $drawDate    = trim((string)($args['draw_date'] ?? ''));
    $drawAtRaw   = trim((string)($args['draw_at'] ?? ''));
    $drawSession = mylottoexpertNormalizeTargetSession($args['draw_session'] ?? '');
    $family      = strtolower(trim((string)($args['prediction_family'] ?? 'regular')));
    $type        = strtolower(trim((string)($args['prediction_type'] ?? $family)));
    $pickSize    = (int)($args['pick_size'] ?? 0);
    $extraCount  = (int)($args['extra_count'] ?? 0);

    $drawAtSql = null;
    if ($drawAtRaw !== '') {
        try {
            $drawAtSql = (new \Joomla\CMS\Date\Date($drawAtRaw, $timezoneId))->toSql();
        } catch (\Throwable $e) {
            $drawAtSql = null;
        }
    }

    $keyLottery = $lotteryId > 0 ? (string)$lotteryId : '0';
    $keyType    = preg_replace('/[^a-z0-9]+/i', '-', ($type !== '' ? $type : 'regular'));
    $keyDate    = preg_replace('/[^0-9\-]/', '', ($drawDate !== '' ? $drawDate : 'undated'));
    $keySession = preg_replace('/[^a-z0-9]+/i', '-', ($drawSession !== '' ? $drawSession : 'unspecified'));
    $canonicalKey = strtolower(trim($keyLottery . '-' . $keyType . '-' . $keyDate . '-' . $keySession, '-'));
    if ($canonicalKey === '') {
        $canonicalKey = '0-regular-undated-unspecified';
    }
    $targetId = 'ptg_' . substr(hash('sha256', $canonicalKey), 0, 40);

    return array(
        'prediction_target_id'     => $targetId,
        'prediction_target_key'    => $canonicalKey,
        'prediction_target_json'   => json_encode(array(
            'prediction_target_id' => $targetId,
            'canonical_key'        => $canonicalKey,
            'game_id'              => $gameId !== '' ? $gameId : null,
            'lottery_id'           => $lotteryId > 0 ? $lotteryId : null,
            'draw_date'            => $drawDate !== '' ? $drawDate : null,
            'draw_at'              => $drawAtSql,
            'draw_session'         => $drawSession !== '' ? $drawSession : null,
            'timezone_id'          => $timezoneId !== '' ? $timezoneId : null,
            'prediction_family'    => $family !== '' ? $family : null,
            'prediction_type'      => $type !== '' ? $type : null,
            'pick_size'            => $pickSize > 0 ? $pickSize : null,
            'extra_count'          => $extraCount >= 0 ? $extraCount : 0,
        ), JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE | JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES),
        'target_game_id'           => $gameId !== '' ? $gameId : null,
        'target_lottery_id'        => $lotteryId > 0 ? $lotteryId : null,
        'target_draw_date'         => $drawDate !== '' ? $drawDate : null,
        'target_draw_at'           => $drawAtSql,
        'target_draw_session'      => $drawSession !== '' ? $drawSession : null,
        'target_timezone_id'       => $timezoneId !== '' ? $timezoneId : null,
        'target_prediction_family' => $family !== '' ? $family : null,
        'target_prediction_type'   => $type !== '' ? $type : null,
        'target_pick_size'         => $pickSize > 0 ? $pickSize : null,
        'target_extra_count'       => $extraCount >= 0 ? $extraCount : 0,
    );
}

function mylottoexpertResolvePredictionTargetMeta($row)
{
    $predictionTargetId = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'prediction_target_id') ?? ''));
    $predictionTargetKey = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'prediction_target_key') ?? ''));
    $targetGameId = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_game_id') ?? mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'game_id') ?? ''));
    $targetLotteryId = (int)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_lottery_id') ?? mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'lottery_id') ?? 0);
    $targetDrawDate = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_draw_date') ?? mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'next_draw_date') ?? ''));
    // [FIX-LEGACY-DATE] Joomla null-date sentinel ('0000-00-00*') is not a real draw date;
    // clear it so the value is treated as absent rather than propagated as an invalid string.
    if ($targetDrawDate !== '' && strncmp($targetDrawDate, '0000-00-00', 10) === 0) {
        $targetDrawDate = '';
    }
    if ($targetDrawDate !== '') {
        $ts = strtotime($targetDrawDate);
        if ($ts !== false && $ts > 0) {
            $targetDrawDate = date('Y-m-d', $ts);
        } else {
            // [FIX-LEGACY-DATE] Unparseable or pre-epoch date -> treat as absent so downstream
            // draw lookups receive an empty string rather than a garbage date.
            $targetDrawDate = '';
        }
    }
    $targetDrawAt = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_draw_at') ?? mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'next_draw_at') ?? ''));
    $targetDrawSession = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_draw_session') ?? mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'draw_session') ?? ''));
    $targetDrawSession = mylottoexpertNormalizeTargetSession($targetDrawSession);
    $targetTimezoneId = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_timezone_id') ?? mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'timezone_id') ?? 'America/New_York'));
    $targetPredictionFamily = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_prediction_family') ?? mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'prediction_family') ?? 'regular'));
    $targetPredictionType = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_prediction_type') ?? mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'prediction_type') ?? $targetPredictionFamily));
    $targetPickSize = (int)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_pick_size') ?? mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'daily_pick_size') ?? 0);
    $targetExtraCount = (int)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'target_extra_count') ?? 0);

    if ($predictionTargetId === '' || $predictionTargetKey === '') {
        $fallbackTarget = mylottoexpertBuildPredictionTarget(array(
            'game_id'           => $targetGameId,
            'lottery_id'        => $targetLotteryId,
            'draw_date'         => $targetDrawDate,
            'draw_at'           => $targetDrawAt,
            'draw_session'      => $targetDrawSession,
            'timezone_id'       => $targetTimezoneId,
            'prediction_family' => $targetPredictionFamily !== '' ? $targetPredictionFamily : 'regular',
            'prediction_type'   => $targetPredictionType !== '' ? $targetPredictionType : ($targetPredictionFamily !== '' ? $targetPredictionFamily : 'regular'),
            'pick_size'         => $targetPickSize,
            'extra_count'       => $targetExtraCount,
        ));
        if ($predictionTargetId === '') {
            $predictionTargetId = (string)($fallbackTarget['prediction_target_id'] ?? '');
        }
        if ($predictionTargetKey === '') {
            $predictionTargetKey = (string)($fallbackTarget['prediction_target_key'] ?? '');
        }
    }

    return array(
        'prediction_target_id'     => $predictionTargetId,
        'prediction_target_key'    => $predictionTargetKey,
        'target_game_id'           => $targetGameId,
        'target_lottery_id'        => $targetLotteryId,
        'target_draw_date'         => $targetDrawDate,
        'target_draw_at'           => $targetDrawAt,
        'target_draw_session'      => $targetDrawSession,
        'target_timezone_id'       => $targetTimezoneId,
        'target_prediction_family' => $targetPredictionFamily,
        'target_prediction_type'   => $targetPredictionType,
        'target_pick_size'         => $targetPickSize,
        'target_extra_count'       => $targetExtraCount,
    );
}


function mylottoexpertResolveRunLineageMeta($row)
{
    $rowId = (int)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'id') ?? 0);
    $runUuid = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'run_uuid') ?? ''));
    $snapshotRunUuid = trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'snapshot_run_uuid') ?? ''));

    $runUuid = preg_replace('/[^a-zA-Z0-9\-_.]/', '', $runUuid);
    $snapshotRunUuid = preg_replace('/[^a-zA-Z0-9\-_.]/', '', $snapshotRunUuid);

    $effectiveRunUuid = $runUuid !== '' ? $runUuid : $snapshotRunUuid;
    $identityKey = '';
    if ($effectiveRunUuid !== '') {
        $identityKey = 'runuuid:' . strtolower($effectiveRunUuid);
    } elseif ($rowId > 0) {
        $identityKey = 'rowid:' . $rowId;
    }

    return array(
        'row_id'             => $rowId,
        'run_uuid'           => $runUuid,
        'snapshot_run_uuid'  => $snapshotRunUuid,
        'effective_run_uuid' => $effectiveRunUuid,
        'run_identity_key'   => $identityKey,
    );
}

function mylottoexpertGenerateRunUuid()
{
    try {
        return sprintf(
            '%04x%04x-%04x-%04x-%04x-%04x%04x%04x',
            random_int(0, 0xffff), random_int(0, 0xffff), random_int(0, 0xffff),
            random_int(0, 0x0fff) | 0x4000, random_int(0, 0x3fff) | 0x8000,
            random_int(0, 0xffff), random_int(0, 0xffff), random_int(0, 0xffff)
        );
    } catch (\Throwable $e) {
        return uniqid('mle_run_', true);
    }
}

function mylottoexpertEnsureUserSavedNumbersPlayColumns($db)
{
    $prefix  = $db->getPrefix();
    $rawName = $prefix . 'user_saved_numbers';

    $requiredCols = array(
        'save_intent'       => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `save_intent` varchar(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `source`",
        'origin_source'     => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `origin_source` varchar(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `save_intent`",
        'play_status'       => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `play_status` varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'draft' AFTER `origin_source`",
        'user_editable'     => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `user_editable` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 AFTER `play_status`",
        'play_notes'        => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `play_notes` text NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `user_editable`",
        'wheel_exported_at' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `wheel_exported_at` datetime NULL DEFAULT NULL AFTER `play_notes`",
        'wheel_export_count'=> "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `wheel_export_count` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 AFTER `wheel_exported_at`",
        'is_favorite_play'  => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `is_favorite_play` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 AFTER `wheel_export_count`"
    );

    foreach ($requiredCols as $colName => $alterSql) {
        try {
            $db->setQuery(
                "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS"
              . " WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = DATABASE()"
              . "   AND TABLE_NAME = " . $db->quote($rawName)
              . "   AND COLUMN_NAME = " . $db->quote($colName)
            );
            if ((int)$db->loadResult() <= 0) {
                $db->setQuery($alterSql);
                $db->execute();
            }
        } catch (Exception $e) {
        }
    }

    return true;
}

function mylottoexpertParseNumberCsv($csv, $allowZero = false)
{
    $raw = array_filter(explode(',', (string)$csv), 'strlen');
    $out = array();
    foreach ($raw as $part) {
        $n = (int)trim((string)$part);
        if ($allowZero ? ($n < 0) : ($n <= 0)) {
            continue;
        }
        if (!in_array($n, $out, true)) {
            $out[] = $n;
        }
    }
    return $out;
}

function mylottoexpertResolvePlayIntentMeta($row)
{
    $saveIntent   = strtolower(trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'save_intent') ?? '')));
    $originSource = strtolower(trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'origin_source') ?? '')));
    $playStatus   = strtolower(trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'play_status') ?? '')));
    $source       = strtolower(trim((string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'source') ?? '')));

    if ($saveIntent === '') {
        if ($source === 'strategy_set') {
            $saveIntent = 'play_set';
        } else {
            $saveIntent = 'prediction_archive';
        }
    }

    if ($originSource === '') {
        if ($source === 'strategy_set') {
            $originSource = 'strategy_builder';
        } elseif ($saveIntent === 'custom_play') {
            $originSource = 'manual';
        } else {
            $originSource = 'skai_prediction';
        }
    }

    if ($playStatus === '') {
        $playStatus = ($saveIntent === 'prediction_archive') ? 'archived' : 'ready';
    }

    return array(
        'save_intent'   => $saveIntent,
        'origin_source' => $originSource,
        'play_status'   => $playStatus
    );
}

function mylottoexpertResolvePlaySourceBadge($originSource, $saveIntent)
{
    $originSource = strtolower(trim((string)$originSource));
    $saveIntent   = strtolower(trim((string)$saveIntent));

    if ($originSource === 'strategy_builder') {
        return 'From Strategy Builder';
    }
    if ($originSource === 'manual' || $saveIntent === 'custom_play') {
        return 'Custom Selection';
    }
    if ($originSource === 'imported') {
        return 'Imported';
    }
    return 'From Prediction';
}

function mylottoexpertBuildGroupIdentity(array $targetMeta)
{
    $predictionTargetId = trim((string)($targetMeta['prediction_target_id'] ?? ''));
    if ($predictionTargetId !== '') {
        return 'target:' . $predictionTargetId;
    }
    $gameId = trim((string)($targetMeta['target_game_id'] ?? ''));
    $lotteryId = (int)($targetMeta['target_lottery_id'] ?? 0);
    $drawDate = trim((string)($targetMeta['target_draw_date'] ?? ''));
    $drawAt = trim((string)($targetMeta['target_draw_at'] ?? ''));
    $drawSession = trim((string)($targetMeta['target_draw_session'] ?? ''));
    return 'legacy:' . strtolower(implode('|', array(
        $gameId !== '' ? $gameId : '0',
        $lotteryId > 0 ? (string)$lotteryId : '0',
        $drawDate !== '' ? $drawDate : 'undated',
        $drawAt !== '' ? $drawAt : 'no-time',
        $drawSession !== '' ? $drawSession : 'no-session',
    )));
}

function mylottoexpertResolveEffectiveSettings($row)
{
    $settings = array();
    $jsonCandidates = array('settings_json', 'settings', 'params_json', 'params', 'digit_probabilities');

    foreach ($jsonCandidates as $jsonKey) {
        $rawJson = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $jsonKey);
        if ($rawJson === null || $rawJson === '') {
            continue;
        }
        $decoded = json_decode((string)$rawJson, true);
        if (json_last_error() === JSON_ERROR_NONE && is_array($decoded)) {
            $settings = $decoded;
            break;
        }
    }

    if (!is_array($settings)) {
        $settings = array();
    }

    $dbFallbackKeys = array(
        'label','skai_run_mode','pure_mode',
        'skai_blend_skip_pct','skai_blend_ai_pct',
        'blend_skip_pct','blend_ai_pct','skip_pct','ai_pct',
        'epochs','batch_size','dropout_rate','learning_rate',
        'activation_function','hidden_layers','recency_decay',
        'walks','burn_in','laplace_k','decay','chain_len',
        'draws_analyzed','freq_weight','skip_weight','hist_weight',
        'draws_used','skip_window','auto_tune','tune_used','best_window',
        'sampling_temperature','diversity_penalty','gap_scale',
        'skai_window_size','skai_top_n_numbers','skai_top_n_combos',
        'profile','training_style','risk_profile','strategy','blend','blend_percent'
    );

    foreach ($dbFallbackKeys as $key) {
        if (!array_key_exists($key, $settings) || $settings[$key] === '' || $settings[$key] === null) {
            $dbVal = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, $key);
            if ($dbVal !== null && $dbVal !== '') {
                $settings[$key] = $dbVal;
            }
        }
    }

    return $settings;
}

function mylottoexpertBuildPreciseBlendDisplay($row, $settings)
{
    $blendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings);
    return (string)$blendInfo['technical'];
}

function mylottoexpertResolveRunDisplayInfo($row, array $methodLabels)
{
    $settings = mylottoexpertResolveEffectiveSettings($row);
    $src = (string)(mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'source') ?: '');

    $baseLabel = isset($methodLabels[$src])
        ? (string)$methodLabels[$src]
        : ucwords(str_replace('_', ' ', $src));

    $savedLabel = '';
    if (isset($settings['label']) && mylottoexpertIsValidSavedLabel($settings['label'])) {
        $savedLabel = trim((string)$settings['label']);
    } else {
        $rowLabel = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'label');
        if (mylottoexpertIsValidSavedLabel($rowLabel)) {
            $savedLabel = trim((string)$rowLabel);
        }
    }

    $runModeRaw = '';
    if (!empty($settings['skai_run_mode'])) {
        $runModeRaw = (string)$settings['skai_run_mode'];
    } else {
        $rowRunMode = mylottoexpertResolveRowValue($row, 'skai_run_mode');
        if (!empty($rowRunMode)) {
            $runModeRaw = (string)$rowRunMode;
        }
    }

    $runMode = $runModeRaw !== '' ? ucwords(str_replace('_', ' ', $runModeRaw)) : '';
    $blendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($row, $settings);

    $trainingStyle = '';
    if (!empty($settings['profile'])) {
        $trainingStyle = (string)$settings['profile'];
    } elseif (!empty($settings['training_style'])) {
        $trainingStyle = (string)$settings['training_style'];
    } elseif (!empty($settings['risk_profile'])) {
        $trainingStyle = (string)$settings['risk_profile'];
    }

    $simpleModeLabel = mylottoexpertBuildSimpleModeLabel($trainingStyle !== '' ? $trainingStyle : $runMode);
    $simpleBlendLabel = mylottoexpertBuildSimpleBlendLabel($blendInfo);

    $modeDisplay = $simpleModeLabel !== '' ? 'Mode: ' . $simpleModeLabel : '';
    $modeDisplayHtml = $simpleModeLabel !== '' ? 'Mode: <strong>' . htmlspecialchars($simpleModeLabel, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8') . '</strong>' : '';

    $effectiveLabel = $savedLabel !== '' ? $savedLabel : ($runMode !== '' ? $runMode : $baseLabel);
    $effectiveLabelHtml = htmlspecialchars($effectiveLabel, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8');

    if ($src === 'skai_prediction') {
        $labelPartsPlain = array();
        $labelPartsHtml  = array();

        if ($modeDisplay !== '') {
            $labelPartsPlain[] = $modeDisplay;
            $labelPartsHtml[]  = $modeDisplayHtml;
        }
        if ($simpleBlendLabel !== '') {
            $labelPartsPlain[] = 'Label: ' . $simpleBlendLabel;
            $labelPartsHtml[]  = 'Label: <strong>' . htmlspecialchars($simpleBlendLabel, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8') . '</strong>';
        }

        if (!empty($labelPartsPlain)) {
            $effectiveLabel = implode(' | ', $labelPartsPlain);
            $effectiveLabelHtml = implode('<br>', $labelPartsHtml);
        }
    }

    return array(
        'base_label'        => $baseLabel,
        'label'             => $effectiveLabel,
        'label_html'        => $effectiveLabelHtml,
        'saved_label'       => $savedLabel,
        'mode'              => $modeDisplay,
        'mode_html'         => $modeDisplayHtml,
        'run_mode'          => $runMode,
        'blend_display'     => $simpleBlendLabel,
        'blend_technical'   => (string)$blendInfo['technical'],
        'blend_strategy'    => (string)$blendInfo['strategy_label'],
        'blend_explainer'   => (string)$blendInfo['explanation'],
        'source'            => $src,
        'settings'          => $settings
    );
}
/**
 * Derive a concise label from a saved run row for the Best Setup Snapshot.
 * Shows method name and optional run mode / template name.
 */
function mylottoexpertBuildBestSettingsSummary(array $row, array $methodLabels)
{
    $disp = mylottoexpertResolveRunDisplayInfo($row, $methodLabels);
    $label = (string)$disp['base_label'];

    $templateName = '';
    if (isset($row['template_name']) && $row['template_name'] !== null && $row['template_name'] !== '') {
        $templateName = (string)$row['template_name'];
    } elseif (isset($row['settings_template_name']) && $row['settings_template_name'] !== null && $row['settings_template_name'] !== '') {
        $templateName = (string)$row['settings_template_name'];
    }
    if ($templateName !== '') {
        return $label . ' - ' . $templateName;
    }

    if ((string)$disp['source'] === 'skai_prediction') {
        $modeLabel = (string)$disp['mode'];
        if ($modeLabel === '') {
            $modeLabel = 'Default';
        }
        return $label . ' - ' . $modeLabel;
    }

    if ($disp['saved_label'] !== '' && $disp['saved_label'] !== $label) {
        return $disp['saved_label'];
    }

    return $label;
}

function mylottoexpertBuildActionTweakFromSettings(array $settings)
{
    $src = isset($settings['source']) ? (string)$settings['source'] : '';
    $action = 'Add more saved runs before making a setting change recommendation.';
    $stable = 'Keep the current setup the same until you have enough repeated history to test one variable clearly.';

    if ($src === 'skai_prediction') {
        $bestWindowOn = (!empty($settings['best_window']) && (string)$settings['best_window'] !== '0');
        $windowSize   = isset($settings['skai_window_size']) ? (float)$settings['skai_window_size'] : 0.0;
        $autoTuneOn   = (!empty($settings['auto_tune']) && (string)$settings['auto_tune'] !== '0');
        $divPenalty   = isset($settings['diversity_penalty']) ? (float)$settings['diversity_penalty'] : 0.0;

        if (!$bestWindowOn) {
            $action = 'Turn on Best Window before changing anything else. That is the cleanest next test for this SKAI setup.';
            $stable = 'Keep the current run mode, blend, and window size unchanged while you test Best Window.';
        } elseif ($windowSize > 50) {
            $action = 'Reduce the SKAI window slightly to tighten the pool and see whether overlap improves.';
            $stable = 'Keep the current run mode and blend stable while you test a smaller window.';
        } elseif (!$autoTuneOn) {
            $action = 'Enable Auto-tune next so the setup can adapt without changing the current mode or blend.';
            $stable = 'Do not change the run mode, blend, or Best Window at the same time.';
        } elseif ($divPenalty > 0.65) {
            $action = 'Reduce diversity penalty one step to see whether the repeated-number cluster becomes tighter.';
            $stable = 'Hold the current run mode, blend, and window size steady during that test.';
        } else {
            $action = 'Increase or decrease diversity penalty one step at a time to refine clustering without breaking the current signal.';
            $stable = 'Keep the current run mode, blend, window size, and Best Window setting stable.';
        }
    } elseif ($src === 'skip_hit') {
        $skipWeight = isset($settings['skip_weight']) ? (float)$settings['skip_weight'] : 1.0;
        $histWeight = isset($settings['hist_weight']) ? (float)$settings['hist_weight'] : 1.0;
        if ($skipWeight > ($histWeight * 1.3)) {
            $action = 'Increase historical weight slightly so history has more influence against the current skip bias.';
            $stable = 'Keep draws analyzed stable while you test weighting.';
        } else {
            $action = 'Increase or decrease draws analyzed by about 20 while keeping the weight balance unchanged.';
            $stable = 'Hold skip weight and historical weight steady for the next test.';
        }
    } elseif ($src === 'mcmc_prediction') {
        $action = 'Increase or decrease chain length next while keeping the decay rate unchanged.';
        $stable = 'Keep recency decay stable so you can isolate the effect of chain length.';
    } elseif ($src === 'ai_prediction') {
        $action = 'Adjust recency decay slightly before you touch epochs or architecture.';
        $stable = 'Keep epochs, hidden layers, and dropout unchanged during that test.';
    }

    return array('action' => $action, 'stable' => $stable);
}

function mylottoexpertRenderModuleById($moduleId, $style = 'none') {
    $moduleId = (int) $moduleId;
    if ($moduleId <= 0) {
        return '';
    }

    $module = \Joomla\CMS\Helper\ModuleHelper::getModuleById($moduleId);

    if (empty($module) || empty($module->module)) {
        return '';
    }

    return \Joomla\CMS\Helper\ModuleHelper::renderModule($module, ['style' => (string) $style]);
}

// ======================================================================
// SKAI Learning performance Measurement System
// Tracks and stores prediction quality metrics per run / per draw so
// users can see whether SKAI is improving over time.
// ======================================================================

/**
 * Calculate winning rank metrics from a ranked prediction list and actual drawn numbers.
 *
 * The 'rank' of a drawn number is its 1-based position in the ranked prediction array.
 * Example: if the actual winning number is at index 4 in pred_main, its rank = 5.
 * Lower rank = better (number was predicted more confidently).
 *
 * Ties: when building $positionMap we use FIRST occurrence only.
 * Missing numbers: drawn numbers absent from the prediction list are NOT included
 *   in rank averages; they are counted separately as 'missing_count'.
 *
 * @param array $rankedNumbers  Ordered predicted numbers (rank 1 = index 0). Zeros ignored.
 * @param array $drawnNumbers   Actual drawn numbers.
 * @return array
 */
function skaiCalcWinningRankMetrics(array $rankedNumbers, array $drawnNumbers)
{
    // Build position map: number => 1-based rank. First occurrence wins ties.
    $positionMap = array();
    foreach ($rankedNumbers as $idx => $num) {
        $num = (int)$num;
        if ($num > 0 && !isset($positionMap[$num])) {
            $positionMap[$num] = $idx + 1;
        }
    }

    $ranks        = array();
    $missingCount = 0;
    foreach ($drawnNumbers as $drawn) {
        $drawn = (int)$drawn;
        if ($drawn <= 0) {
            continue;
        }
        if (isset($positionMap[$drawn])) {
            $ranks[] = $positionMap[$drawn];
        } else {
            $missingCount++;
        }
    }

    if (empty($ranks)) {
        return array(
            'ranks'          => array(),
            'avg_rank'       => null,
            'best_rank'      => null,
            'worst_rank'     => null,
            'median_rank'    => null,
            'weighted_score' => 0.0,
            'top10_hits'     => 0,
            'top20_hits'     => 0,
            'top30_hits'     => 0,
            'top50_hits'     => 0,
            'missing_count'  => $missingCount,
            'found_count'    => 0,
        );
    }

    $count   = count($ranks);
    $sum     = array_sum($ranks);
    $avgRank = round($sum / $count, 2);

    $bestRank  = min($ranks);
    $worstRank = max($ranks);

    // Median: sort ascending, pick middle element(s)
    $sorted = $ranks;
    sort($sorted);
    $mid = (int)floor($count / 2);
    if ($count % 2 === 0) {
        $medianRank = round(($sorted[$mid - 1] + $sorted[$mid]) / 2.0, 2);
    } else {
        $medianRank = (float)$sorted[$mid];
    }

    // Weighted quality score: sum of (1 / rank) for each found number.
    // Higher score = better (winning numbers appeared near the top of the ranking).
    $weightedScore = 0.0;
    foreach ($ranks as $r) {
        if ($r > 0) {
            $weightedScore += 1.0 / (float)$r;
        }
    }
    $weightedScore = round($weightedScore, 6);

    $top10Hits = 0;
    $top20Hits = 0;
    $top30Hits = 0;
    $top50Hits = 0;
    foreach ($ranks as $r) {
        if ($r <= 10) { $top10Hits++; }
        if ($r <= 20) { $top20Hits++; }
        if ($r <= 30) { $top30Hits++; }
        if ($r <= 50) { $top50Hits++; }
    }

    return array(
        'ranks'          => $ranks,
        'avg_rank'       => $avgRank,
        'best_rank'      => $bestRank,
        'worst_rank'     => $worstRank,
        'median_rank'    => $medianRank,
        'weighted_score' => $weightedScore,
        'top10_hits'     => $top10Hits,
        'top20_hits'     => $top20Hits,
        'top30_hits'     => $top30Hits,
        'top50_hits'     => $top50Hits,
        'missing_count'  => $missingCount,
        'found_count'    => $count,
    );
}

/**
 * Create the skai_learning_performance table if it does not already exist.
 * Safe to call on every page load (CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS).
 *
 * @param  object $db  Joomla DB object
 * @return bool
 */
function skaiEnsurePerformanceTable($db)
{
    $prefix  = $db->getPrefix();
    $tblName = $prefix . 'skai_learning_performance';
    $sql = "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `{$tblName}` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `lottery_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `lottery_name` varchar(191) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `draw_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `run_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `run_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `run_uuid` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `snapshot_run_uuid` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `run_identity_key` varchar(128) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `prediction_target_id` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `prediction_target_key` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `target_game_id` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `target_lottery_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `target_draw_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `target_draw_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `target_draw_session` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `target_timezone_id` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `target_prediction_family` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `target_prediction_type` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `source` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `actual_numbers_json` mediumtext,
  `predicted_ranking_json` mediumtext,
  `avg_winning_rank` decimal(8,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `best_winning_rank` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `worst_winning_rank` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `median_winning_rank` decimal(8,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `weighted_quality_score` decimal(10,6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `top10_hits` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `top20_hits` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `top30_hits` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `top50_hits` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `missing_hits_count` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `combo_hit_summary_json` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `tail_enabled` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `tail_active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `tail_promoted_count` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `tail_promoted_hit_count` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `calibration_enabled` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `calibration_active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `shared_learning_enabled` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `pairwise_enabled` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `gibbs_enabled` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `live_tuning_enabled` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  `confidence_level` varchar(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'insufficient_data',
  `trend_bucket` varchar(32) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  `notes_json` text DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_user_lottery` (`user_id`,`lottery_id`),
  KEY `idx_draw_date` (`draw_date`),
  KEY `idx_run_identity_key` (`run_identity_key`),
  KEY `idx_prediction_target_id` (`prediction_target_id`),
  KEY `idx_target_game_draw` (`target_game_id`,`target_draw_date`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uq_user_run_draw_source` (`user_id`,`run_id`,`draw_date`,`source`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uq_user_lineage_draw_source` (`user_id`,`run_identity_key`,`draw_date`,`source`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci";
    try {
        $db->setQuery($sql);
        $db->execute();
        return true;
    } catch (Exception $e) {
        return false;
    }
}

function skaiEnsurePerformanceTableSchema($db)
{
    $prefix  = $db->getPrefix();
    $rawName = $prefix . 'skai_learning_performance';

    $requiredCols = array(
        'run_uuid' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `run_uuid` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `run_id`",
        'snapshot_run_uuid' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `snapshot_run_uuid` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `run_uuid`",
        'run_identity_key' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `run_identity_key` varchar(128) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `snapshot_run_uuid`",
        'prediction_target_id' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `prediction_target_id` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `run_identity_key`",
        'prediction_target_key' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `prediction_target_key` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `prediction_target_id`",
        'target_game_id' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `target_game_id` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `prediction_target_key`",
        'target_lottery_id' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `target_lottery_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 AFTER `target_game_id`",
        'target_draw_date' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `target_draw_date` date DEFAULT NULL AFTER `target_lottery_id`",
        'target_draw_at' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `target_draw_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL AFTER `target_draw_date`",
        'target_draw_session' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `target_draw_session` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `target_draw_at`",
        'target_timezone_id' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `target_timezone_id` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `target_draw_session`",
        'target_prediction_family' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `target_prediction_family` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `target_timezone_id`",
        'target_prediction_type' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD COLUMN `target_prediction_type` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' AFTER `target_prediction_family`"
    );

    foreach ($requiredCols as $colName => $alterSql) {
        try {
            $db->setQuery(
                "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.COLUMNS"
              . " WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = DATABASE()"
              . "   AND TABLE_NAME = " . $db->quote($rawName)
              . "   AND COLUMN_NAME = " . $db->quote($colName)
            );
            if ((int)$db->loadResult() <= 0) {
                $db->setQuery($alterSql);
                $db->execute();
            }
        } catch (Exception $e) {
        }
    }

    $requiredIndexes = array(
        'idx_run_identity_key' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD KEY `idx_run_identity_key` (`run_identity_key`)",
        'idx_prediction_target_id' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD KEY `idx_prediction_target_id` (`prediction_target_id`)",
        'idx_target_game_draw' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD KEY `idx_target_game_draw` (`target_game_id`,`target_draw_date`)",
        'uq_user_lineage_draw_source' => "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` ADD UNIQUE KEY `uq_user_lineage_draw_source` (`user_id`,`run_identity_key`,`draw_date`,`source`)"
    );

    foreach ($requiredIndexes as $indexName => $alterSql) {
        try {
            $db->setQuery(
                "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.STATISTICS"
              . " WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = DATABASE()"
              . "   AND TABLE_NAME = " . $db->quote($rawName)
              . "   AND INDEX_NAME = " . $db->quote($indexName)
            );
            if ((int)$db->loadResult() <= 0) {
                $db->setQuery($alterSql);
                $db->execute();
            }
        } catch (Exception $e) {
        }
    }

    return true;
}

/**
 * Insert or update a performance record.
 * Uses UNIQUE KEY (user_id, run_id, draw_date, source) to prevent duplicates.
 * Including draw_date in the key means the same run can be scored once per draw
 * date - ensuring true historical accumulation across multiple draw cycles.
 *
 * @param  object $db
 * @param  int    $userId
 * @param  array  $data
 * @return bool
 */
function skaiUpsertPerformanceRecord($db, $userId, array $data)
{
    $userId = (int) $userId;
    if ($userId <= 0) {
        return false;
    }

    $prefix  = $db->getPrefix();
    $tblName = '`' . $prefix . 'skai_learning_performance`';
    $now     = date('Y-m-d H:i:s');

    $actualJson  = json_encode(array_values((array)($data['actual_numbers'] ?? array())), JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE);    $rankingJson = json_encode(array_values((array)($data['predicted_ranking'] ?? array())), JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE);
    $comboJson   = json_encode((array)($data['combo_hit_summary'] ?? array()), JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE);
    $notesJson   = json_encode((array)($data['notes'] ?? array()), JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE);

    $avgRank    = (isset($data['avg_winning_rank'])    && $data['avg_winning_rank']    !== null) ? round((float)$data['avg_winning_rank'],    2) : null;
    $bestRank   = (isset($data['best_winning_rank'])   && $data['best_winning_rank']   !== null) ? (int)$data['best_winning_rank']             : null;
    $worstRank  = (isset($data['worst_winning_rank'])  && $data['worst_winning_rank']  !== null) ? (int)$data['worst_winning_rank']            : null;
    $medianRank = (isset($data['median_winning_rank']) && $data['median_winning_rank'] !== null) ? round((float)$data['median_winning_rank'], 2) : null;
    $wScore     = (isset($data['weighted_quality_score']) && $data['weighted_quality_score'] !== null) ? round((float)$data['weighted_quality_score'], 6) : null;

    $runDateSql         = !empty($data['run_date'])  ? $db->quote((string)$data['run_date'])  : 'NULL';
    $drawDateSql        = !empty($data['draw_date']) ? $db->quote((string)$data['draw_date']) : 'NULL';
    $targetDrawDateSql  = !empty($data['target_draw_date']) ? $db->quote((string)$data['target_draw_date']) : 'NULL';
    $targetDrawAtSql    = !empty($data['target_draw_at']) ? $db->quote((string)$data['target_draw_at']) : 'NULL';
    $avgSql             = ($avgRank    !== null) ? $avgRank    : 'NULL';
    $bestSql            = ($bestRank   !== null) ? $bestRank   : 'NULL';
    $worstSql           = ($worstRank  !== null) ? $worstRank  : 'NULL';
    $medianSql          = ($medianRank !== null) ? $medianRank : 'NULL';
    $wSql               = ($wScore     !== null) ? $wScore     : 'NULL';

    $runUuid             = preg_replace('/[^a-zA-Z0-9\-_.]/', '', (string)($data['run_uuid'] ?? ''));
    $snapshotRunUuid     = preg_replace('/[^a-zA-Z0-9\-_.]/', '', (string)($data['snapshot_run_uuid'] ?? ''));
    $runIdentityKey      = (string)($data['run_identity_key'] ?? '');
    $predictionTargetId  = preg_replace('/[^a-zA-Z0-9\-_.]/', '', (string)($data['prediction_target_id'] ?? ''));
    $predictionTargetKey = (string)($data['prediction_target_key'] ?? '');
    $targetGameId        = (string)($data['target_game_id'] ?? '');
    $targetLotteryId     = (int)($data['target_lottery_id'] ?? 0);
    $targetDrawSession   = (string)($data['target_draw_session'] ?? '');
    $targetTimezoneId    = (string)($data['target_timezone_id'] ?? '');
    $targetPredFamily    = (string)($data['target_prediction_family'] ?? '');
    $targetPredType      = (string)($data['target_prediction_type'] ?? '');

    $sql = "INSERT INTO {$tblName}
        (`user_id`,`lottery_id`,`lottery_name`,`draw_date`,`run_date`,`run_id`,`run_uuid`,`snapshot_run_uuid`,`run_identity_key`,
         `prediction_target_id`,`prediction_target_key`,`target_game_id`,`target_lottery_id`,`target_draw_date`,`target_draw_at`,`target_draw_session`,`target_timezone_id`,`target_prediction_family`,`target_prediction_type`,`source`,
         `actual_numbers_json`,`predicted_ranking_json`,
         `avg_winning_rank`,`best_winning_rank`,`worst_winning_rank`,`median_winning_rank`,`weighted_quality_score`,
         `top10_hits`,`top20_hits`,`top30_hits`,`top50_hits`,`missing_hits_count`,`combo_hit_summary_json`,
         `tail_enabled`,`tail_active`,`tail_promoted_count`,`tail_promoted_hit_count`,
         `calibration_enabled`,`calibration_active`,
         `shared_learning_enabled`,`pairwise_enabled`,`gibbs_enabled`,`live_tuning_enabled`,
         `confidence_level`,`trend_bucket`,`notes_json`,`created_at`,`updated_at`)
        VALUES (
         " . (int)$userId . ",
         " . (int)($data['lottery_id'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . $db->quote((string)($data['lottery_name'] ?? '')) . ",
         {$drawDateSql},
         {$runDateSql},
         " . (int)($data['run_id'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . $db->quote($runUuid) . ",
         " . $db->quote($snapshotRunUuid) . ",
         " . $db->quote($runIdentityKey) . ",
         " . $db->quote($predictionTargetId) . ",
         " . $db->quote($predictionTargetKey) . ",
         " . $db->quote($targetGameId) . ",
         " . $targetLotteryId . ",
         {$targetDrawDateSql},
         {$targetDrawAtSql},
         " . $db->quote($targetDrawSession) . ",
         " . $db->quote($targetTimezoneId) . ",
         " . $db->quote($targetPredFamily) . ",
         " . $db->quote($targetPredType) . ",
         " . $db->quote((string)($data['source'] ?? '')) . ",
         " . $db->quote((string)$actualJson) . ",
         " . $db->quote((string)$rankingJson) . ",
         {$avgSql},{$bestSql},{$worstSql},{$medianSql},{$wSql},
         " . (int)($data['top10_hits'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['top20_hits'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['top30_hits'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['top50_hits'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['missing_hits_count'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . $db->quote((string)$comboJson) . ",
         " . (int)($data['tail_enabled'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['tail_active'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['tail_promoted_count'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['tail_promoted_hit_count'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['calibration_enabled'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['calibration_active'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['shared_learning_enabled'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['pairwise_enabled'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['gibbs_enabled'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . (int)($data['live_tuning_enabled'] ?? 0) . ",
         " . $db->quote((string)($data['confidence_level'] ?? 'insufficient_data')) . ",
         " . $db->quote((string)($data['trend_bucket'] ?? 'unknown')) . ",
         " . $db->quote((string)$notesJson) . ",
         " . $db->quote($now) . ",
         " . $db->quote($now) . "
        )
        ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
         `lottery_name`            = VALUES(`lottery_name`),
         `draw_date`               = VALUES(`draw_date`),
         `run_date`                = VALUES(`run_date`),
         `run_uuid`                = VALUES(`run_uuid`),
         `snapshot_run_uuid`       = VALUES(`snapshot_run_uuid`),
         `run_identity_key`        = VALUES(`run_identity_key`),
         `prediction_target_id`    = VALUES(`prediction_target_id`),
         `prediction_target_key`   = VALUES(`prediction_target_key`),
         `target_game_id`          = VALUES(`target_game_id`),
         `target_lottery_id`       = VALUES(`target_lottery_id`),
         `target_draw_date`        = VALUES(`target_draw_date`),
         `target_draw_at`          = VALUES(`target_draw_at`),
         `target_draw_session`     = VALUES(`target_draw_session`),
         `target_timezone_id`      = VALUES(`target_timezone_id`),
         `target_prediction_family`= VALUES(`target_prediction_family`),
         `target_prediction_type`  = VALUES(`target_prediction_type`),
         `actual_numbers_json`     = VALUES(`actual_numbers_json`),
         `predicted_ranking_json`  = VALUES(`predicted_ranking_json`),
         `avg_winning_rank`        = VALUES(`avg_winning_rank`),
         `best_winning_rank`       = VALUES(`best_winning_rank`),
         `worst_winning_rank`      = VALUES(`worst_winning_rank`),
         `median_winning_rank`     = VALUES(`median_winning_rank`),
         `weighted_quality_score`  = VALUES(`weighted_quality_score`),
         `top10_hits`              = VALUES(`top10_hits`),
         `top20_hits`              = VALUES(`top20_hits`),
         `top30_hits`              = VALUES(`top30_hits`),
         `top50_hits`              = VALUES(`top50_hits`),
         `missing_hits_count`      = VALUES(`missing_hits_count`),
         `combo_hit_summary_json`  = VALUES(`combo_hit_summary_json`),
         `tail_enabled`            = VALUES(`tail_enabled`),
         `tail_active`             = VALUES(`tail_active`),
         `tail_promoted_count`     = VALUES(`tail_promoted_count`),
         `tail_promoted_hit_count` = VALUES(`tail_promoted_hit_count`),
         `calibration_enabled`     = VALUES(`calibration_enabled`),
         `calibration_active`      = VALUES(`calibration_active`),
         `shared_learning_enabled` = VALUES(`shared_learning_enabled`),
         `pairwise_enabled`        = VALUES(`pairwise_enabled`),
         `gibbs_enabled`           = VALUES(`gibbs_enabled`),
         `live_tuning_enabled`     = VALUES(`live_tuning_enabled`),
         `confidence_level`        = VALUES(`confidence_level`),
         `trend_bucket`            = VALUES(`trend_bucket`),
         `notes_json`              = VALUES(`notes_json`),
         `updated_at`              = VALUES(`updated_at`)";
    try {
        $db->setQuery($sql);
        $db->execute();
        return true;
    } catch (Exception $e) {
        return false;
    }
}

/**
 * Migrate the skai_learning_performance table's unique index from the old
 * three-column key (user_id, run_id, source) to the corrected four-column key
 * (user_id, run_id, draw_date, source).
 *
 * WHY THIS IS NECESSARY:
 * The original key `uq_user_run_source` only covered (user_id, run_id, source).
 * This meant that when the same saved prediction run was evaluated against a new
 * draw date, the INSERT ... ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE silently overwrote the previous
 * performance record instead of appending a new one - breaking true historical
 * accumulation across multiple draw cycles.
 *
 * Adding `draw_date` to the key ensures each run produces exactly one record per
 * draw date, allowing the panel to show a genuine per-draw history.
 *
 * MIGRATION SAFETY:
 * - Reads INFORMATION_SCHEMA before any ALTER to avoid unnecessary writes.
 * - DROP and ADD are wrapped in separate try/catch blocks so a failure on one
 *   step does not abort the other.
 * - Existing rows are unaffected: with the old key there was at most one row per
 *   (run_id, source), so no (run_id, draw_date, source) duplicates can exist.
 * - Safe to call on every page load; both checks are read-only until a change
 *   is actually needed.
 *
 * @param  object $db  Joomla DB object
 * @return bool  true if migration was a no-op or succeeded, false on hard error
 */
function skaiMigratePerformanceTableKeys($db)
{
    $prefix  = $db->getPrefix();
    $rawName = $prefix . 'skai_learning_performance';

    // -- Check whether the OLD key still exists ----------------------------
    $oldKeyExists = false;
    try {
        $db->setQuery(
            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.STATISTICS
              WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = DATABASE()
                AND TABLE_NAME   = " . $db->quote($rawName) . "
                AND INDEX_NAME   = 'uq_user_run_source'"
        );
        $oldKeyExists = ((int)$db->loadResult() > 0);
    } catch (Exception $e) {
        return false;
    }

    // -- Check whether the NEW key already exists --------------------------
    $newKeyExists = false;
    try {
        $db->setQuery(
            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM INFORMATION_SCHEMA.STATISTICS
              WHERE TABLE_SCHEMA = DATABASE()
                AND TABLE_NAME   = " . $db->quote($rawName) . "
                AND INDEX_NAME   = 'uq_user_run_draw_source'"
        );
        $newKeyExists = ((int)$db->loadResult() > 0);
    } catch (Exception $e) {
        return false;
    }

    // -- Drop the old key if present ---------------------------------------
    if ($oldKeyExists) {
        try {
            $db->setQuery("ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}` DROP INDEX `uq_user_run_source`");
            $db->execute();
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            // Ignore - may already have been removed by a parallel request
        }
    }

    // -- Add the new key if not yet present --------------------------------
    if (!$newKeyExists) {
        try {
            $db->setQuery(
                "ALTER TABLE `{$rawName}`
                  ADD UNIQUE KEY `uq_user_run_draw_source` (`user_id`,`run_id`,`draw_date`,`source`)"
            );
            $db->execute();
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            // Ignore - may already have been added by a parallel request
        }
    }

    return true;
}

/**
 * Load performance history for a user and optional lottery.
 * Returns records ordered by draw_date DESC (most recent first).
 *
 * @param  object $db
 * @param  int    $userId
 * @param  int    $lotteryId  0 = all lotteries
 * @param  int    $limit      Max records
 * @return array
 */
function skaiLoadPerformanceHistory($db, $userId, $lotteryId, $limit)
{
    $userId = (int) $userId;
    if ($userId <= 0) {
        return array();
    }

    $prefix  = $db->getPrefix();
    $tblName = '`' . $prefix . 'skai_learning_performance`';
    $limit   = max(1, min(500, (int)$limit));

    $where = '`user_id` = ' . $userId;
    if ((int)$lotteryId > 0) {
        $where .= ' AND `lottery_id` = ' . (int)$lotteryId;
    }
    $sql = "SELECT * FROM {$tblName} WHERE {$where} ORDER BY `draw_date` DESC, `run_id` DESC LIMIT {$limit}";
    try {
        $db->setQuery($sql);
        $rows = $db->loadAssocList();
        return is_array($rows) ? $rows : array();
    } catch (Exception $e) {
        return array();
    }
}

/**
 * Compute rolling trend analytics from a set of performance records.
 * Records must be sorted most-recent-first.
 *
 * Trend metric: avg_winning_rank (lower = better).
 * Improvement = current 10-run window avg rank is LOWER than prior 10-run window.
 * delta_10vs20 is positive when rank improved (lower number).
 *
 * @param  array $records  Performance records (most recent first)
 * @return array
 */
function skaiComputeTrend(array $records)
{
    // Only use records with a valid avg_winning_rank
    $scored = array();
    foreach ($records as $rec) {
        if (isset($rec['avg_winning_rank']) && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== null && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== '') {
            $scored[] = (float)$rec['avg_winning_rank'];
        }
    }

    $total = count($scored);

    if ($total < 5) {
        $confidence = 'insufficient_data';
    } elseif ($total < 15) {
        $confidence = 'early_trend';
    } elseif ($total < 35) {
        $confidence = 'moderate';
    } else {
        $confidence = 'strong';
    }

    if ($total === 0) {
        return array(
            'last10_avg'   => null,
            'last25_avg'   => null,
            'last50_avg'   => null,
            'lifetime_avg' => null,
            'sample_count' => 0,
            'delta_10vs20' => null,
            'trend_bucket' => 'unknown',
            'confidence'   => 'insufficient_data',
        );
    }

    $avgFn = function (array $slice) {
        if (empty($slice)) { return null; }
        return round(array_sum($slice) / count($slice), 2);
    };

    $last10   = $avgFn(array_slice($scored, 0, 10));
    $last25   = $avgFn(array_slice($scored, 0, 25));
    $last50   = $avgFn(array_slice($scored, 0, 50));
    $lifetime = $avgFn($scored);

    // Compare most recent 10 vs the 10 before that.
    // Positive delta_10vs20 = rank improved (current avg rank is lower = better).
    $delta       = null;
    $trendBucket = 'unknown';
    if ($total >= 10) {
        $currentWindow = $avgFn(array_slice($scored, 0, 10));
        $priorWindow   = $avgFn(array_slice($scored, 10, 10));
        if ($priorWindow !== null && $currentWindow !== null) {
            $delta = round($priorWindow - $currentWindow, 2);
            // 1.5 rank positions = minimum meaningful shift threshold.
            // Smaller differences are treated as 'flat' (within normal variance).
            $trendThreshold = 1.5;
            if ($delta > $trendThreshold) {
                $trendBucket = 'improving';
            } elseif ($delta < -$trendThreshold) {
                $trendBucket = 'declining';
            } else {
                $trendBucket = 'flat';
            }
        }
    }

    return array(
        'last10_avg'   => $last10,
        'last25_avg'   => $last25,
        'last50_avg'   => $last50,
        'lifetime_avg' => $lifetime,
        'sample_count' => $total,
        'delta_10vs20' => $delta,
        'trend_bucket' => $trendBucket,
        'confidence'   => $confidence,
    );
}

/**
 * Derive a user-friendly scorecard status from trend analytics.
 * Status determination logic is fully documented here:
 *
 * - confidence=insufficient_data              => 'Needs More Data'
 * - confidence=early_trend + improving bucket => 'Early Positive Trend'
 * - confidence=early_trend + declining bucket => 'Early Negative Trend'
 * - confidence=moderate/strong + improving    => 'Improving'
 * - confidence=moderate/strong + flat         => 'Stable'
 * - confidence=moderate/strong + declining    => 'Declining'
 * - unknown trend bucket                      => 'Calibrating'
 *
 * @param  array $trend  Result of skaiComputeTrend()
 * @return array { label, class, description }
 */
function skaiDeriveScorecard(array $trend)
{
    $conf   = (string)($trend['confidence']   ?? 'insufficient_data');
    $bucket = (string)($trend['trend_bucket'] ?? 'unknown');

    if ($conf === 'insufficient_data') {
        return array(
            'label'       => 'Needs More Data',
            'class'       => 'skai-lp-status--neutral',
            'description' => 'More validated draw results are needed to measure a reliable trend. Keep saving runs and checking back after each draw.',
        );
    }
    if ($bucket === 'improving') {
        if ($conf === 'early_trend') {
            return array(
                'label'       => 'Early Positive Trend',
                'class'       => 'skai-lp-status--good',
                'description' => 'Early evidence suggests predictions are improving. Continue monitoring as more draws are validated.',
            );
        }
        return array(
            'label'       => 'Improving',
            'class'       => 'skai-lp-status--good',
            'description' => 'Winning numbers are consistently appearing higher in SKAI\'s ranked predictions over recent draws.',
        );
    }
    if ($bucket === 'declining') {
        if ($conf === 'early_trend') {
            return array(
                'label'       => 'Early Negative Trend',
                'class'       => 'skai-lp-status--caution',
                'description' => 'Early data suggests prediction quality may be declining. Review your settings and method selection.',
            );
        }
        return array(
            'label'       => 'Declining',
            'class'       => 'skai-lp-status--bad',
            'description' => 'Average winning rank has increased over recent draws. Consider reviewing SKAI settings or method combinations.',
        );
    }
    if ($bucket === 'flat') {
        return array(
            'label'       => 'Stable',
            'class'       => 'skai-lp-status--neutral',
            'description' => 'Prediction quality is consistent. No significant improvement or decline detected in recent draws.',
        );
    }
    return array(
        'label'       => 'Calibrating',
        'class'       => 'skai-lp-status--neutral',
        'description' => 'Not enough completed draw cycles to calculate a performance trend yet.',
    );
}

/**
 * Determine a module's activity status from a flag count and sample size.
 * Called in the per-group panel to avoid redeclaring an inline function.
 *
 * Returns 'active' if the flag is set in > 50% of sampled runs,
 * 'building' if set in any runs, or 'inactive'.
 *
 * @param  int $count        Number of runs where the flag was set
 * @param  int $sampleCount  Total runs sampled
 * @return string
 */
function skaiLpModStatus($count, $sampleCount)
{
    if ($sampleCount <= 0 || $count <= 0) { return 'inactive'; }
    // 'active' = flag set in a strict majority (> 50%) of sampled runs
    $majorityThreshold = (int)floor($sampleCount / 2) + 1;
    return ($count >= $majorityThreshold) ? 'active' : 'building';
}

/**
 * Grade a single average-rank value into a performance tier.
 *
 * Grading scale (documented for auditability):
 *   1-5   -> Elite    (winning numbers appear in the very top predictions)
 *   6-10  -> Strong   (winning numbers near the top)
 *   11-20 -> Moderate (winning numbers in the middle range)
 *   21+   -> Weak     (winning numbers appear far down the list)
 *   null  -> Unknown
 *
 * @param  float|null $avgRank
 * @return array { grade, label, class }
 */
function skaiLpGrade($avgRank)
{
    if ($avgRank === null || $avgRank === '') {
        return array('grade' => 'unknown', 'label' => 'Unknown', 'class' => 'skai-lp-grade--unknown');
    }
    $r = (float)$avgRank;
    if ($r <= 5)  { return array('grade' => 'elite',    'label' => 'Elite',    'class' => 'skai-lp-grade--elite'); }
    if ($r <= 10) { return array('grade' => 'strong',   'label' => 'Strong',   'class' => 'skai-lp-grade--strong'); }
    if ($r <= 20) { return array('grade' => 'moderate', 'label' => 'Moderate', 'class' => 'skai-lp-grade--moderate'); }
    return             array('grade' => 'weak',     'label' => 'Weak',     'class' => 'skai-lp-grade--weak');
}

/**
 * Calculate performance consistency from an array of avg_rank values.
 *
 * Method: population standard deviation of avg_winning_rank values.
 * Lower standard deviation = more consistent / predictable performance.
 *
 * Classification thresholds (documented):
 *   stddev < 3   -> High Consistency   (runs produce similar results)
 *   stddev < 7   -> Moderate           (some run-to-run variation)
 *   stddev >= 7  -> Volatile           (unpredictable swings)
 *
 * @param  array $records  Performance records (most-recent-first), each with 'avg_winning_rank'
 * @return array { level, label, description, stddev }
 */
function skaiLpConsistency(array $records)
{
    $vals = array();
    foreach ($records as $rec) {
        if (isset($rec['avg_winning_rank']) && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== null && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== '') {
            $vals[] = (float)$rec['avg_winning_rank'];
        }
    }
    $n = count($vals);
    if ($n < 3) {
        return array(
            'level'       => 'unknown',
            'label'       => 'Not enough data',
            'description' => 'At least 3 scored runs are needed to measure consistency.',
            'stddev'      => null,
        );
    }
    $mean   = array_sum($vals) / $n;
    $sumSq  = 0.0;
    foreach ($vals as $v) { $sumSq += ($v - $mean) * ($v - $mean); }
    $stddev = round(sqrt($sumSq / $n), 2);

    // Consistency thresholds (named for auditability / easy tuning):
    //   High: stddev < 3 rank positions  (tight, reliable output)
    //   Moderate: stddev 3-7 rank positions (some run-to-run variation)
    //   Volatile: stddev >= 7 rank positions (unpredictable swings)
    $CONS_HIGH_THRESHOLD     = 3.0;
    $CONS_MODERATE_THRESHOLD = 7.0;

    if ($stddev < $CONS_HIGH_THRESHOLD) {
        return array(
            'level'       => 'high',
            'label'       => 'High Consistency',
            'description' => 'Results are reliably similar across runs. SKAI performs predictably.',
            'stddev'      => $stddev,
        );
    }
    if ($stddev < $CONS_MODERATE_THRESHOLD) {
        return array(
            'level'       => 'moderate',
            'label'       => 'Moderate Consistency',
            'description' => 'Some variation between runs, with occasional stronger or weaker results.',
            'stddev'      => $stddev,
        );
    }
    return array(
        'level'       => 'volatile',
