        'label'       => 'Volatile',
        'description' => 'Performance varies significantly between runs. Results are unpredictable.',
        'stddev'      => $stddev,
    );
}

/**
 * Produce enriched trend intelligence: direction + strength labels.
 *
 * Direction: improving / declining / flat / unknown
 * Strength classification based on absolute delta (documented):
 *   |delta| < 1.5  -> no meaningful change (flat)
 *   |delta| 1.5-4  -> Slight
 *   |delta| 4-8    -> Moderate
 *   |delta| >= 8   -> Strong
 *
 * @param  float|null $delta  Positive = improving (rank decreased), negative = declining
 * @return array { direction, strength, label, arrow }
 */
function skaiLpTrendIntelligence($delta)
{
    if ($delta === null) {
        return array(
            'direction' => 'unknown',
            'strength'  => '',
            'label'     => 'Not enough data for a trend',
            'arrow'     => '&#8212;',
        );
    }
    $abs = abs((float)$delta);

    // Trend thresholds (named for auditability / easy tuning):
    //   Flat:     |delta| < 1.5  (within normal variance; no meaningful change)
    //   Slight:   |delta| 1.5-4  (noticeable but modest shift)
    //   Moderate: |delta| 4-8    (clear improvement or decline)
    //   Strong:   |delta| >= 8   (large rank shift across periods)
    $TREND_FLAT_THRESHOLD     = 1.5;
    $TREND_SLIGHT_THRESHOLD   = 4.0;
    $TREND_MODERATE_THRESHOLD = 8.0;

    if ($abs < $TREND_FLAT_THRESHOLD) {
        return array(
            'direction' => 'flat',
            'strength'  => 'minimal',
            'label'     => 'No significant change',
            'arrow'     => '&#8594;',
        );
    }

    // Strength tiers
    if ($abs < $TREND_SLIGHT_THRESHOLD)   { $strength = 'Slight'; }
    elseif ($abs < $TREND_MODERATE_THRESHOLD) { $strength = 'Moderate'; }
    else                                  { $strength = 'Strong'; }

    if ((float)$delta > 0) {
        return array(
            'direction' => 'improving',
            'strength'  => $strength,
            'label'     => $strength . ' Improvement',
            'arrow'     => '&#8593;',
        );
    }
    return array(
        'direction' => 'declining',
        'strength'  => $strength,
        'label'     => $strength . ' Decline',
        'arrow'     => '&#8595;',
    );
}

/**
 * Extract best-run opportunity metrics from the history records.
 * These metrics show the system's CEILING performance, not its average.
 *
 * @param  array $records  Performance records
 * @return array { best_avg_rank, best_single_rank, max_top10_hits, max_top20_hits,
 *                 best_weighted_score, best_run_date }
 */
function skaiLpBestRunStats(array $records)
{
    $bestAvgRank    = null;
    $bestSingleRank = null;
    $maxTop10       = 0;
    $maxTop20       = 0;
    $bestWScore     = null;
    $bestRunDate    = '';

    foreach ($records as $rec) {
        $avg = (isset($rec['avg_winning_rank']) && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== null && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== '')
            ? (float)$rec['avg_winning_rank'] : null;
        $best = (isset($rec['best_winning_rank']) && $rec['best_winning_rank'] !== null)
            ? (int)$rec['best_winning_rank'] : null;
        $t10  = (int)($rec['top10_hits'] ?? 0);
        $t20  = (int)($rec['top20_hits'] ?? 0);
        $ws   = (isset($rec['weighted_quality_score']) && $rec['weighted_quality_score'] !== null && $rec['weighted_quality_score'] !== '')
            ? (float)$rec['weighted_quality_score'] : null;

        // Best (lowest) average rank
        if ($avg !== null && ($bestAvgRank === null || $avg < $bestAvgRank)) {
            $bestAvgRank = $avg;
            $bestRunDate = (string)($rec['draw_date'] ?? '');
        }
        // Best (lowest) single number rank
        if ($best !== null && ($bestSingleRank === null || $best < $bestSingleRank)) {
            $bestSingleRank = $best;
        }
        // Best top-N hit counts
        if ($t10 > $maxTop10) { $maxTop10 = $t10; }
        if ($t20 > $maxTop20) { $maxTop20 = $t20; }
        // Best weighted score (higher = better)
        if ($ws !== null && ($bestWScore === null || $ws > $bestWScore)) {
            $bestWScore = $ws;
        }
    }

    return array(
        'best_avg_rank'    => ($bestAvgRank    !== null) ? round($bestAvgRank, 1) : null,
        'best_single_rank' => $bestSingleRank,
        'max_top10_hits'   => $maxTop10,
        'max_top20_hits'   => $maxTop20,
        'best_weighted'    => ($bestWScore !== null) ? round($bestWScore, 3) : null,
        'best_run_date'    => $bestRunDate,
    );
}

// ==========================================================================
// DUAL BEST-RUN MODEL - Scoring & Selection
// Separates two distinct concepts:
//   A. Best ranking setup example  - strongest ranking quality (lowest avg rank, etc.)
//   B. Best Hit Run     - strongest hit-oriented outcome (highest Top-20, etc.)
//   C. Recommended run  - composite recommendation under configurable strategy
// ==========================================================================

// Sentinel value for missing/null rank values.
// Treated as worst case (very high rank position) during scoring.
if (!defined('SKAI_LP_NULL_RANK_SENTINEL')) {
    define('SKAI_LP_NULL_RANK_SENTINEL', 9999.0);
}

/**
 * Safe [0..1] normalization helper.
 * When max == min (all values are equal), returns 1.0 so every record
 * is treated as "best possible" rather than being penalised.
 * If max < min (inverted range - should not happen in practice), also
 * returns 1.0 defensively rather than producing a negative result.
 * Clamps val to the [min..max] range before normalizing.
 *
 * @param  float $val
 * @param  float $min
 * @param  float $max
 * @return float  normalized value in [0..1]
 */
function skaiLpNormalize($val, $min, $max)
{
    // Guard: zero or inverted range -> treat as "all equal / best"
    if ((float)$max - (float)$min < 1.0e-10) { return 1.0; }
    $v = max((float)$min, min((float)$max, (float)$val));
    return ($v - (float)$min) / ((float)$max - (float)$min);
}

/**
 * Compute per-record composite scores for all records in the history array.
 *
 * Scoring formulas (all weights documented and sum to 1.00):
 *
 * SYSTEM QUALITY SCORE - measures ranking intelligence:
 *   sys = (norm_avg_rank_inv x 0.45)   // lower avg rank -> better
 *       + (norm_weighted    x 0.30)   // higher weighted score -> better
 *       + (norm_best_rank_inv x 0.15) // lower best rank -> better
 *       + (norm_missing_inv x 0.10)   // fewer missing -> better
 *
 * HIT OPPORTUNITY SCORE - measures playable hit-range outcome:
 *   hit = (norm_top20       x 0.45)   // more Top-20 hits -> better
 *       + (norm_top10       x 0.30)   // more Top-10 hits -> better
 *       + (norm_missing_inv x 0.15)   // fewer missing -> better
 *       + (norm_avg_rank_inv x 0.10)  // lower avg rank -> secondary tie-break
 *
 * BALANCED RECOMMENDATION SCORE:
 *   balanced = (sys x 0.60) + (hit x 0.40)
 *
 * "Inv" normalization: for "lower is better" metrics, normalize the
 * INVERTED distance from the maximum:
 *   norm_inv = (max - val) / (max - min)
 * This maps min_val -> 1.0 (best) and max_val -> 0.0 (worst).
 *
 * Null / missing values are treated as worst case:
 *   avg_rank and best_rank -> sentinel 9999 (very high = worst)
 *   weighted_quality_score -> 0.0 (no quality)
 *
 * Ties are resolved by the highest composite score; if scores are equal,
 * the first occurring record (most recent, since history is newest-first) wins.
 *
 * @param  array $records  Performance records (most-recent-first)
 * @return array  One entry per record: { sys, hit, balanced }
 */
function skaiLpComputeRunScores(array $records)
{
    if (empty($records)) { return array(); }

    $NULL_RANK = SKAI_LP_NULL_RANK_SENTINEL;  // Sentinel for missing rank values (see constant above)

    $avgRanks  = array();
    $wScores   = array();
    $bestRanks = array();
    $missings  = array();
    $top10s    = array();
    $top20s    = array();

    foreach ($records as $rec) {
        $avgRanks[]  = (isset($rec['avg_winning_rank']) && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== null && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== '')
            ? (float)$rec['avg_winning_rank'] : $NULL_RANK;
        $wScores[]   = (isset($rec['weighted_quality_score']) && $rec['weighted_quality_score'] !== null && $rec['weighted_quality_score'] !== '')
            ? (float)$rec['weighted_quality_score'] : 0.0;
        $bestRanks[] = (isset($rec['best_winning_rank']) && $rec['best_winning_rank'] !== null)
            ? (float)$rec['best_winning_rank'] : $NULL_RANK;
        $missings[]  = (int)($rec['missing_hits_count'] ?? 0);
        $top10s[]    = (int)($rec['top10_hits'] ?? 0);
        $top20s[]    = (int)($rec['top20_hits'] ?? 0);
    }

    // Pre-compute range boundaries for normalization
    $minAvg  = min($avgRanks);   $maxAvg  = max($avgRanks);
    $minWs   = min($wScores);    $maxWs   = max($wScores);
    $minBest = min($bestRanks);  $maxBest = max($bestRanks);
    $minMis  = min($missings);   $maxMis  = max($missings);
    $minT10  = min($top10s);     $maxT10  = max($top10s);
    $minT20  = min($top20s);     $maxT20  = max($top20s);

    $scores = array();
    $n = count($records);
    for ($i = 0; $i < $n; $i++) {
        // "Lower is better" -> normalize the inverted distance from max
        $normAvgInv  = skaiLpNormalize($maxAvg  - $avgRanks[$i],  0.0, $maxAvg  - $minAvg);
        $normBestInv = skaiLpNormalize($maxBest - $bestRanks[$i], 0.0, $maxBest - $minBest);
        $normMisInv  = skaiLpNormalize($maxMis  - $missings[$i],  0.0, $maxMis  - $minMis);
        // "Higher is better" -> standard normalization
        $normWs  = skaiLpNormalize($wScores[$i], $minWs,  $maxWs);
        $normT10 = skaiLpNormalize($top10s[$i],  $minT10, $maxT10);
        $normT20 = skaiLpNormalize($top20s[$i],  $minT20, $maxT20);

        // System Quality Score (weights total 1.00)
        $sys = ($normAvgInv  * 0.45)
             + ($normWs      * 0.30)
             + ($normBestInv * 0.15)
             + ($normMisInv  * 0.10);

        // Hit Opportunity Score (weights total 1.00)
        $hit = ($normT20    * 0.45)
             + ($normT10    * 0.30)
             + ($normMisInv * 0.15)
             + ($normAvgInv * 0.10);

        // Balanced Recommendation Score
        $balanced = ($sys * 0.60) + ($hit * 0.40);

        $scores[] = array(
            'sys'      => round($sys,      4),
            'hit'      => round($hit,      4),
            'balanced' => round($balanced, 4),
        );
    }

    return $scores;
}

/**
 * Internal helper: extract a clean display record from history + scores at index $idx.
 *
 * @param  array $records  Full history
 * @param  int   $idx      Record index
 * @return array
 */
/**
 * Build a compact, user-facing run-setting label from AI share used percent and
 * strategy family name.
 *
 * Examples:  "55% * Balanced Mix"   "72% * AI-Forward"   "28% * Skip Pattern Boost"
 *            "55%"  (family unknown)  "Balanced Mix"  (pct unknown)
 *            ""     (both unknown - legacy row)
 *
 * NOTE: AI percent is rounded to the nearest integer for display.
 * The strategy family thresholds (AI<=40, AI 41-64, AI>=65) are defined at whole
 * numbers, so sub-integer precision has no user-visible meaning.  Displaying
 * "55%" is always more readable than "55.4%" in a KPI label.
 *
 * @param  float|null  $aiPct       AI share used percent (0-100), or null if unknown
 * @param  string      $stratFamily Strategy family label, or '' if unknown
 * @return string
 */
function skaiLpFormatRunSettingLabel($aiPct, $stratFamily)
{
    $stratFamily = (string)$stratFamily;
    if ($aiPct !== null && $stratFamily !== '') {
        return (string)(int)round((float)$aiPct) . '% - ' . $stratFamily;
    }
    if ($aiPct !== null) {
        return (string)(int)round((float)$aiPct) . '%';
    }
    if ($stratFamily !== '') {
        return $stratFamily;
    }
    return '';
}

function skaiLpFormatTrainingStyleLabel($value)
{
    $value = trim((string)$value);
    if ($value === '') {
        return '';
    }
    $value = str_replace(array('_','-'), ' ', $value);
    return ucwords($value);
}


function skaiLpExtractRunRecord(array $records, $idx)
{
    $rec = $records[(int)$idx];
    $ts  = strtotime((string)($rec['draw_date'] ?? ''));

    // Decode run configuration persisted in notes_json.
    // Fields added when run_ai_pct / run_strategy_family were persisted at scoring time.
    // Graceful fallback for legacy rows that contain only [] or null.
    $notesArr = array();
    if (!empty($rec['notes_json'])) {
        $notesDecoded = json_decode((string)$rec['notes_json'], true);
        if (is_array($notesDecoded)) {
            $notesArr = $notesDecoded;
        }
    }
    $runAiPct       = (isset($notesArr['run_ai_pct']) && $notesArr['run_ai_pct'] !== null && $notesArr['run_ai_pct'] !== '')
                        ? round((float)$notesArr['run_ai_pct'], 1) : null;
    $runStratFamily = (isset($notesArr['run_strategy_family']) && (string)$notesArr['run_strategy_family'] !== '')
                        ? (string)$notesArr['run_strategy_family'] : '';

    // Build compact user-facing setting label via shared helper (avoids duplication)
    $runSettingLabel = skaiLpFormatRunSettingLabel($runAiPct, $runStratFamily);

    return array(
        'idx'                 => (int)$idx,
        'run_id'              => (int)($rec['run_id'] ?? 0),
        'label'               => $ts ? date('M j, Y', $ts) : (string)($rec['draw_date'] ?? ''),
        'avg_rank'            => (isset($rec['avg_winning_rank']) && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== null && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== '')
                                   ? round((float)$rec['avg_winning_rank'], 1) : null,
        'best_rank'           => ($rec['best_winning_rank'] !== null) ? (int)$rec['best_winning_rank'] : null,
        'weighted'            => (isset($rec['weighted_quality_score']) && $rec['weighted_quality_score'] !== null && $rec['weighted_quality_score'] !== '')
                                   ? round((float)$rec['weighted_quality_score'], 3) : null,
        'missing'             => (int)($rec['missing_hits_count'] ?? 0),
        'top10'               => (int)($rec['top10_hits'] ?? 0),
        'top20'               => (int)($rec['top20_hits'] ?? 0),
        // Run configuration fields (from notes_json, empty for legacy rows)
        'run_ai_pct'          => $runAiPct,
        'run_strategy_family' => $runStratFamily,
        'run_setting_label'   => $runSettingLabel,
    );
}

/**
 * Select the run with the strongest ranking quality (Best ranking setup example).
 *
 * Selection priority (via composite sys score):
 *   1. Lowest avg winning rank (weight 0.45)
 *   2. Highest weighted quality score (weight 0.30)
 *   3. Lowest best rank (weight 0.15)
 *   4. Lowest missing count (weight 0.10)
 * Ties: first record (most recent) wins.
 *
 * @param  array $records  Performance records
 * @return array|null  Run record + score, or null if no records
 */
function skaiLpSelectBestSystemRun(array $records)
{
    if (empty($records)) { return null; }

    $scores   = skaiLpComputeRunScores($records);
    $bestIdx  = 0;
    $bestScore = -1.0;
    foreach ($scores as $i => $s) {
        if ($s['sys'] > $bestScore) { $bestScore = $s['sys']; $bestIdx = $i; }
    }

    $result        = skaiLpExtractRunRecord($records, $bestIdx);
    $result['score'] = $bestScore;
    return $result;
}

/**
 * Select the run with the strongest hit-oriented outcome (Best Hit Run).
 *
 * Selection priority (via composite hit score):
 *   1. Highest Top-20 hits (weight 0.45)
 *   2. Highest Top-10 hits (weight 0.30)
 *   3. Lowest missing count (weight 0.15)
 *   4. Lowest avg winning rank (weight 0.10 - secondary tie-break)
 * Ties: first record (most recent) wins.
 *
 * @param  array $records  Performance records
 * @return array|null  Run record + score, or null if no records
 */
function skaiLpSelectBestHitRun(array $records)
{
    if (empty($records)) { return null; }

    $scores   = skaiLpComputeRunScores($records);
    $bestIdx  = 0;
    $bestScore = -1.0;
    foreach ($scores as $i => $s) {
        if ($s['hit'] > $bestScore) { $bestScore = $s['hit']; $bestIdx = $i; }
    }

    $result        = skaiLpExtractRunRecord($records, $bestIdx);
    $result['score'] = $bestScore;
    return $result;
}

/**
 * Select the recommended run for a given strategy.
 *
 * Supported modes:
 *   'balanced'      - 60% system quality + 40% hit opportunity (default)
 *   'hit_priority'  - pure hit opportunity score
 *   'rank_priority' - pure system quality score
 *
 * @param  array  $records  Performance records
 * @param  string $mode     Strategy mode (see above)
 * @return array|null  Run record + strategy metadata, or null if no records
 */
function skaiLpSelectRecommendedRun(array $records, $mode)
{
    if (empty($records)) { return null; }

    // Strategy -> score key + human labels
    $strategyMap = array(
        'balanced'      => array(
            'key'    => 'balanced',
            'label'  => 'Balanced Strategy',
            'reason' => 'This setting produced the strongest combined ranking quality and hit coverage in recent scored runs.',
        ),
        'hit_priority'  => array(
            'key'    => 'hit',
            'label'  => 'Hit Priority Strategy',
            'reason' => 'Maximizes hit-range outcomes - prioritizes Top-20 and Top-10 coverage.',
        ),
        'rank_priority' => array(
            'key'    => 'sys',
            'label'  => 'Rank Priority Strategy',
            'reason' => 'Focuses on overall ranking quality by prioritizing average rank and weighted score.',
        ),
    );
    $strategy  = $strategyMap[$mode] ?? $strategyMap['balanced'];
    $scoreKey  = $strategy['key'];

    $scores   = skaiLpComputeRunScores($records);
    $bestIdx  = 0;
    $bestScore = -1.0;
    foreach ($scores as $i => $s) {
        if ($s[$scoreKey] > $bestScore) { $bestScore = $s[$scoreKey]; $bestIdx = $i; }
    }

    $result                  = skaiLpExtractRunRecord($records, $bestIdx);
    $result['score']         = $bestScore;
    $result['mode']          = $mode;
    $result['strategy_label']= $strategy['label'];
    $result['reason']        = $strategy['reason'];
    return $result;
}

/**
 * Generate the "Why these results differ" explanation text for the dual-model panel.
 * Text is determined by whether the best system run and best hit run are the same record.
 *
 * @param  array|null $bestSys      Result of skaiLpSelectBestSystemRun()
 * @param  array|null $bestHit      Result of skaiLpSelectBestHitRun()
 * @param  int        $sampleCount  Total scored runs (for early-stage caveat)
 * @return string  HTML-safe plain-text explanation
 */
function skaiLpDualRunInsight($bestSys, $bestHit, $sampleCount)
{
    if ($bestSys === null || $bestHit === null) { return ''; }

    if ((int)$bestSys['idx'] === (int)$bestHit['idx']) {
        $text = 'The same run delivered both the best ranking quality and the strongest hit performance, '
              . 'indicating unusually strong alignment between system quality and playable outcome.';
    } else {
        $text = 'The strongest ranking-quality run differed from the strongest hit-oriented run. '
              . 'This shows that SKAI can rank winning numbers well overall while a different run '
              . 'may produce better short-range hit concentration - both results are valid and useful '
              . 'depending on what you are evaluating.';
    }

    if ((int)$sampleCount < 10) {
        $text .= ' Note: the current sample is still very early - these patterns will become more '
               . 'reliable as additional scored runs accumulate.';
    }

    return $text;
}

/**
 * Select the worst-performing run (highest average winning rank).
 * Consistent with the pattern used by skaiLpSelectBestSystemRun() and
 * skaiLpSelectBestHitRun() - avoids duplicating the null-safe loop inline.
 *
 * @param  array $records  Performance records
 * @return int|null  Array index of the worst run, or null if no scored records
 */
function skaiLpSelectWorstRun(array $records)
{
    $worstIdx = null;
    $worstVal = null;
    foreach ($records as $i => $rec) {
        $avg = (isset($rec['avg_winning_rank']) && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== null && $rec['avg_winning_rank'] !== '')
            ? (float)$rec['avg_winning_rank'] : null;
        if ($avg === null) { continue; }
        if ($worstVal === null || $avg > $worstVal) { $worstVal = $avg; $worstIdx = $i; }
    }
    return $worstIdx;
}

/**
 * Return a tiered confidence label with run-count context.
 *
 * Thresholds (documented):
 *   < 10 runs  -> Very Early Stage
 *   10-24      -> Early Stage
 *   25-49      -> Moderate Confidence
 *   50+        -> Strong Confidence
 *
 * @param  int $sampleCount
 * @return array { level, label, description }
 */
function skaiLpConfidenceLabel($sampleCount)
{
    $n = (int)$sampleCount;
    if ($n < 10) {
        return array(
            'level'       => 'very_early',
            'label'       => 'Very Early Stage',
            'description' => 'Results are based on fewer than 10 validated runs. Treat patterns as hints only.',
        );
    }
    if ($n < 25) {
        return array(
            'level'       => 'early',
            'label'       => 'Early Stage',
            'description' => 'Some patterns are emerging but the sample is still small. Observe a few more draw cycles before acting on trends.',
        );
    }
    if ($n < 50) {
        return array(
            'level'       => 'moderate',
            'label'       => 'Moderate Confidence',
            'description' => 'A meaningful sample is available. Trend direction and grade are likely reliable.',
        );
    }
    return array(
        'level'       => 'strong',
        'label'       => 'Strong Confidence',
        'description' => 'Large sample size. Performance metrics are statistically robust.',
    );
}

/**
 * Return an improved human-readable module status label and description.
 * Replaces "Not Detected" with context-appropriate language.
 *
 * @param  string $status  'active' | 'building' | 'inactive'
 * @return array { badge_class, badge_text, note }
 */
function skaiLpModStatusLabel($status)
{
    if ($status === 'active') {
        return array(
            'badge_class' => 'skai-lp-mod-badge--active',
            'badge_text'  => 'Active',
            'note'        => 'Detected in recent scored runs',
        );
    }
    if ($status === 'building') {
        return array(
            'badge_class' => 'skai-lp-mod-badge--building',
            'badge_text'  => 'Building',
            'note'        => 'Seen in some recent scored runs',
        );
    }
    return array(
        'badge_class' => 'skai-lp-mod-badge--inactive',
        'badge_text'  => 'Not recently detected',
        'note'        => 'Not detected in recent scored runs',
    );
}

/**
 * Hybrid module status for the latest accumulated draw context.
 * It combines:
 * 1) whether the latest draw context is using the engine now
 * 2) whether scored history supports that engine
 */
function skaiLpCurrentHybridStatus($activeNow, $historyCount, $sampleCount)
{
    $activeNow = ((int)$activeNow > 0);
    $historyCount = (int)$historyCount;
    $sampleCount = (int)$sampleCount;

    if ($activeNow) {
        if ($historyCount <= 0 || $sampleCount <= 0) {
            return array(
                'badge_class' => 'skai-lp-mod-badge--building',
                'badge_text'  => 'Active now',
                'note'        => 'Used in the latest draw context, but history is still early',
            );
        }
        $historyStatus = skaiLpModStatus($historyCount, $sampleCount);
        if ($historyStatus === 'active') {
            return array(
                'badge_class' => 'skai-lp-mod-badge--active',
                'badge_text'  => 'Active now',
                'note'        => 'Used in the latest draw context and supported by past results',
            );
        }
        return array(
            'badge_class' => 'skai-lp-mod-badge--building',
            'badge_text'  => 'Active now',
            'note'        => 'Used in the latest draw context and still building history',
        );
    }

    if ($historyCount > 0 && $sampleCount > 0) {
        $historyStatus = skaiLpModStatus($historyCount, $sampleCount);
        if ($historyStatus === 'active') {
            return array(
                'badge_class' => 'skai-lp-mod-badge--building',
                'badge_text'  => 'Used before',
                'note'        => 'Supported by past results, but not active in the latest draw context',
            );
        }
        return array(
            'badge_class' => 'skai-lp-mod-badge--inactive',
            'badge_text'  => 'Used before',
            'note'        => 'Seen in past results, but not active in the latest draw context',
        );
    }

    return array(
        'badge_class' => 'skai-lp-mod-badge--inactive',
        'badge_text'  => 'Not used now',
        'note'        => 'Not detected in the latest draw context or recent scored history',
    );
}

/**
 * Generate a dynamic "What this means" interpretation paragraph.
 * Combines grade, trend intelligence, and consistency into a single
 * plain-language insight for the user.
 *
 * DO NOT fake metrics - all conditions are based on real computed values.
 *
 * @param  array  $grade       Result of skaiLpGrade()
 * @param  array  $trend       Result of skaiLpTrendIntelligence()
 * @param  array  $consistency Result of skaiLpConsistency()
 * @param  array  $confidence  Result of skaiLpConfidenceLabel()
 * @return string  HTML-safe plain text paragraph
 */
function skaiLpInsight(array $grade, array $trend, array $consistency, array $confidence)
{
    // -- Grade phrase ----------------------------------------------
    $gradeMap = array(
        'elite'    => 'performing at an elite level',
        'strong'   => 'performing strongly',
        'moderate' => 'performing at a moderate level',
        'weak'     => 'producing weaker results than expected',
        'unknown'  => 'not yet rated',
    );
    $gradePhrase = $gradeMap[$grade['grade']] ?? 'performing at an unclassified level';

    // -- Trend phrase ----------------------------------------------
    $trendDir = $trend['direction'];
    if ($trendDir === 'improving') {
        $trendPhrase = 'with a ' . strtolower((string)$trend['strength']) . ' recent improvement in prediction quality';
    } elseif ($trendDir === 'declining') {
        $trendPhrase = 'but showing a ' . strtolower((string)$trend['strength']) . ' decline in recent runs';
    } elseif ($trendDir === 'flat') {
        $trendPhrase = 'with no significant recent change in quality';
    } else {
        $trendPhrase = 'with insufficient trend data';
    }

    // -- Consistency phrase ----------------------------------------
    $consMap = array(
        'high'     => 'Results are reliably consistent across runs.',
        'moderate' => 'Performance varies moderately between runs.',
        'volatile' => 'Results vary significantly between runs - some runs perform much better or worse than average.',
        'unknown'  => '',
    );
    $consPhrase = $consMap[$consistency['level']] ?? '';

    // -- Confidence caveat -----------------------------------------
    $confCaveat = '';
    if (in_array($confidence['level'], array('very_early', 'early'), true)) {
        $confCaveat = ' Note: the sample size is still small, so these trends may shift with more draws.';
    }

    $sentence = 'The system is currently ' . $gradePhrase . ', ' . $trendPhrase . '. '
              . ($consPhrase !== '' ? $consPhrase . ' ' : '')
              . $confCaveat;

    return trim($sentence);
}

        'SKAI Learning performance: unique key migration failed - check database permissions.',
        \Joomla\CMS\Log\Log::WARNING,
        'skai.learning'
    );
}

// --------------------------------------------------
// Numbers to Play payload endpoint for Wheel Builder import
// --------------------------------------------------
$__mleAction = strtolower(trim($app->input->getString('mle_action', '')));
if ($__mleAction === 'play_set_payload') {
    $app->setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json; charset=utf-8', true);
    $app->setHeader('Cache-Control', 'no-store, no-cache, must-revalidate, max-age=0', true);
    $app->setHeader('Pragma', 'no-cache', true);

    $playSetId = $app->input->getInt('play_set_id', 0);
    if ($playSetId <= 0) {
        echo json_encode(array('ok' => false, 'error' => 'Missing play_set_id.'));
        exit;
    }

    $snCols = array();
    try {
        $snColsRaw = $db->getTableColumns('#__user_saved_numbers', false);
        $snCols = is_array($snColsRaw) ? array_keys($snColsRaw) : array();
    } catch (\Throwable $e) {
        $snCols = array();
    }

    $q = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select('*')
        ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . (int)$playSetId)
        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int)$workspaceUserId);
    if (in_array('save_intent', $snCols, true)) {
        $q->where(
            '(' .
            $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " IN ('play_set','custom_play','wheel_candidate')" .
            ' OR (' . $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = '' AND " . $db->quoteName('source') . " = 'strategy_set')" .
            ')'
        );
    } else {
        $q->where($db->quoteName('source') . " = 'strategy_set'");
    }
    $db->setQuery($q, 0, 1);
    $row = $db->loadAssoc();

    if (empty($row)) {
        echo json_encode(array('ok' => false, 'error' => 'Play set not found.'));
        exit;
    }

    $meta = mylottoexpertResolvePlayIntentMeta($row);
    $main = mylottoexpertParseNumberCsv($row['main_numbers'] ?? '', true);
    $extra = mylottoexpertParseNumberCsv($row['extra_ball_numbers'] ?? '', true);
    if (empty($main)) {
        echo json_encode(array('ok' => false, 'error' => 'Play set has no main numbers.'));
        exit;
    }

    $payload = array(
        'play_set_id'             => (int)($row['id'] ?? 0),
        'lottery_id'              => (int)($row['lottery_id'] ?? 0),
        'target_game_id'          => trim((string)($row['target_game_id'] ?? '')),
        'target_prediction_type'  => trim((string)($row['target_prediction_type'] ?? '')),
        'target_pick_size'        => (int)($row['target_pick_size'] ?? count($main)),
        'target_extra_count'      => (int)($row['target_extra_count'] ?? count($extra)),
        'main_numbers'            => $main,
        'extra_ball_numbers'      => $extra,
        'label'                   => trim((string)($row['label'] ?? '')),
        'origin_source'           => $meta['origin_source'],
        'save_intent'             => $meta['save_intent'],
        'play_status'             => $meta['play_status']
    );

    echo json_encode(array('ok' => true, 'payload' => $payload), JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE | JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES);
    exit;
}

// --------------------------------------------------
// Numbers to Play list endpoint for Wheel Builder picker
// --------------------------------------------------
if ($__mleAction === 'play_sets_list') {
    $app->setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json; charset=utf-8', true);
    $app->setHeader('Cache-Control', 'no-store, no-cache, must-revalidate, max-age=0', true);
    $app->setHeader('Pragma', 'no-cache', true);

    $snCols2 = array();
    try {
        $snColsRaw2 = $db->getTableColumns('#__user_saved_numbers', false);
        $snCols2 = is_array($snColsRaw2) ? array_keys($snColsRaw2) : array();
    } catch (\Throwable $e) {
        $snCols2 = array();
    }

    $q = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select(array(
            $db->quoteName('id'),
            $db->quoteName('label'),
            $db->quoteName('lottery_id'),
            $db->quoteName('main_numbers'),
            $db->quoteName('extra_ball_numbers'),
            $db->quoteName('date_saved'),
            $db->quoteName('source')
        ))
        ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . (int)$workspaceUserId);

    if (in_array('origin_source', $snCols2, true)) {
        $q->select($db->quoteName('origin_source'));
    }
    if (in_array('play_status', $snCols2, true)) {
        $q->select($db->quoteName('play_status'));
        $q->where($db->quoteName('play_status') . " <> 'archived'");
    }
    if (in_array('save_intent', $snCols2, true)) {
        $q->where(
            '(' .
            $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " IN ('play_set','custom_play','wheel_candidate')" .
            ' OR (' . $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = '' AND " . $db->quoteName('source') . " = 'strategy_set')" .
            ')'
        );
    } else {
        $q->where($db->quoteName('source') . " = 'strategy_set'");
    }
    $q->order($db->quoteName('id') . ' DESC');
    $db->setQuery($q, 0, 50);
    $listRows = $db->loadAssocList() ?: array();

    $listSets = array();
    foreach ($listRows as $lRow) {
        $lMain = mylottoexpertParseNumberCsv($lRow['main_numbers'] ?? '', true);
        if (empty($lMain)) { continue; }
        $lLabel = trim((string)($lRow['label'] ?? ''));
        $lOrigin = strtolower(trim((string)($lRow['origin_source'] ?? $lRow['source'] ?? '')));
        if (in_array($lOrigin, array('skai_prediction', 'prediction', 'ai_prediction'), true)) {
            $lBadge = 'From Prediction';
        } elseif (in_array($lOrigin, array('strategy_builder', 'strategy_set'), true) || ($lRow['source'] ?? '') === 'strategy_set') {
            $lBadge = 'From Strategy Builder';
        } elseif (in_array($lOrigin, array('manual', 'custom'), true)) {
            $lBadge = 'Custom Selection';
        } else {
            $lBadge = 'Saved Set';
        }
        $lSavedTs = strtotime((string)($lRow['date_saved'] ?? ''));
        $lSavedLabel = $lSavedTs ? date('M j, Y', $lSavedTs) : trim((string)($lRow['date_saved'] ?? ''));
        $listSets[] = array(
            'id'                 => (int)$lRow['id'],
            'label'              => $lLabel !== '' ? $lLabel : ('Play Set #' . (int)$lRow['id']),
            'main_numbers'       => $lMain,
            'extra_ball_numbers' => mylottoexpertParseNumberCsv($lRow['extra_ball_numbers'] ?? '', true),
            'source_badge'       => $lBadge,
            'date_saved'         => $lSavedLabel,
        );
    }
    echo json_encode(array('ok' => true, 'sets' => $listSets), JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE | JSON_UNESCAPED_SLASHES);
    exit;
}

// New Features toggle (persisted in #__user_profiles)

    ? (mylottoexpertGetUserPref($db, $workspaceUserId, 'showNewFeatures', '1') === '1')
    : true;
// Allow POST toggle via form
if (!MLE_DEMO_MODE && $app->input->getMethod() === 'POST' && $app->input->post->get('toggle_new_features', '', 'STRING') !== '') {    if (!\Joomla\CMS\Session\Session::checkToken('post')) {
        $app->enqueueMessage('Your session has expired. Please refresh and try again.', 'error');
        $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        exit;
    }
    $newVal = $app->input->post->get('new_features_enabled', '0', 'STRING') === '1' ? '1' : '0';
    mylottoexpertSetUserPref($db, $workspaceUserId, 'showNewFeatures', $newVal);
    $showNewFeatures = ($newVal === '1');
}

// --------------------------------------------------
$predSortPref = ($workspaceUserId > 0)
    ? mylottoexpertGetUserPref($db, $workspaceUserId, 'predSort', 'desc')
    : 'desc'; // 'desc' = newest-to-oldest (default)
$predSortDir  = (strtolower($predSortPref) === 'asc') ? 'ASC' : 'DESC';

if (!MLE_DEMO_MODE && $app->input->getMethod() === 'POST' && $app->input->post->get('change_sort_dir', '', 'STRING') !== '') {    if (!\Joomla\CMS\Session\Session::checkToken('post')) {
        $app->enqueueMessage('Your session has expired. Please refresh and try again.', 'error');
        $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        exit;
    }
    $dir = strtolower($app->input->post->get('pred_sort_dir', 'desc', 'STRING'));
    $dir = ($dir === 'asc') ? 'asc' : 'desc';
    mylottoexpertSetUserPref($db, $workspaceUserId, 'predSort', $dir);
    $predSortDir = ($dir === 'asc') ? 'ASC' : 'DESC';
}

// --------------------------------------------------
// Handle Prediction Deletion / Template Actions
// IMPORTANT: Only enforce CSRF when THIS page's actions are triggered.
// This avoids breaking unrelated module POSTs that may target this URL.
// --------------------------------------------------

if (!MLE_DEMO_MODE && $app->input->getMethod() === 'POST') {
    // Detect whether this POST is intended for mylottoexpert actions
    $hasDashboardAction =
        ($app->input->post->getInt('delete_set', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->get('delete_set_selected', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->get('delete_all_predictions', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->get('delete_lottery_predictions', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('save_prediction_as_play', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('duplicate_play_entry', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('update_play_entry', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('archive_play_entry', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('delete_play_entry', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('send_play_to_wheel', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('delete_setting_template', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->get('save_setting_template', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('update_setting_note', 0) > 0) ||
        ($app->input->post->get('toggle_new_features', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->get('change_sort_dir', '', 'STRING') !== '') ||
        ($app->input->post->getInt('save_strategy_set', 0) > 0);

    if ($hasDashboardAction && !\Joomla\CMS\Session\Session::checkToken('post')) {
        $app->enqueueMessage('Your session expired. Please refresh and try again.', 'error');
        $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        exit;
    }

    $__actionSnCols = array();
    try {
        $__actionSnColsRaw = $db->getTableColumns('#__user_saved_numbers', false);
        $__actionSnCols = is_array($__actionSnColsRaw) ? array_keys($__actionSnColsRaw) : array();
    } catch (\Throwable $__snColsE) {
        $__actionSnCols = array();
    }

    // Delete single prediction (hardened: use Joomla input filtering)
    $id = $app->input->post->getInt('delete_set', 0);
    if ($id > 0) {

        $q = $db->getQuery(true)

            ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
            ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . $id)
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
        if (in_array('save_intent', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
            $q->where(
                '(' .
                $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = 'prediction_archive' OR (" .
                $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = '' AND " . $db->quoteName('source') . " <> 'strategy_set'))"
            );
        }

        $db->setQuery($q);
        try {
            $db->execute();
            $app->enqueueMessage('Prediction deleted.', 'message');
            $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            error_log('[MLE] Error deleting prediction id=' . $id . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
            $app->enqueueMessage('An error occurred while deleting. Please try again.', 'error');
        }
    }
    // Delete multiple predictions via PRC table checkboxes (comma-separated IDs)
    $__rawSelected = $app->input->post->get('delete_set_selected', '', 'STRING');
    if ($__rawSelected !== '') {
        // intval() cast ensures all values are pure integers; safe to embed directly in SQL.
        $__selectedIds = array_values(array_filter(array_map('intval', explode(',', $__rawSelected))));
        if (!empty($__selectedIds)) {
            $q = $db->getQuery(true)
                ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
                ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' IN (' . implode(',', $__selectedIds) . ')')
                ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
            if (in_array('save_intent', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
                $q->where(
                    '(' .
                    $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = 'prediction_archive' OR (" .
                    $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = '' AND " . $db->quoteName('source') . " <> 'strategy_set'))"
                );
            }
            $db->setQuery($q);
            try {
                $db->execute();
                $count = count($__selectedIds);
                $app->enqueueMessage($count . ' prediction' . ($count !== 1 ? 's' : '') . ' deleted.', 'message');
                $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
            } catch (Exception $e) {
                error_log('[MLE] Error deleting multiple predictions: ' . $e->getMessage());
                $app->enqueueMessage('An error occurred while deleting. Please try again.', 'error');
            }
        }
    }

    // Delete all predictions (hardened: use Joomla input filtering)
    $doDeleteAll = $app->input->post->get('delete_all_predictions', '', 'STRING') !== '';
    if ($doDeleteAll) {
        $q = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
        if (in_array('save_intent', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
            $q->where(
                '(' .
                $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = 'prediction_archive' OR (" .
                $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = '' AND " . $db->quoteName('source') . " <> 'strategy_set'))"
            );
        }

        $db->setQuery($q);
        try {
            $db->execute();
            $app->enqueueMessage('All predictions deleted.', 'message');
            $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            error_log('[MLE] Error deleting all predictions for user=' . $workspaceUserId . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
            $app->enqueueMessage('An error occurred while deleting. Please try again.', 'error');
        }
    }

// Delete all predictions for a single canonical target draw (group delete)  -  hardened input
$doGroupDelete          = $app->input->post->get('delete_lottery_predictions', '', 'STRING') !== '';
$lotteryId              = $app->input->post->getInt('lottery_id', 0);
$drawDateRaw            = $app->input->post->getString('draw_date', '');
$predictionTargetIdPost = trim($app->input->post->getString('prediction_target_id', ''));
$targetDrawSessionPost  = mylottoexpertNormalizeTargetSession($app->input->post->getString('target_draw_session', ''));
$targetDrawAtPost       = trim($app->input->post->getString('target_draw_at', ''));
if ($doGroupDelete && ($predictionTargetIdPost !== '' || ($lotteryId && $drawDateRaw !== ''))) {
    $drawDate = '';
    if ($drawDateRaw !== '') {
        $drawDateTs = strtotime($drawDateRaw);
        $drawDate   = $drawDateTs !== false ? date('Y-m-d', $drawDateTs) : '';
    }

    // [FIX-DELETE-COLS] $__snCols is defined much later in this file (at the page-render phase).
    // Fetch column names locally here so the delete handler knows which optional columns exist,
    // regardless of where in the page lifecycle this POST fires.
    $__delSnCols = array();
    try {
        $__delSnColsRaw = $db->getTableColumns('#__user_saved_numbers', false);
        $__delSnCols = is_array($__delSnColsRaw) ? array_keys($__delSnColsRaw) : array();
    } catch (\Throwable $__delE) { $__delSnCols = array(); }

    // Helper: build the draw-date WHERE fragment using target_draw_date (COALESCE) when the
    // column exists, or next_draw_date as the sole fallback.  Reused in both branches below.
    $__buildDateCond = function ($date) use ($db, $__delSnCols) {
        if (in_array('target_draw_date', $__delSnCols, true)) {
            return 'DATE(COALESCE(' . $db->quoteName('target_draw_date') . ',' . $db->quoteName('next_draw_date') . ')) = ' . $db->quote($date);
        }
        return 'DATE(' . $db->quoteName('next_draw_date') . ') = ' . $db->quote($date);
    };

    $q = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
    if (in_array('save_intent', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
        $q->where(
            '(' .
            $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = 'prediction_archive' OR (" .
            $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = '' AND " . $db->quoteName('source') . " <> 'strategy_set'))"
        );
    }

    // [FIX-DELETE-LEGACY] When prediction_target_id is available (new rows), use it directly.
    // Older rows may have the column present but empty because they were saved before the
    // target-identity system was introduced. To delete both old and new rows reliably we
    // combine: (prediction_target_id = X  OR  (lottery_id = Y AND date = Z)).
    // The OR ensures legacy rows without a populated prediction_target_id are also removed.
    $hasPtidCol = in_array('prediction_target_id', $__delSnCols, true);
    if ($predictionTargetIdPost !== '' && $hasPtidCol && $lotteryId && $drawDate !== '') {
        $q->where(
            '(' .
            $db->quoteName('prediction_target_id') . ' = ' . $db->quote($predictionTargetIdPost) .
            ' OR (' . $db->quoteName('lottery_id') . ' = ' . $lotteryId . ' AND ' . $__buildDateCond($drawDate) . ')' .
            ')'
        );
    } elseif ($predictionTargetIdPost !== '' && $hasPtidCol) {
        $q->where($db->quoteName('prediction_target_id') . ' = ' . $db->quote($predictionTargetIdPost));
    } else {
        $q->where($db->quoteName('lottery_id') . ' = ' . $lotteryId);
        if ($drawDate !== '') {
            $q->where($__buildDateCond($drawDate));
        }
        if ($targetDrawSessionPost !== '' && in_array('target_draw_session', $__delSnCols, true)) {
            $q->where('LOWER(TRIM(COALESCE(' . $db->quoteName('target_draw_session') . ', ' . $db->quoteName('draw_session') . '))) = ' . $db->quote($targetDrawSessionPost));
        }
        if ($targetDrawAtPost !== '' && in_array('target_draw_at', $__delSnCols, true)) {
            $q->where('COALESCE(' . $db->quoteName('target_draw_at') . ', ' . $db->quoteName('next_draw_at') . ') = ' . $db->quote($targetDrawAtPost));
        }
    }

    $db->setQuery($q);
    try {
        $db->execute();
        $app->enqueueMessage('Deleted all predictions for this draw.', 'message');
        $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    } catch (Exception $e) {
        error_log('[MLE] Error deleting prediction group for user=' . $workspaceUserId . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
        $app->enqueueMessage('An error occurred while deleting. Please try again.', 'error');
    }
}

// Save prediction as Numbers to Play
$__savePredictionAsPlay = $app->input->post->getInt('save_prediction_as_play', 0);
if ($__savePredictionAsPlay > 0) {
    $__predictionSetId = $app->input->post->getInt('prediction_set_id', 0);
    if ($__predictionSetId > 0) {
        $q = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->select('*')
            ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
            ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . $__predictionSetId)
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
        $db->setQuery($q, 0, 1);
        $__srcRow = (array)$db->loadAssoc();

        if (!empty($__srcRow)) {
            $__srcMain = mylottoexpertParseNumberCsv($__srcRow['main_numbers'] ?? '', true);
            if (!empty($__srcMain)) {
                $__playInsert = $__srcRow;
                unset($__playInsert['id']);
                $__playInsert['source'] = 'strategy_set';
                $__playInsert['date_saved'] = date('Y-m-d H:i:s');
                $__playInsert['generated_at'] = date('Y-m-d H:i:s');
                $__playInsert['label'] = trim((string)($__srcRow['label'] ?? '')) !== ''
                    ? (trim((string)$__srcRow['label']) . ' - Play')
                    : ('Play Set - ' . date('Y-m-d H:i'));
                $__playInsert['save_intent'] = 'play_set';
                $__playInsert['origin_source'] = 'skai_prediction';
                $__playInsert['play_status'] = 'ready';
                $__playInsert['user_editable'] = 1;
                $__playInsert['wheel_export_count'] = 0;
                $__playInsert['wheel_exported_at'] = null;
                $__playInsert['is_favorite_play'] = 0;
                $__playInsert['play_notes'] = null;

                $__cols = array();
                $__vals = array();
                foreach ($__playInsert as $__col => $__val) {
                    if (!empty($__actionSnCols) && !in_array($__col, $__actionSnCols, true)) {
                        continue;
                    }
                    $__cols[] = $db->quoteName($__col);
                    if ($__val === null || $__val === '') {
                        $__vals[] = 'NULL';
                    } elseif (is_int($__val) || is_float($__val)) {
                        $__vals[] = (string)$__val;
                    } else {
                        $__vals[] = $db->quote((string)$__val);
                    }
                }

                if (!empty($__cols)) {
                    $q = $db->getQuery(true)
                        ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
                        ->columns($__cols)
                        ->values(implode(',', $__vals));
                    $db->setQuery($q);
                    try {
                        $db->execute();
                        $app->enqueueMessage('Saved as play set in Numbers to Play.', 'message');
                    } catch (Exception $__spE) {
                        error_log('[MLE] Failed Save as Play for row=' . $__predictionSetId . ': ' . $__spE->getMessage());
                        $app->enqueueMessage('Could not save this play set right now.', 'error');
                    }
                }
            } else {
                $app->enqueueMessage('This prediction has no numbers to save as a play set.', 'warning');
            }
        }
    }
    $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    exit;
}

// Update play set label/notes
$__updatePlayEntry = $app->input->post->getInt('update_play_entry', 0);
if ($__updatePlayEntry > 0) {
    $__playId = $app->input->post->getInt('play_set_id', 0);
    $__newLabel = substr(trim($app->input->post->getString('play_label', '')), 0, 80);
    $__newNotes = substr(trim($app->input->post->getString('play_notes', '')), 0, 1000);
    if ($__playId > 0 && $__newLabel !== '') {
        $q = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->update($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
            ->set($db->quoteName('label') . ' = ' . $db->quote($__newLabel))
            ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . $__playId)
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
        if (in_array('play_notes', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
            $q->set($db->quoteName('play_notes') . ' = ' . ($__newNotes !== '' ? $db->quote($__newNotes) : 'NULL'));
        }
        $db->setQuery($q);
        try {
            $db->execute();
            $app->enqueueMessage('Play set updated.', 'message');
        } catch (Exception $__upe) {
            error_log('[MLE] update_play_entry failed: ' . $__upe->getMessage());
            $app->enqueueMessage('Could not update this play set right now.', 'error');
        }
    }
    $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    exit;
}

// Duplicate play entry
$__duplicatePlayEntry = $app->input->post->getInt('duplicate_play_entry', 0);
if ($__duplicatePlayEntry > 0) {
    $__playId = $app->input->post->getInt('play_set_id', 0);
    if ($__playId > 0) {
        $q = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->select('*')
            ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
            ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . $__playId)
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
        if (in_array('save_intent', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
            $q->where(
                '(' . $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " IN ('play_set','custom_play','wheel_candidate')" .
                ' OR (' . $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = '' AND " . $db->quoteName('source') . " = 'strategy_set')" .
                ')'
            );
        }
        $db->setQuery($q, 0, 1);
        $__dupRow = (array)$db->loadAssoc();
        if (!empty($__dupRow)) {
            unset($__dupRow['id']);
            $__dupRow['label'] = substr(trim((string)($__dupRow['label'] ?? '')) . ' (Copy)', 0, 80);
            $__dupRow['date_saved'] = date('Y-m-d H:i:s');
            $__dupRow['generated_at'] = date('Y-m-d H:i:s');
            if (in_array('wheel_export_count', $__actionSnCols, true)) { $__dupRow['wheel_export_count'] = 0; }
            if (in_array('wheel_exported_at', $__actionSnCols, true)) { $__dupRow['wheel_exported_at'] = null; }

            $__cols = array();
            $__vals = array();
            foreach ($__dupRow as $__col => $__val) {
                if (!empty($__actionSnCols) && !in_array($__col, $__actionSnCols, true)) {
                    continue;
                }
                $__cols[] = $db->quoteName($__col);
                if ($__val === null || $__val === '') {
                    $__vals[] = 'NULL';
                } elseif (is_int($__val) || is_float($__val)) {
                    $__vals[] = (string)$__val;
                } else {
                    $__vals[] = $db->quote((string)$__val);
                }
            }

            if (!empty($__cols)) {
                $q = $db->getQuery(true)
                    ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
                    ->columns($__cols)
                    ->values(implode(',', $__vals));
                $db->setQuery($q);
                try {
                    $db->execute();
                    $app->enqueueMessage('Play set duplicated.', 'message');
                } catch (Exception $__dpe) {
                    error_log('[MLE] duplicate_play_entry failed: ' . $__dpe->getMessage());
                    $app->enqueueMessage('Could not duplicate this play set right now.', 'error');
                }
            }
        }
    }
    $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    exit;
}

            $db->execute();

        } catch (Exception $__ape) {
            error_log('[MLE] archive_play_entry failed: ' . $__ape->getMessage());
            $app->enqueueMessage('Could not archive this play set right now.', 'error');
        }

    $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());

// Send play set to Wheel Builder
$__sendPlayToWheel = $app->input->post->getInt('send_play_to_wheel', 0);
if ($__sendPlayToWheel > 0) {
    $__playId = $app->input->post->getInt('play_set_id', 0);
    $__systemId = $app->input->post->getInt('play_system_id', 0);
    if ($__playId > 0) {
        $q = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->select(array('id', 'main_numbers'))
            ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
            ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . $__playId)
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
        if (in_array('save_intent', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
            $q->where(
                '(' . $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " IN ('play_set','custom_play','wheel_candidate')" .
                ' OR (' . $db->quoteName('save_intent') . " = '' AND " . $db->quoteName('source') . " = 'strategy_set')" .
                ')'
            );
        }
        $db->setQuery($q, 0, 1);
        $__playForWheel = (array)$db->loadAssoc();

        if (!empty($__playForWheel) && !empty(mylottoexpertParseNumberCsv($__playForWheel['main_numbers'] ?? '', true))) {
            if (in_array('wheel_export_count', $__actionSnCols, true) || in_array('wheel_exported_at', $__actionSnCols, true) || in_array('play_status', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
                $q = $db->getQuery(true)
                    ->update($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
                    ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . $__playId)
                    ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
                if (in_array('wheel_export_count', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
                    $q->set($db->quoteName('wheel_export_count') . ' = COALESCE(' . $db->quoteName('wheel_export_count') . ',0) + 1');
                }
                if (in_array('wheel_exported_at', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
                    $q->set($db->quoteName('wheel_exported_at') . ' = ' . $db->quote(date('Y-m-d H:i:s')));
                }
                if (in_array('play_status', $__actionSnCols, true)) {
                    $q->set($db->quoteName('play_status') . " = 'wheeled'");
                }
                $db->setQuery($q);
                try {
                    $db->execute();
                } catch (Exception $__swe) {
                    error_log('[MLE] send_play_to_wheel usage update failed: ' . $__swe->getMessage());
                }
            }

            $__wheelUrl = '/wheel-builder1?play_set_id=' . (int)$__playId . '&source=mylottoexpert';
            if ($__systemId > 0) {
                $__wheelUrl .= '&system_id=' . (int)$__systemId;
            }
            $__endpointUri = \Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::base());
            $__endpointUri->setPath(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString(array('path')));
            $__endpointUri->setVar('mle_action', 'play_set_payload');
            $__endpointUrl = $__endpointUri->toString(array('path', 'query'));
            $__wheelUrl .= '&play_set_endpoint=' . rawurlencode($__endpointUrl);
            $__endpointUri->setVar('mle_action', 'play_sets_list');
            $__listEndpointUrl = $__endpointUri->toString(array('path', 'query'));
            $__wheelUrl .= '&play_sets_endpoint=' . rawurlencode($__listEndpointUrl);
            $app->redirect($__wheelUrl);
            exit;
        }
    }
    $app->enqueueMessage('Play set could not be loaded for wheel export.', 'error');
    $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    exit;
}

// [[MLE_USER_NOTES_MIGRATION]] Add user_notes column if it does not yet exist.
// Wrapped in try/catch so it is a no-op on databases that already have the column.
try {
    $db->setQuery("ALTER TABLE " . $db->quoteName('#__user_saved_settings') . " ADD COLUMN `user_notes` TEXT NULL DEFAULT NULL");
    $db->execute();
} catch (Exception $__e) { /* column already exists - safe to ignore */ }

// Update saved-settings note
$__noteId = $app->input->post->getInt('update_setting_note', 0);
if ($__noteId > 0) {
    $__noteText = $app->input->post->get('user_notes', '', 'STRING');
    // Limit to 1000 chars and strip control characters except newlines/tabs
    $__noteText = preg_replace('/[^\P{C}\n\t]/u', '', substr(trim((string)$__noteText), 0, 1000));
    $q = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->update($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_settings'))
        ->set($db->quoteName('user_notes') . ' = ' . $db->quote($__noteText))
        ->where($db->quoteName('id')      . ' = ' . $__noteId)
        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
    $db->setQuery($q);
    try {
        $db->execute();
    } catch (Exception $__ne) {
        error_log('[MLE] Failed to save note for setting id=' . $__noteId . ': ' . $__ne->getMessage());
        $app->enqueueMessage('An error occurred while saving the note. Please try again.', 'error');
    }
    $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    exit;
}

// Delete saved setting template (hardened: use Joomla input filtering)
$id = $app->input->post->getInt('delete_setting_template', 0);
if ($id > 0) {

        // $id already sanitized above
        $q = $db->getQuery(true)
            ->delete($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_settings'))

            ->where($db->quoteName('id') . ' = ' . $id)
            ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);

        $db->setQuery($q);
        try {
            $db->execute();
            $app->enqueueMessage('Saved setting deleted.', 'message');
            $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        } catch (Exception $e) {
            error_log('[MLE] Error deleting saved setting id=' . $id . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
            $app->enqueueMessage('An error occurred while deleting the saved setting. Please try again.', 'error');
        }
    }

    // Save prediction settings as a named template (hardened: use Joomla input filtering)
    if ($app->input->post->get('save_setting_template', '', 'STRING') !== '') {
        $settingName     = trim($app->input->post->getString('setting_name', ''));
        $source          = $app->input->post->getString('source', '');
        $lotteryId       = $app->input->post->getInt('lottery_id', 0);
        // [[FIX]] Use a scoped name to avoid clobbering the Joomla Registry $params
        // that the module framework injects and that is used later at render time.
        $__sstParamsData = [];

        // Define expected params based on source
        $keys = match ($source) {
            'ai_prediction'   => [
                'epochs', 'batch_size', 'dropout_rate',
                'learning_rate', 'activation_function',
                'hidden_layers', 'recency_decay',
            ],
            'skai_prediction' => [
                // Core neural hyperparameters
                'epochs', 'batch_size', 'dropout_rate',
                'learning_rate', 'activation_function',
                'hidden_layers', 'recency_decay',
                // Windows
                'skai_window_size', 'skip_window', 'draws_used', 'tuned_window',
                // Behavior & sampling
                'sampling_temperature', 'diversity_penalty', 'gap_scale',
                // Mode / automation
                'skai_run_mode', 'auto_tune', 'tune_used', 'best_window',
                // Smart blend / strategy
                'profile', 'training_style', 'strategy', 'blend',
                'skai_blend_skip_pct', 'skai_blend_ai_pct',
                'blend_skip_pct', 'blend_ai_pct',
                'skip_pct', 'ai_pct',
                // Output size
                'skai_top_n_numbers', 'skai_top_n_combos',
            ],
            'mcmc_prediction' => ['walks', 'burn_in', 'laplace_k', 'decay', 'chain_len'],
            'skip_hit'        => ['draws_analyzed', 'freq_weight', 'skip_weight', 'hist_weight'],
            default           => []
        };

        foreach ($keys as $k) {
            $val = $app->input->post->get($k, null, 'STRING'); // keep as STRING to avoid behavior changes
            if ($val !== null && $val !== '') {
                $__sstParamsData[$k] = $val;
            }
        }

        // Always capture the four identity fields for consistent recall display.
        // These are captured from all sources so that the saved settings card always shows:
        //   Training Style / Strategy / Mode / Blend
        foreach (['training_style', 'profile', 'strategy', 'skai_run_mode', 'blend',
                  'skai_blend_skip_pct', 'skai_blend_ai_pct'] as $__identKey) {
            if (!array_key_exists($__identKey, $__sstParamsData)) {
                $__iv = $app->input->post->get($__identKey, null, 'STRING');
                if ($__iv !== null && $__iv !== '') {
                    $__sstParamsData[$__identKey] = $__iv;
                }
            }
        }
        // Capture the page/context this was saved from (Sky, AI, etc.) for recall display.
        $__pageSaved = trim($app->input->post->getString('page_saved_from', ''));
        if ($__pageSaved !== '') {
            $__sstParamsData['page_saved_from'] = substr($__pageSaved, 0, 64);
        }

        if ($settingName && $source && $lotteryId && $__sstParamsData) {
            $q = $db->getQuery(true)
                ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_settings'))
                ->columns(['user_id', 'lottery_id', 'source', 'setting_name', 'params'])
                ->values(implode(',', [
                    $workspaceUserId,
                    $lotteryId,
                    $db->quote($source),
                    $db->quote($settingName),
                    $db->quote(json_encode($__sstParamsData, JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE))
                ]));

            $db->setQuery($q);
            try {
                $db->execute();
                $app->enqueueMessage('Settings saved.', 'message');
            } catch (Exception $e) {
                error_log('[MLE] Failed to save settings template for user=' . $workspaceUserId . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
                $app->enqueueMessage('An error occurred while saving. Please try again.', 'error');
            }
        }
        // [[FIX]] Always redirect after save (Post-Redirect-Get) to prevent double-submit
        // and to ensure execution never falls through to render code with $__sstParamsData in scope.
        $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
        exit;
    }

    // Module keys needed for save_strategy_set source whitelisting below.
    // Defined here so it is available before the main render block (line ~1736).
    if (!isset($modules)) {
        $modules = array(
            array('key' => 'skip_hit',        'label' => 'SKIP Model',      'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Analyzes historical draw patterns'),
            array('key' => 'ai_prediction',   'label' => 'Neural Network',  'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Deep learning model trained on draw history'),
            array('key' => 'mcmc_prediction', 'label' => 'MCMC',            'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Statistical sampling method'),
            array('key' => 'heatmap',         'label' => 'Frequency Map',   'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Visual frequency analysis'),
            array('key' => 'skai_prediction', 'label' => 'SKAI Model',      'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Combines multiple analytical methods'),
        );
    }

    // Save Strategy Set (from Overview PRE-DRAW workspace)
    if ($app->input->post->getInt('save_strategy_set', 0) > 0) {
        // Require authenticated user
        if ($user->guest || $workspaceUserId <= 0) {
            $app->enqueueMessage('You must be logged in to save a strategy set.', 'error');
            $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
            exit;
        }
        $__stLid  = $app->input->post->getInt('strategy_lottery_id', 0);
        $__stDate = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_draw_date', ''));
        $__stMain = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_main_numbers', ''));
        $__stExt  = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_extra_numbers', ''));
        $__stLbl  = substr(trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_label', '')), 0, 80);
        $__stSrc  = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_active_sources', ''));
        $__stTargetGameId         = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_target_game_id', ''));
        $__stTargetDrawAt         = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_target_draw_at', ''));
        $__stTargetDrawSession    = mylottoexpertNormalizeTargetSession($app->input->post->getString('strategy_target_draw_session', ''));
        $__stTargetPredictionType = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_target_prediction_type', ''));
        $__stTargetFamily         = trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_target_prediction_family', ''));
        $__stSaveIntent           = strtolower(trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_save_intent', 'play_set')));
        $__stOriginSource         = strtolower(trim($app->input->post->getString('strategy_origin_source', 'strategy_builder')));
        if (!in_array($__stSaveIntent, array('play_set', 'custom_play', 'wheel_candidate'), true)) {
            $__stSaveIntent = 'play_set';
        }
        if (!in_array($__stOriginSource, array('strategy_builder', 'manual', 'imported', 'skai_prediction'), true)) {
            $__stOriginSource = ($__stSaveIntent === 'custom_play') ? 'manual' : 'strategy_builder';
        }

        // Validate lottery_id exists in lotteries table
        $__stLidCheck = 0;
        $__stLottoRow = null;
        if ($__stLid > 0) {
            $__qLid = $db->getQuery(true)->select(array('lottery_id','game_id','name'))
                ->from($db->quoteName('#__lotteries'))
                ->where($db->quoteName('lottery_id') . ' = ' . (int)$__stLid);
            $db->setQuery($__qLid, 0, 1);
            $__stLottoRow = $db->loadAssoc();
            $__stLidCheck = (int)($__stLottoRow['lottery_id'] ?? 0);
            if ($__stTargetGameId === '' && !empty($__stLottoRow['game_id'])) {
                $__stTargetGameId = (string)$__stLottoRow['game_id'];
            }
        }

        // Whitelist active sources against known module keys
        $__validSrcKeys = array_column($modules, 'key');
        $__stSrcKeys    = array_values(array_filter(
            array_map('trim', explode(',', $__stSrc)),
            static function($k) use ($__validSrcKeys) { return in_array($k, $__validSrcKeys, true); }
        ));

        // Parse and validate numbers (positive integers only)
        $__stMainNums = array_values(array_filter(array_map('intval',
            array_filter(explode(',', $__stMain), 'strlen')),
            static function($n) { return $n > 0; }));
        $__stExtNums  = array_values(array_filter(array_map('intval',
            array_filter(explode(',', $__stExt), 'strlen')),
            static function($n) { return $n > 0; }));

        // Normalize date; reject if unparseable
        $__stTs       = $__stDate !== '' ? strtotime($__stDate) : false;
        $__stNormDate = $__stTs !== false ? date('Y-m-d', $__stTs) : '';

        if ($__stLidCheck > 0 && $__stNormDate !== '' && count($__stMainNums) > 0) {
            $__stLabel = $__stLbl !== '' ? $__stLbl
                : 'Play Set - ' . date('Y-m-d H:i');

            if ($__stTargetFamily === '') {
                $__stTargetFamily = 'regular';
            }
            if ($__stTargetPredictionType === '') {
                $__stTargetPredictionType = $__stTargetFamily;
            }

            $__stTarget = mylottoexpertBuildPredictionTarget(array(
                'game_id'           => $__stTargetGameId,
                'lottery_id'        => $__stLidCheck,
                'draw_date'         => $__stNormDate,
                'draw_at'           => $__stTargetDrawAt,
                'draw_session'      => $__stTargetDrawSession,
                'timezone_id'       => 'America/New_York',
                'prediction_family' => $__stTargetFamily,
                'prediction_type'   => $__stTargetPredictionType,
                'pick_size'         => count($__stMainNums),
                'extra_count'       => count($__stExtNums),
            ));

            $__strategyRunUuid = mylottoexpertGenerateRunUuid();
            $__stInsert = array(
                'user_id'                 => $workspaceUserId,
                'lottery_id'              => $__stLidCheck,
                'next_draw_date'          => $__stNormDate,
                'next_draw_at'            => ($__stTarget['target_draw_at'] ?? null),
                'draw_session'            => ($__stTarget['target_draw_session'] ?? null),
                'source'                  => 'strategy_set',
                'label'                   => $__stLabel,
                'main_numbers'            => implode(',', $__stMainNums),
                'extra_ball_numbers'      => implode(',', $__stExtNums),
                'date_saved'              => date('Y-m-d H:i:s'),
                'generated_at'            => date('Y-m-d H:i:s'),
                'run_uuid'                => $__strategyRunUuid,
                'snapshot_run_uuid'       => $__strategyRunUuid,
                'prediction_target_id'    => ($__stTarget['prediction_target_id'] ?? null),
                'prediction_target_key'   => ($__stTarget['prediction_target_key'] ?? null),
                'prediction_target_json'  => ($__stTarget['prediction_target_json'] ?? null),
                'target_game_id'          => ($__stTarget['target_game_id'] ?? null),
                'target_lottery_id'       => ($__stTarget['target_lottery_id'] ?? null),
                'target_draw_date'        => ($__stTarget['target_draw_date'] ?? null),
                'target_draw_at'          => ($__stTarget['target_draw_at'] ?? null),
                'target_draw_session'     => ($__stTarget['target_draw_session'] ?? null),
                'target_timezone_id'      => ($__stTarget['target_timezone_id'] ?? null),
                'target_prediction_family'=> ($__stTarget['target_prediction_family'] ?? null),
                'target_prediction_type'  => ($__stTarget['target_prediction_type'] ?? null),
                'target_pick_size'        => ($__stTarget['target_pick_size'] ?? null),
                'target_extra_count'      => ($__stTarget['target_extra_count'] ?? null),
                'save_intent'             => $__stSaveIntent,
                'origin_source'           => $__stOriginSource,
                'play_status'             => 'ready',
                'user_editable'           => 1,
                'wheel_export_count'      => 0,
                'wheel_exported_at'       => null,
                'is_favorite_play'        => 0,
            );

            $__stColumnsMap = array();
            try {
                $__stColumnsRaw = $db->getTableColumns('#__user_saved_numbers');
                $__stColumnsMap = is_array($__stColumnsRaw) ? array_change_key_case($__stColumnsRaw, CASE_LOWER) : array();
            } catch (Exception $e) {
                $__stColumnsMap = array();
            }

            $__stColumns = array();
            $__stValues  = array();
            foreach ($__stInsert as $__stCol => $__stVal) {
                if (!empty($__stColumnsMap) && !array_key_exists(strtolower($__stCol), $__stColumnsMap)) {
                    continue;
                }
                $__stColumns[] = $db->quoteName($__stCol);
                if ($__stVal === null || $__stVal === '') {
                    $__stValues[] = 'NULL';
                } elseif (is_int($__stVal) || is_float($__stVal)) {
                    $__stValues[] = (string)$__stVal;
                } else {
                    $__stValues[] = $db->quote((string)$__stVal);
                }
            }

            $q = $db->getQuery(true)
                ->insert($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
                ->columns($__stColumns)
                ->values(implode(',', $__stValues));
            $db->setQuery($q);
            try {
                $db->execute();
                $app->enqueueMessage('Play set saved to Numbers to Play.', 'message');
            } catch (Exception $e) {
                error_log('[MLE] Error saving strategy for user=' . $workspaceUserId . ': ' . $e->getMessage());
                $app->enqueueMessage('An error occurred while saving the play set. Please try again.', 'error');
            }
        } else {
            $app->enqueueMessage('Please add at least one number before saving.', 'warning');
        }
        $app->redirect(\Joomla\CMS\Uri\Uri::getInstance()->toString());
    }
}

// --------------------------------------------------
// Echo your Sorcerer module
// --------------------------------------------------
echo mylottoexpertRenderModuleById((int) $params->get('header_module_id', 126), (string) $params->get('header_module_style', 'none'));

       . '<strong>Demo Workspace:</strong> You are viewing the real LottoExpert workspace in read-only demo mode. Saving, deleting, and account-specific changes are disabled.'
       . '</div>';
}
