            'target_prediction_type'   => $__targetMeta['target_prediction_type'],
            'preds'                    => array(),
        );
    }

    $groups[$__groupKey]['preds'][] = $s;

    // Build tableInfo by canonical game_id, using either the master config or the daily catalog.
    if (!isset($tableInfo[$__groupGameId])) {
        $spec = mylottoexpertLoadLotterySpec($__groupGameId);
        $__lc = isset($spec['lotteryConfig']) && is_array($spec['lotteryConfig']) ? $spec['lotteryConfig'] : array();

        // Build extras array: support extra_ball_columns (array), extra_ball_column, extra_ball_column_2
        $__teExtras = [];
        if (!empty($__lc['extra_ball_columns']) && is_array($__lc['extra_ball_columns'])) {
            foreach ($__lc['extra_ball_columns'] as $__ec) {
                $__ec = trim((string)$__ec);
                if ($__ec !== '' && !in_array($__ec, $__teExtras, true)) { $__teExtras[] = $__ec; }
            }
        }
        foreach (['extra_ball_column', 'extra_ball_column_2'] as $__eck) {
            if (!empty($__lc[$__eck])) {
                $__ec = trim((string)$__lc[$__eck]);
                if ($__ec !== '' && !in_array($__ec, $__teExtras, true)) { $__teExtras[] = $__ec; }
            }
        }
        $__teIsDaily = !empty($__lc['is_daily']);
        $__teNumExtra = max(count($__teExtras), (int)($__lc['num_extra_balls_drawn'] ?? 0));
        if (!$__teIsDaily && empty($__teExtras)) {
            $__teNumExtra = 0;
        }

        $tableInfo[$__groupGameId] = array(
            'table'              => $spec['dbCol'] ?? '',
            'main'               => $__lc['main_ball_columns'] ?? array(),
            'extra'              => $__teExtras[0] ?? null,
            'extra2'             => $__teExtras[1] ?? null,
            'extras'             => $__teExtras,
            'num_extra_expected' => $__teNumExtra,
        );
    }
}

// Compute the maximum number of main balls and the maximum number of extra ball columns
// across all games (used to build uniform UNION ALL SELECT lists).
$maxMain   = 0;
$maxExtras = 0;

foreach ($tableInfo as $info) {
    $mainCount = count($info['main']);
    if ($mainCount > $maxMain) { $maxMain = $mainCount; }

    $extrasCount = max(count($info['extras'] ?? []), (int)($info['num_extra_expected'] ?? 0));
    if ($extrasCount > $maxExtras) { $maxExtras = $extrasCount; }
}
// Backward compat: if no game explicitly listed extra columns but the old $hasExtra logic found one,
// ensure $maxExtras >= 1.
$hasExtra = ($maxExtras >= 1);

// Build UNION ALL query parts for actual draws and construct a preloaded draw map.
$unionParts = array();

foreach ($groups as $g) {
    $tblKey = (string)($g['game_id'] ?? '');

    if ($tblKey === '' || empty($tableInfo[$tblKey]['table'])) {
        continue;
    }

    $tblName = $tableInfo[$tblKey]['table'];
    $tbl     = $db->quoteName($db->replacePrefix($tblName));

    // Build column list: draw_date + aliased mains + optional aliased extras.
    $cols   = array();
    $cols[] = $db->quoteName('draw_date');

    for ($i = 0; $i < $maxMain; $i++) {
        if (!empty($tableInfo[$tblKey]['main'][$i])) {
            // Alias each main ball column to a normalized name: main_0, main_1, ...
            $cols[] = $db->quoteName($tableInfo[$tblKey]['main'][$i]) . ' AS main_' . $i;
        } else {
            $cols[] = 'NULL AS main_' . $i;
        }
    }

    // Alias all extra ball columns uniformly.
    // Naming convention: index 0 -> 'extra_ball', index 1 -> 'extra_ball_2', index 2 -> 'extra_ball_3', ...
    // (extra_ball is the legacy name for the first extra; subsequent extras use _2, _3, ... suffixes)
    // All SELECT statements in the UNION must have the same number of columns, so games
    // with fewer extras emit NULL placeholders.
    for ($__ei = 0; $__ei < $maxExtras; $__ei++) {
        $__eAlias  = $__ei === 0 ? 'extra_ball' : 'extra_ball_' . ($__ei + 1);
        $__eCol    = $tableInfo[$tblKey]['extras'][$__ei] ?? null;
        if (!empty($__eCol)) {
            $cols[] = $db->quoteName($__eCol) . ' AS ' . $__eAlias;
        } else {
            $cols[] = 'NULL AS ' . $__eAlias;
        }
    }

    $cols     = implode(',', $cols);
    // Normalize the date to Y-m-d to ensure clean DATE() comparison regardless of time component.
    $__drawTs = strtotime((string)($g['draw_date'] ?? ''));
    $__drawDateNorm = ($__drawTs !== false && $__drawTs > 0) ? date('Y-m-d', $__drawTs) : (string)($g['draw_date'] ?? '');
    $escapedDate = $db->quote($__drawDateNorm);

    $unionParts[] =
        'SELECT ' . $db->quote($tblKey) . ' AS game_id, ' . $cols . ', ' . $escapedDate . ' AS req_date'
        . ' FROM ' . $tbl
        . ' WHERE ' . $db->quoteName('game_id') . ' = ' . $db->quote($tblKey)
        . ' AND DATE(' . $db->quoteName('draw_date') . ') = ' . $escapedDate;
}

$unionSql = implode(' UNION ALL ', $unionParts);

/**
 * Preload all requested draws into a normalized draw map:
 * $drawMap["<game_id>|<Y-m-d>"] = array(
 *     'game_id'      => int,
 *     'draw_date'    => 'Y-m-d ...',
 *     'main_0'       => int|null,
 *     'main_1'       => int|null,
 *     ...
 *     'extra_ball'   => int|null,
 *     'extra_ball_2' => int|null,   // second extra (e.g. EuroMillions Lucky Star 2), if maxExtras >= 2
 *     'extra_ball_3' => int|null,   // third extra, if maxExtras >= 3
 * );
 */
$drawMap = array();

if (!empty($unionSql)) {
    try {
        $db->setQuery($unionSql);
        $rows = (array) $db->loadAssocList();

        foreach ($rows as $row) {
            // Normalize requested date to Y-m-d for consistent keying.
            $reqDate = isset($row['req_date']) ? $row['req_date'] : $row['draw_date'];
            try {
                $dt      = new DateTime($reqDate);
                $norm    = $dt->format('Y-m-d');
            } catch (Exception $e) {
                // Fallback: use raw value if parsing fails.
                $norm = $reqDate;
            }

            $gId = isset($row['game_id']) ? trim((string)$row['game_id']) : '';
            if ($gId === '') {
                continue;
            }

            $mapKey = strtolower($gId) . '|' . $norm;

            // Store the entire row; rendering logic can map fields as needed.
            $drawMap[$mapKey] = $row;
        }
    } catch (RuntimeException $e) {
        // If UNION query fails for any reason, fall back to per-card getDrawByDate().
        $drawMap = array();
    }
}

// ------------------------------------------------------------------
// 6) Compute Best Opportunities per lottery (Agreement / Top-Hits)
//    Uses the preloaded $drawMap as the single data source -- no extra DB queries.
//    Results stored in $bestOpps[lottery_id] for the summary panel.
// ------------------------------------------------------------------

$bestOpps = array();

// Per-game+date draw cache used by the fallback below (avoids repeated DB queries).
$__drawCache = array();

// Shared rank comparator: hits desc -> extra_hits desc -> rank_score desc -> run_id desc
$__rankCompare = function (array $a, array $b) {
    if ($a['hits'] !== $b['hits']) { return $b['hits'] - $a['hits']; }
    if ($a['extra_hits'] !== $b['extra_hits']) { return $b['extra_hits'] - $a['extra_hits']; }
    if ($a['rank_score'] !== $b['rank_score']) { return $b['rank_score'] - $a['rank_score']; }
    return $b['run_id'] - $a['run_id'];
};

foreach ($groups as $groupKey => $g) {
    $lid = (int)$g['lottery_id'];

    if (!isset($bestOpps[$lid])) {
        $bestOpps[$lid] = array(
            'lottery_name'    => (string)($g['lottery_name'] ?? ''),
            'lottery_id'      => $lid,
            'game_id'         => (string)($g['game_id'] ?? ''),
            'state_name'      => (string)($lottoMetaById[$lid]['state'] ?? ''),
            'total_runs'      => 0,
            'best_agreement'  => array('score' => -1, 'draw_date' => '', 'numbers' => array(), 'methods' => array(), 'run_id' => 0, 'source' => ''),
            'best_rank'       => array('score' => -1, 'draw_date' => '', 'run_id' => 0, 'source' => '', 'hits' => 0, 'extra_hits' => 0, 'numbers' => array(), 'extra_number' => 0),
            'all_scored_runs' => array(),
        );
    }
    $bestOpps[$lid]['total_runs'] += count($g['preds']);

    // -- Agreement scoring: numbers shared across different methods --
    $allSourceNumPool = array();
    foreach ($g['preds'] as $s) {
        $src  = (string)$s->source;
        $__isDailyRow = (
            (isset($s->prediction_family) && (string)$s->prediction_family === 'daily') ||
            (isset($s->render_mode) && (string)$s->render_mode === 'daily_combos') ||
            (!empty($s->daily_primary_prediction))
        );
        if ($__isDailyRow) {
            $nums = array();
            if (!empty($s->daily_primary_prediction_json)) {
                $__dpj = json_decode((string)$s->daily_primary_prediction_json, true);
                if (is_array($__dpj)) { $nums = array_map('intval', $__dpj); }
            }
            if (empty($nums) && !empty($s->daily_primary_prediction)) {
                preg_match_all('/\d/', (string)$s->daily_primary_prediction, $__dm);
                if (!empty($__dm[0])) { $nums = array_map('intval', $__dm[0]); }
            }
            if (empty($nums)) {
                $__fc = explode(',', (string)($s->main_numbers ?? ''));
                preg_match_all('/\d/', (string)($__fc[0] ?? ''), $__dm2);
                if (!empty($__dm2[0])) { $nums = array_map('intval', $__dm2[0]); }
            }
        } else {
            $nums = array_filter(array_map('intval', explode(',', (string)($s->main_numbers ?? ''))));
        }
        if (!isset($allSourceNumPool[$src])) { $allSourceNumPool[$src] = array(); }
        foreach ($nums as $n) { $allSourceNumPool[$src][$n] = true; }
    }
    foreach ($g['preds'] as $s) {
        $src    = (string)$s->source;
        $__isDailyRow2 = (
            (isset($s->prediction_family) && (string)$s->prediction_family === 'daily') ||
            (isset($s->render_mode) && (string)$s->render_mode === 'daily_combos') ||
            (!empty($s->daily_primary_prediction))
        );
        if ($__isDailyRow2) {
            $myNums = array();
            if (!empty($s->daily_primary_prediction_json)) {
                $__dpj2 = json_decode((string)$s->daily_primary_prediction_json, true);
                if (is_array($__dpj2)) { $myNums = array_map('intval', $__dpj2); }
            }
            if (empty($myNums) && !empty($s->daily_primary_prediction)) {
                preg_match_all('/\d/', (string)$s->daily_primary_prediction, $__dm3);
                if (!empty($__dm3[0])) { $myNums = array_map('intval', $__dm3[0]); }
            }
            if (empty($myNums)) {
                $__fc2 = explode(',', (string)($s->main_numbers ?? ''));
                preg_match_all('/\d/', (string)($__fc2[0] ?? ''), $__dm4);
                if (!empty($__dm4[0])) { $myNums = array_map('intval', $__dm4[0]); }
            }
        } else {
            $myNums = array_filter(array_map('intval', explode(',', (string)($s->main_numbers ?? ''))));
        }
        $otherNums = array();
        $otherSrcList = array();
        foreach ($allSourceNumPool as $otherSrc => $numSet) {
            if ($otherSrc !== $src) {
                foreach ($numSet as $n => $_unused) { $otherNums[$n] = true; }
                $otherSrcList[] = $otherSrc;
            }
        }
        $otherSrcList = array_unique($otherSrcList);
        $agreed = array();
        foreach ($myNums as $n) {
            if (isset($otherNums[$n])) { $agreed[] = $n; }
        }
        $score = count($agreed);
        $prev  = $bestOpps[$lid]['best_agreement'];
        $isBetter = ($score > $prev['score'])
            || ($score === $prev['score'] && count($otherSrcList) > count($prev['methods']))
            || ($score === $prev['score'] && count($otherSrcList) === count($prev['methods']) && (int)$s->id > (int)$prev['run_id']);
        if ($isBetter) {
            sort($agreed);
            $bestOpps[$lid]['best_agreement'] = array(
                'score'     => $score,
                'draw_date' => (string)$g['draw_date'],
                'numbers'   => $agreed,
                'methods'   => $otherSrcList,
                'run_id'    => (int)$s->id,
                'source'    => $src,
            );
        }
    }

    // -- Hit scoring: compare each prediction to the actual drawn numbers via $drawMap --
    foreach ($g['preds'] as $s) {
        $__isDailyPred = (
            (isset($s->prediction_family) && (string)$s->prediction_family === 'daily') ||
            (isset($s->render_mode) && (string)$s->render_mode === 'daily_combos') ||
            (!empty($s->daily_primary_prediction))
        );
        if ($__isDailyPred) {
            $predMain = array();
            if (!empty($s->daily_primary_prediction_json)) {
                $__dpj3 = json_decode((string)$s->daily_primary_prediction_json, true);
                if (is_array($__dpj3)) { $predMain = array_values(array_map('intval', $__dpj3)); }
            }
            if (empty($predMain) && !empty($s->daily_primary_prediction)) {
                preg_match_all('/\d/', (string)$s->daily_primary_prediction, $__dm5);
                if (!empty($__dm5[0])) { $predMain = array_map('intval', $__dm5[0]); }
            }
            if (empty($predMain)) {
                $__fc3 = explode(',', (string)($s->main_numbers ?? ''));
                preg_match_all('/\d/', (string)($__fc3[0] ?? ''), $__dm6);
                if (!empty($__dm6[0])) { $predMain = array_map('intval', $__dm6[0]); }
            }
        } else {
            $predMain = array_values(array_filter(
                array_map('intval', explode(',', (string)($s->main_numbers ?? ''))),
                function ($n) { return $n !== 0; }
            ));
        }
        $predExtra = 0;
        if (isset($s->extra_ball_numbers) && $s->extra_ball_numbers !== '' && $s->extra_ball_numbers !== null) {
            $tmp = array_values(array_filter(array_map('intval', explode(',', (string)$s->extra_ball_numbers))));
            if (!empty($tmp)) { $predExtra = (int)$tmp[0]; }
        }

        $__scored = scoreRunFromDrawMap($drawMap, (string)$g['game_id'], (string)$g['draw_date'], $predMain, $predExtra);

        // -- Fallback: when the UNION-ALL/drawMap path has no data for this
        //    game+date (common for regular lotteries without an extra ball or
        //    when the UNION ALL query failed), fall back to a direct DB lookup  - 
        //    same two-phase logic used by the per-draw-group rendering code. --
        if (!$__scored['has_draw']) {
            $__bkTs  = strtotime((string)$g['draw_date']);
            $__bkKey = $g['game_id'] . ':' . ($__bkTs ? date('Y-m-d', $__bkTs) : (string)$g['draw_date']);
            if (!array_key_exists($__bkKey, $__drawCache)) {
                $__bkRow    = getDrawByDate($g['game_id'], (string)$g['draw_date'], $db);
                $__bkMain   = array();
                $__bkExtra  = array();
                if ($__bkRow !== null) {
                    if (array_key_exists('main_0', $__bkRow)) {
                        // Row came from $drawMap (normalized fields)
                        for ($__bi = 0; $__bi < 25; $__bi++) {
                            $__bk = 'main_' . $__bi;
                            if (isset($__bkRow[$__bk]) && $__bkRow[$__bk] !== '' && $__bkRow[$__bk] !== null) {
                                $__bv = (int)$__bkRow[$__bk];
                                // [FIX-DAILY-ZERO] Allow digit 0 for daily games (Pick3/4/5 use 0 as a valid digit).
                                if ($__isDailyPred || $__bv !== 0) { $__bkMain[] = $__bv; }
                            }
                        }
                        // Read normalized extra aliases only when this game expects extras.
                        $__bkFieldsNorm = getDrawFields($g['game_id']);
                        if ((int)($__bkFieldsNorm['num_extra_expected'] ?? 0) > 0) {
                            for ($__bei = 0; $__bei < 10; $__bei++) {
                                $__bek = $__bei === 0 ? 'extra_ball' : 'extra_ball_' . ($__bei + 1);
                                if (isset($__bkRow[$__bek]) && $__bkRow[$__bek] !== '' && $__bkRow[$__bek] !== null) {
                                    $__bv = (int)$__bkRow[$__bek];
                                    if ($__isDailyPred || $__bv !== 0) { $__bkExtra[] = $__bv; }
                                } else {
                                    break;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    } else {
                        // Raw row: use config column names (same as per-card fallback)
                        $__bkFields = getDrawFields($g['game_id']);
                        foreach (($__bkFields['main'] ?? array()) as $__bc) {
                            if (isset($__bkRow[$__bc]) && $__bkRow[$__bc] !== '') { $__bkMain[] = (int)$__bkRow[$__bc]; }
                        }
                        // Read all configured extra columns (supports extra_ball_columns array)
                        foreach (($__bkFields['extras'] ?? array_values(array_filter([$__bkFields['extra'] ?? null, $__bkFields['extra2'] ?? null]))) as $__bec) {
                            if (!empty($__bec) && isset($__bkRow[$__bec]) && $__bkRow[$__bec] !== '') {
                                $__bkExtra[] = (int)$__bkRow[$__bec];
                            }
                        }
                        // Final fallback / supplementation via generic extractor when configured
                        // columns gave nothing OR when daily sibling-F extras are still missing.
                        if (empty($__bkMain) || empty($__bkExtra)) {
                            $__bkExtracted = mylottoexpertExtractDrawNumbersFromRow($g['game_id'], $__bkRow);
                            if (empty($__bkMain)) { $__bkMain = $__bkExtracted['main']; }
                            if (empty($__bkExtra)) { $__bkExtra = $__bkExtracted['extra']; }
                        }
                    }
                }
                $__bkFinalFields = getDrawFields($g['game_id']);
                if ((int)($__bkFinalFields['num_extra_expected'] ?? 0) === 0) {
                    $__bkExtra = array();
                }
                $__bkCanonical = mylottoexpertCanonicalizeResolvedDrawParts($g['game_id'], (array)$__bkRow, $__bkMain, $__bkExtra);
                $__drawCache[$__bkKey] = array('main' => $__bkCanonical['main'], 'extra' => $__bkCanonical['extra']);
            }
            $__bkDraw = $__drawCache[$__bkKey];
            if (!empty($__bkDraw['main'])) {
                $__hm = 0; $__he = 0;
                foreach ($predMain as $__pn) {
                    // For regular lotteries skip 0 (not a valid ball; used as padding).
                    // For daily games 0 IS a valid digit (e.g. Pick-3 "012" -> [0,1,2]).
                    if (!$__isDailyPred && !$__pn) { continue; }
                    if (in_array((int)$__pn, $__bkDraw['main'], true)) { $__hm++; }
                }
                // [FIX-DAILY-EXTRA-ZERO] Daily bonus / extra digits can legitimately be 0.
                if ($predExtra !== null && $predExtra !== '' && !empty($__bkDraw['extra']) && in_array((int)$predExtra, $__bkDraw['extra'], true)) $__he = 1;
                $__scored = array(
                    'has_draw'   => true,
                    'hits_main'  => $__hm,
                    'hits_extra' => $__he,
                    'drawMain'   => $__bkDraw['main'],
                    'drawExtra'  => $__bkDraw['extra'],
                );
            }
        }

        if (!$__scored['has_draw']) {
            continue; // draw not yet available; skip this run
        }

        $mainHitCount  = (int)$__scored['hits_main'];
        $extraHitCount = (int)$__scored['hits_extra'];
        $actualMain    = $__scored['drawMain'];
        $actualExtra   = $__scored['drawExtra'];

        // Position sum for tie-breaking
        $posSum = 0;
        foreach ($predMain as $pos0 => $n) {
            if (in_array($n, $actualMain, true)) {
                $posSum += ($pos0 + 1);
            }
        }
        $rankScore = ($mainHitCount * 10000) - $posSum + ($extraHitCount * 1000);

        $bestOpps[$lid]['all_scored_runs'][] = array(
            'run_id'       => (int)$s->id,
            'game_id'      => (string)$g['game_id'],
            'draw_date'    => (string)$g['draw_date'],
            'source'       => (string)$s->source,
            'hits'         => $mainHitCount,
            'extra_hits'   => $extraHitCount,
            'rank_score'   => $rankScore,
            'pred_main'    => $predMain,
            'pred_extra'   => $predExtra,
            'actual_main'  => $actualMain,
            'actual_extra' => $actualExtra,
            'has_draw'     => true,
        );
    }
}

// Post-process: sort scored runs and promote #1 to best_rank
foreach ($bestOpps as $lid => &$oppRef) {
    if (!empty($oppRef['all_scored_runs'])) {
        usort($oppRef['all_scored_runs'], $__rankCompare);
        $oppWinner = $oppRef['all_scored_runs'][0];
        if (!empty($oppWinner['has_draw'])) {
            $oppRef['best_rank'] = array(
                'score'        => (int)$oppWinner['rank_score'],
                'draw_date'    => (string)$oppWinner['draw_date'],
                'run_id'       => (int)$oppWinner['run_id'],
                'source'       => (string)$oppWinner['source'],
                'hits'         => (int)$oppWinner['hits'],
                'extra_hits'   => (int)$oppWinner['extra_hits'],
                'numbers'      => (array)$oppWinner['pred_main'],
                'extra_number' => (int)$oppWinner['pred_extra'],
                'has_draw'     => true,
            );
        }
    }
}
unset($oppRef);

// Build a run_id => row lookup from the already-loaded $savedSets.
// Used as fallback in best_avg_hits display-name resolution below.
$__savedSetsById = array();
foreach ($savedSets as $__s) {
    if (!empty($__s->id)) { $__savedSetsById[(int)$__s->id] = (array)$__s; }
}

// Collect winner run IDs for display-name lookup (single query, not per-run)
$__winnerRunIds = array();
foreach ($bestOpps as $__lid => $__opp) {
    $__rid = (int)($__opp['best_rank']['run_id'] ?? 0);
    if ($__rid > 0) { $__winnerRunIds[] = $__rid; }
}
$__winnerRows = array();
if (!empty($__winnerRunIds)) {
    $__wq = $db->getQuery(true)
        ->select('*')
        ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_numbers'))
        ->where($db->quoteName('id')      . ' IN (' . implode(',', array_map('intval', $__winnerRunIds)) . ')')
        ->where($db->quoteName('user_id') . ' = ' . $workspaceUserId);
    $db->setQuery($__wq);
    foreach (($db->loadAssocList() ?: array()) as $__wr) {
        $__winnerRows[(int)$__wr['id']] = $__wr;
    }
}

// Compute best-max-hits per lottery (for snapshot cards)
foreach ($bestOpps as $__bavLid => &$__bavOpp) {
    $__bavRuns = $__bavOpp['all_scored_runs'] ?? array();
    if (empty($__bavRuns)) {
        $__bavOpp['best_avg_hits'] = array('run_id' => 0, 'max_hits' => 0, 'scored_runs' => 0, 'last_scored_date' => '', 'display_name' => 'No scored runs yet');
        continue;
    }
    $__bavByRun = array();
    foreach ($__bavRuns as $__bavR) {
        $__rid2 = (int)$__bavR['run_id'];
        if (!isset($__bavByRun[$__rid2])) {
            $__bavByRun[$__rid2] = array('run_id' => $__rid2, 'source' => (string)$__bavR['source'], 'total' => 0, 'count' => 0, 'max' => 0, 'lastdate' => '');
        }
        $__bavByRun[$__rid2]['total'] += (int)$__bavR['hits'];
        $__bavByRun[$__rid2]['count']++;
        $__hits = (int)$__bavR['hits'];
        if ($__hits > $__bavByRun[$__rid2]['max']) { $__bavByRun[$__rid2]['max'] = $__hits; }
        $__d = (string)$__bavR['draw_date'];
        if ($__d !== '' && $__d > $__bavByRun[$__rid2]['lastdate']) {
            $__bavByRun[$__rid2]['lastdate'] = $__d;
        }
    }
    $__bavBest = null;
    foreach ($__bavByRun as $__bavEntry) {
        if ($__bavBest === null) {
            $__bavBest = $__bavEntry;
        } else {
            $isBetter2 = ($__bavEntry['max'] > $__bavBest['max'])
                || ($__bavEntry['max'] === $__bavBest['max'] && $__bavEntry['total'] > $__bavBest['total'])
                || ($__bavEntry['max'] === $__bavBest['max'] && $__bavEntry['total'] === $__bavBest['total'] && $__bavEntry['run_id'] > $__bavBest['run_id']);
            if ($isBetter2) {
                $__bavBest = $__bavEntry;
            }
        }
    }
    $__bavTotalScored = array_sum(array_column($__bavByRun, 'count'));
    $__bavSrc   = (string)($__bavBest['source'] ?? '');
    $__bavLabel = $__methodLabels[$__bavSrc] ?? ucwords(str_replace('_', ' ', $__bavSrc));
    // Use the DB-fetched row if available; fall back to the already-loaded savedSets row.
    // $__winnerRows only contains best_rank run IDs, which may differ from $__bavBest's run ID.
    $__bavRunId2    = (int)$__bavBest['run_id'];
    $__bavWinnerRow = isset($__winnerRows[$__bavRunId2])
        ? $__winnerRows[$__bavRunId2]
        : (isset($__savedSetsById[$__bavRunId2]) ? $__savedSetsById[$__bavRunId2] : null);
    $__bavDisplayName = ($__bavWinnerRow !== null)
        ? mylottoexpertBuildBestSettingsSummary((array)$__bavWinnerRow, $__methodLabels)
        : $__bavLabel;
    $__bavWinnerDisp = ($__bavWinnerRow !== null)
        ? mylottoexpertResolveRunDisplayInfo((array)$__bavWinnerRow, $__methodLabels)
        : array('mode' => '');
    $__bavOpp['best_avg_hits'] = array(
        'run_id'           => (int)$__bavBest['run_id'],
        'max_hits'         => (int)$__bavBest['max'],
        'scored_runs'      => $__bavTotalScored,
        'last_scored_date' => (string)($__bavBest['lastdate'] ?? ''),
        'display_name'     => $__bavDisplayName,
        'run_mode'         => (string)($__bavWinnerDisp['mode'] ?? ''),
    );
}
unset($__bavOpp);

// ------------------------------------------------------------------
// 7) Build per-lottery prediction-results summary for the comparison table.
//    Groups ALL saved runs (scored + unscored) across all draw dates.
//
//    Draw data: uses the preloaded $drawMap (built by the UNION ALL query)
//    as the primary source -- same data used by $bestOpps / scoreRunFromDrawMap.
//    Falls back to a direct getDrawByDate() DB call when $drawMap has no
//    entry for a game+date (e.g. if the UNION ALL failed or returned no row).
// ------------------------------------------------------------------

// Quick lookup: run_id -> display name info (source, mode, label)
$__runDispInfo = array();
foreach ($savedSets as $__s) {
    $__rid = (int)$__s->id;
    $__runDispInfo[$__rid] = mylottoexpertResolveRunDisplayInfo($__s, $__methodLabels);
}

// Draw cache keyed by canonical target identity: game_id|date|draw_at|draw_session.
// Falls back to game_id|date for legacy rows.
$__prcDrawCache = array();

// Group all runs per lottery_id
$__runSummary = array();
foreach ($groups as $__gKey => $__g) {
    $__lid = (int)$__g['lottery_id'];
    if (!isset($__runSummary[$__lid])) {
        $__runSummary[$__lid] = array(
            'lottery_name' => (string)($__g['lottery_name'] ?? ''),
            'state_name'   => (string)($lottoMetaById[$__lid]['state'] ?? ''),
            'country_name' => (string)($lottoMetaById[$__lid]['country'] ?? ''),
            'game_id'      => (string)($__g['game_id'] ?? ''),
            'runs'         => array(),
            'max_hits'     => 0,
            'best_run_id'  => 0,
            'best_pos_sum' => PHP_INT_MAX,
        );
    }
    // Normalise canonical target fields for the cache key.
    $__gDateTs       = strtotime((string)($__g['draw_date'] ?? ''));
    $__gDateNorm     = $__gDateTs ? date('Y-m-d', $__gDateTs) : (string)($__g['draw_date'] ?? '');
    $__gTargetAt     = trim((string)($__g['target_draw_at'] ?? ''));
    $__gTargetSession= mylottoexpertNormalizeTargetSession($__g['target_draw_session'] ?? '');
    $__fbCacheKey    = $__g['game_id'] . '|' . $__gDateNorm . '|' . ($__gTargetAt !== '' ? $__gTargetAt : 'no-time') . '|' . ($__gTargetSession !== '' ? $__gTargetSession : 'no-session');
    // [FIX-SKY-DAILY-LOOKUP] drawMap keys are always lowercase (see strtolower() when building
    // the map). Lowercasing here ensures the legacy lookup matches for any game_id case.
    $__drawMapLegacyKey = strtolower((string)($__g['game_id'] ?? '')) . '|' . $__gDateNorm;
    $__preferCanonicalDrawLookup = ($__gTargetAt !== '' || $__gTargetSession !== '');

    // -- Fetch draw for this canonical target (cached per game+date+time/session) --
    // Primary legacy path: use the preloaded $drawMap when no session/time disambiguation is needed.
    // Canonical path: call getDrawByDate() with draw_session / draw_at so daily sessions cannot collide.
    if (!array_key_exists($__fbCacheKey, $__prcDrawCache)) {
        $__grpMain  = array();
        $__grpExtra = array();
        $__diagRawRow = null;
        $__diagRawSource = '';
        $__diagDrawMapHit = (!$__preferCanonicalDrawLookup && !empty($drawMap) && isset($drawMap[$__drawMapLegacyKey]));
        $__diagSpec = mylottoexpertLoadLotterySpec($__g['game_id']);
        $__diagDbCol = (string)($__diagSpec['dbCol'] ?? '');
        $__diagFields = getDrawFields($__g['game_id']);
        // [FIX-DAILY-FLAG] Initialize the daily flag from the group-level canonical target
        // metadata FIRST, before probing individual prediction rows. A prediction that was
        // saved with target_prediction_family='daily' (set by SKAI at save time) must always
        // be treated as a daily game for draw extraction purposes, regardless of whether
        // structured daily JSON fields (daily_top_picks_json etc.) are present. This ensures:
        //   1. Digit 0 is allowed in draw number extraction (valid Pick3/4/5 digit).
        //   2. The daily raw-row fallback (getDrawByDate on empty drawMap result) runs.
        // Without this, a daily prediction lacking combo_strings would leave $__groupHasDaily
        // false, silently exclude the 0 digit, and leave has_draw=false even when the draw occurred.
        $__groupHasDaily = (strtolower(trim((string)($__g['target_prediction_family'] ?? ''))) === 'daily');
        if (!$__groupHasDaily) {
            $__tpt = strtolower(trim((string)($__g['target_prediction_type'] ?? '')));
            if ($__tpt === 'pick3' || $__tpt === 'pick4' || $__tpt === 'pick5' || $__tpt === 'daily') {
                $__groupHasDaily = true;
            }
        }
        // Probe predictions to detect daily games AND determine how many extra balls are expected.
        // For EuroMillions the extra_ball_numbers field stores both Lucky Stars (e.g. "3,7"),
        // so the prediction count tells us the game has 2 extras even when config only lists 1 column.
        $__expectedExtraCount = (int)($tableInfo[$__g['game_id']]['num_extra_expected'] ?? 0);
        foreach (($__g['preds'] ?? array()) as $__predProbe) {
            if (!$__groupHasDaily) {
                $__dailyProbe = mylottoexpertExtractDailySavedView($__predProbe);
                // [FIX-DAILY-FLAG] Use is_daily alone (not requiring combo_strings) so that
                // predictions flagged daily via prediction_family but lacking structured JSON
                // fields still correctly set the daily gate.
                if (!empty($__dailyProbe['is_daily'])) {
                    $__groupHasDaily = true;
                }
            }
            // Count extra balls stored in this prediction to determine the game's expected extras.
            if (!empty($__predProbe->extra_ball_numbers)) {
                $__prExVals = array_values(array_filter(array_map('intval', explode(',', (string)$__predProbe->extra_ball_numbers))));
                if (count($__prExVals) > $__expectedExtraCount) {
                    $__expectedExtraCount = count($__prExVals);
                }
            }
            if (property_exists($__predProbe, 'regular_extra_numbers_json') && !empty($__predProbe->regular_extra_numbers_json)) {
                $__prExJson = json_decode((string)$__predProbe->regular_extra_numbers_json, true);
                if (is_array($__prExJson) && count($__prExJson) > $__expectedExtraCount) {
                    $__expectedExtraCount = count($__prExJson);
                }
            }
            if ($__expectedExtraCount >= 5) { break; } // 5 extras is well above any real lottery; stop probing early
        }
        // Also check config for EuroMillions even when no predictions carry both Lucky Stars yet.
        if (mylottoexpertIsEuroMillionsLottery('', (string)($__g['lottery_name'] ?? '')) && $__expectedExtraCount < 2) {
            $__expectedExtraCount = 2;
        }
        // [FIX-DAILY-EXTRA-COUNT] For daily lotteries, the catalog / config is the source of
        // truth for how many actual extras are drawn. Do not inflate this from saved prediction
        // candidate values (e.g. multiple suggested FB digits) because that causes Florida-style
        // FB games to expect 3 extras instead of the single real extra.
        if ($__groupHasDaily) {
            $__expectedExtraCount = (int)($tableInfo[$__g['game_id']]['num_extra_expected'] ?? $__expectedExtraCount);
        }
        // For games that the config declares as having no extra balls, do not allow
        // saved prediction data to inflate $__expectedExtraCount above zero. Without
        // this guard, a prediction that accidentally stores extra_ball_numbers triggers
        // the supplemental raw-row scan, which can pick up non-ball columns (such as
        // the last main ball column or a jackpot field) as a false extra.
        if ((int)($tableInfo[$__g['game_id']]['num_extra_expected'] ?? 0) === 0) {
            $__expectedExtraCount = 0;
        }

        if (!$__preferCanonicalDrawLookup && !empty($drawMap) && isset($drawMap[$__drawMapLegacyKey])) {
            // Use preloaded, normalized row (same source as $bestOpps / scoreRunFromDrawMap)
            $__dmRow = $drawMap[$__drawMapLegacyKey];
            for ($__i = 0; $__i < 25; $__i++) {
                $__mk = 'main_' . $__i;
                if (isset($__dmRow[$__mk]) && $__dmRow[$__mk] !== '' && $__dmRow[$__mk] !== null) {
                    $__gv = (int)$__dmRow[$__mk];
                    if ($__groupHasDaily || $__gv !== 0) { $__grpMain[] = $__gv; }
                }
            }
            // Read normalized extra aliases only when this game expects extras.
            if ((int)$__expectedExtraCount > 0) {
                for ($__ei = 0; $__ei < 10; $__ei++) {
                    $__eKey = $__ei === 0 ? 'extra_ball' : 'extra_ball_' . ($__ei + 1);
                    if (isset($__dmRow[$__eKey]) && $__dmRow[$__eKey] !== '' && $__dmRow[$__eKey] !== null) {
                        $__gv = (int)$__dmRow[$__eKey];
                        if ($__groupHasDaily || $__gv !== 0) { $__grpExtra[] = $__gv; }
                    } else {
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            // Fallback / supplementation via generic extractor when the normalized drawMap
            // row lacks raw config mappings. This now runs when EITHER main digits OR extras are
            // still missing so sibling-F daily extras (e.g. FLD -> FLDF) can be resolved too.
            if (empty($__grpMain) || (int)$__expectedExtraCount > 0 && empty($__grpExtra)) {
                $__dmExtracted = mylottoexpertExtractDrawNumbersFromRow($__g['game_id'], $__dmRow);
                if (empty($__grpMain)) {
                    foreach ($__dmExtracted['main'] as $__gv) { if ($__groupHasDaily || $__gv !== 0) { $__grpMain[] = $__gv; } }
                }
                if (empty($__grpExtra)) {
                    foreach ($__dmExtracted['extra'] as $__gv) { if ($__groupHasDaily || $__gv !== 0) { $__grpExtra[] = $__gv; } }
                }
                // -- Daily-game raw-row fallback -----------------------------------------------------
                // Daily games (Pick 3/4/5, etc.) have no main_ball_columns configured.
                // The UNION ALL emits all-NULL main aliases, and the normalized drawMap row
                // has no original digit columns (only main_0..main_N which are all NULL).
                // When the game is detected as daily AND $__grpMain is still empty, fetch
                // the full raw DB row via getDrawByDate() so the defensive numeric-scan in
                // mylottoexpertExtractDrawNumbersFromRow() can locate the actual digit columns.
                if ($__groupHasDaily && empty($__grpMain)) {
                    $__dailyRaw = getDrawByDate($__g['game_id'], (string)($__g['draw_date'] ?? ''), $db, ($__g['target_draw_session'] ?? null), ($__g['target_draw_at'] ?? null));
                    if (is_array($__dailyRaw) && !empty($__dailyRaw)) {
                        $__diagRawRow = $__dailyRaw;
                        $__diagRawSource = 'daily_raw_fallback';
                        $__dailyExt = mylottoexpertExtractDrawNumbersFromRow($__g['game_id'], $__dailyRaw);
                        // Include zero-valued digits (0 is a valid Pick3/4 digit)
                        foreach ($__dailyExt['main']  as $__gv) { $__grpMain[]  = $__gv; }
                        foreach ($__dailyExt['extra'] as $__gv) { $__grpExtra[] = $__gv; }
                    }
                }
            }
        } else {
            // Fallback: direct DB query with config-defined column names.
            // No (int) cast on game_id  -  matches working sections (Placement Heatmap line 3176, stats block line 3287).
            $__grpFields  = getDrawFields($__g['game_id']);
            $__grpDrawRow = getDrawByDate($__g['game_id'], (string)($__g['draw_date'] ?? ''), $db, ($__g['target_draw_session'] ?? null), ($__g['target_draw_at'] ?? null));
            if ($__grpDrawRow) {
                $__diagRawRow = $__grpDrawRow;
                $__diagRawSource = 'direct_db';
                // Read main ball columns by their config-defined names
                foreach (($__grpFields['main'] ?? array()) as $__gc) {
                    if (isset($__grpDrawRow[$__gc]) && $__grpDrawRow[$__gc] !== '' && $__grpDrawRow[$__gc] !== null) {
                        $__gv = (int)$__grpDrawRow[$__gc];
                        if ($__groupHasDaily || $__gv !== 0) { $__grpMain[] = $__gv; }
                    }
                }
                // Read all configured extra ball columns (extra_ball_columns array, or extra_ball_column + extra_ball_column_2)
                foreach (($__grpFields['extras'] ?? array_values(array_filter([$__grpFields['extra'] ?? null, $__grpFields['extra2'] ?? null]))) as $__ec) {
                    if (empty($__ec)) { continue; }
                    if (isset($__grpDrawRow[$__ec]) && $__grpDrawRow[$__ec] !== '' && $__grpDrawRow[$__ec] !== null) {
                        $__gv = (int)$__grpDrawRow[$__ec];
                        if ($__groupHasDaily || $__gv !== 0) { $__grpExtra[] = $__gv; }
                    }
                }
                // Final fallback / supplementation via generic extractor. This now also
                // fills missing extras even when main columns were already resolved, which is
                // required for daily sibling-F bonus sources such as FLD -> FLDF.
                if (empty($__grpMain) || ((int)$__expectedExtraCount > 0 && empty($__grpExtra))) {
                    $__fbExtracted = mylottoexpertExtractDrawNumbersFromRow($__g['game_id'], $__grpDrawRow);
                    if (empty($__grpMain)) {
                        foreach ($__fbExtracted['main'] as $__gv) { if ($__groupHasDaily || $__gv !== 0) { $__grpMain[] = $__gv; } }
                    }
                    if (empty($__grpExtra)) {
                        foreach ($__fbExtracted['extra'] as $__gv) { if ($__groupHasDaily || $__gv !== 0) { $__grpExtra[] = $__gv; } }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        // -- Supplemental raw-row scan ------------------------------------------------------------
        // When the game expects extra balls but we still have fewer than expected, do a targeted
        // raw-row scan for the missing values. This is especially important for daily lotteries,
        // where the config may declare extraBallCount but not name the raw DB extra column.
        if ($__expectedExtraCount > 0 && count($__grpExtra) < $__expectedExtraCount && !empty($__grpMain)) {
            $__suppRawRow = getDrawByDate($__g['game_id'], (string)($__g['draw_date'] ?? ''), $db, ($__g['target_draw_session'] ?? null), ($__g['target_draw_at'] ?? null));
            if (is_array($__suppRawRow)) {
                if ($__diagRawRow === null || empty($__diagRawRow)) {
                    $__diagRawRow = $__suppRawRow;
                    $__diagRawSource = 'supplemental_extra_scan';
                }
                $__suppFields  = getDrawFields($__g['game_id']);
                $__suppMainSet = array_flip($__suppFields['main'] ?? array());
                // Skip columns we already read via configured extras
                $__suppConfigured = array_values(array_filter($__suppFields['extras'] ?? [
                    $__suppFields['extra']  ?? null,
                    $__suppFields['extra2'] ?? null,
                ]));
                $__suppMeta = array('id','asset_id','state','ordering','checked_out','checked_out_time',
                    'created_by','modified_by','country','stateprov_name','stateprov_id',
                    'game_id','game_name','draw_date','next_draw_date','next_jackpot','req_date','draw_results');

                // Prefer common bonus/extra aliases first before falling back to a generic scan.
                $__suppAliasCandidates = array(
                    'extra_ball','extra_ball_2','bonus_ball','bonus','fireball','wildball','wild_ball',
                    'fb','wb','extra','extra1','extra_1','ball_extra','bonus_number'
                );
                foreach ($__suppAliasCandidates as $__aliasKey) {
                    if (count($__grpExtra) >= $__expectedExtraCount) { break; }
                    if (!array_key_exists($__aliasKey, $__suppRawRow)) { continue; }
                    $__sv = $__suppRawRow[$__aliasKey];
                    if ($__sv === '' || $__sv === null || !preg_match('/^\d+$/', (string)$__sv)) { continue; }
                    $__gv = (int)$__sv;
                    if (($__groupHasDaily || $__gv > 0) && !in_array($__gv, $__grpExtra, true)) {
                        $__grpExtra[] = $__gv;
                    }
                }

                foreach ($__suppRawRow as $__sk => $__sv) {
                    if (count($__grpExtra) >= $__expectedExtraCount) { break; }
                    if (in_array($__sk, $__suppMeta, true)) { continue; }
                    if (isset($__suppMainSet[$__sk])) { continue; }
                    if (in_array($__sk, $__suppConfigured, true)) { continue; }
                    if ($__sv === '' || $__sv === null || !preg_match('/^\d+$/', (string)$__sv)) { continue; }
                    $__gv = (int)$__sv;
                    // For regular lotteries, reject values outside the range 1-99. Extra balls
                    // for all known regular lotteries fall within this range (e.g. Mega Ball
                    // 1-25, Powerball 1-26, Lucky Star 1-12). Jackpot amounts are in the
                    // millions and are safely excluded by this upper bound.
                    if (!$__groupHasDaily && ($__gv < 1 || $__gv > 99)) { continue; }
                    if (($__groupHasDaily || $__gv > 0) && !in_array($__gv, $__grpExtra, true)) {
                        $__grpExtra[] = $__gv;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        // Final guard: if the game config declares 0 extra balls, discard any extras
        // that any extraction path may have placed into $__grpExtra. This is the last
        // line of defence to prevent a false extra reaching the display or scoring.
        if ((int)($tableInfo[$__g['game_id']]['num_extra_expected'] ?? 0) === 0) {
            $__grpExtra = array();
        }

        $__diagRawKeys = is_array($__diagRawRow) ? array_keys($__diagRawRow) : array();
        $__diagNumericPreview = array();
        $__diagExtraAliases = array();
        if (is_array($__diagRawRow)) {
            foreach ($__diagRawRow as $__dpk => $__dpv) {
                if ($__dpv === '' || $__dpv === null) { continue; }
                if (preg_match('/^\d+$/', (string)$__dpv)) {
                    $__diagNumericPreview[$__dpk] = (string)$__dpv;
                }
                if (count($__diagNumericPreview) >= 12) { break; }
            }
            foreach (array('extra_ball','extra_ball_2','bonus_ball','bonus_ball_2','bonus','bonus2','bonus_number','bonus_num','fireball','fire_ball','wildball','wild_ball','wild','fb','wb','extra','extra1','extra_1','extra2','extra_2','ball_extra') as $__diagAliasKey) {
                if (array_key_exists($__diagAliasKey, $__diagRawRow)) {
                    $__diagAliasVal = $__diagRawRow[$__diagAliasKey];
                    if ($__diagAliasVal !== '' && $__diagAliasVal !== null) {
                        $__diagExtraAliases[$__diagAliasKey] = (string)$__diagAliasVal;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        $__grpCanonical = mylottoexpertCanonicalizeResolvedDrawParts((string)($__g['game_id'] ?? ''), is_array($__diagRawRow) ? $__diagRawRow : array(), $__grpMain, $__grpExtra);
        $__grpMain = $__grpCanonical['main'];
        $__grpExtra = $__grpCanonical['extra'];

        $__prcDrawCache[$__fbCacheKey] = array(
            'has_draw'  => (count($__grpMain) > 0),
            'drawMain'  => $__grpMain,
            'drawExtra' => $__grpExtra,
            'diag'      => array(
                'game_id'                  => (string)($__g['game_id'] ?? ''),
                'target_game_id'           => (string)($__g['target_game_id'] ?? ''),
                'draw_date'                => (string)($__g['draw_date'] ?? ''),
                'target_draw_session'      => (string)($__g['target_draw_session'] ?? ''),
                'target_draw_at'           => (string)($__g['target_draw_at'] ?? ''),
                'target_prediction_family' => (string)($__g['target_prediction_family'] ?? ''),
                'target_prediction_type'   => (string)($__g['target_prediction_type'] ?? ''),
                'db_table'                 => $__diagDbCol,
                'expected_extra_count'     => (int)$__expectedExtraCount,
                'drawmap_hit'              => $__diagDrawMapHit ? 1 : 0,
                'raw_row_found'            => (is_array($__diagRawRow) && !empty($__diagRawRow)) ? 1 : 0,
                'raw_source'               => $__diagRawSource,
                'configured_main'          => array_values((array)($__diagFields['main'] ?? array())),
                'configured_extras'        => array_values((array)($__diagFields['extras'] ?? array())),
                'raw_keys'                 => $__diagRawKeys,
                'numeric_preview'          => $__diagNumericPreview,
                'raw_extra_aliases'        => $__diagExtraAliases,
                'extracted_draw_extra'     => array_values($__grpExtra),
            ),
        );
    }
    $__grpDraw = $__prcDrawCache[$__fbCacheKey];

    foreach ($__g['preds'] as $__pred) {
        $__rid = (int)$__pred->id;

        // Parse predicted numbers.
        // Daily lotteries use daily_top_picks_json as the sole display/source-of-truth combo list.
        // Regular lotteries continue to use main_numbers / extra_ball_numbers.
        $__dailyViewPr = mylottoexpertExtractDailySavedView($__pred);
        $__isDailyPr   = !empty($__dailyViewPr['is_daily']) && !empty($__dailyViewPr['combo_strings']);

        $__dailyBestComboString = '';
        $__dailyBestComboDigits = array();

        if ($__isDailyPr) {
            $__predNums = !empty($__dailyViewPr['primary_combo_digits'])
                ? array_values($__dailyViewPr['primary_combo_digits'])
                : mylottoexpertDigitStringToArray((string)$__dailyViewPr['combo_strings'][0]);

            $__predExtraAll = !empty($__dailyViewPr['extra_digits'])
                ? array_values(array_map('intval', $__dailyViewPr['extra_digits']))
                : array();

            $__predExtra = !empty($__predExtraAll) ? (int)$__predExtraAll[0] : 0;

            $__predComboStrings = array_values($__dailyViewPr['combo_strings']);
            $__dailyBestComboString = !empty($__predComboStrings) ? (string)$__predComboStrings[0] : '';
            $__dailyBestComboDigits = !empty($__predNums) ? array_values($__predNums) : array();
        } else {
            $__predNums = array_values(array_filter(
                array_map('intval', explode(',', (string)($__pred->main_numbers ?? ''))),
                function ($n) { return $n !== 0; }
            ));

            $__predExtra = 0;
            $__predExtraAll = array();
            if (!empty($__pred->extra_ball_numbers)) {
                $__predExtraVals = array_values(array_filter(array_map('intval', explode(',', (string)$__pred->extra_ball_numbers))));
                if (!empty($__predExtraVals)) {
                    $__predExtra    = (int)$__predExtraVals[0];
                    $__predExtraAll = $__predExtraVals;
                }
            }

            $__predComboStrings = array();
        }

        // -- Score against the direct-DB draw (the sole source for this section) --
        $__scored = null;
        if ($__grpDraw['has_draw']) {
            $__fbMainHits  = 0;
            if ($__isDailyPr && !empty($__predComboStrings) && !empty($__grpDraw['drawMain'])) {
                $__drawComboDigits = array_values(array_map('intval', $__grpDraw['drawMain']));
                $__bestHits = -1;
                $__bestPosSumLocal = PHP_INT_MAX;
                foreach ($__predComboStrings as $__comboCandidate) {
                    $__comboCandidate = (string)$__comboCandidate;
                    $__comboDigits = mylottoexpertDigitStringToArray($__comboCandidate);

                    // [FIX-DAILY-HIT-COUNT] Daily PRC hit totals should reflect digit overlap, not
                    // exact same-position matches. Users expect a drawn digit like 7 to count as a
                    // hit even when it lands in a different slot. Preserve duplicate digits by
                    // consuming matched draw digits one time each, then use position matches only as
                    // the tie-break for choosing the best saved combo to display.
                    $__candidateHits = 0;
                    $__candidatePosSum = 0;
                    $__remainingDrawDigits = $__drawComboDigits;
                    foreach ($__comboDigits as $__ci => $__cd) {
                        $__matchIdx = array_search((int)$__cd, $__remainingDrawDigits, true);
                        if ($__matchIdx !== false) {
                            $__candidateHits++;
                            unset($__remainingDrawDigits[$__matchIdx]);
                        }
                        if (isset($__drawComboDigits[$__ci]) && (string)$__cd === (string)$__drawComboDigits[$__ci]) {
                            $__candidatePosSum += ($__ci + 1);
                        }
                    }

                    if ($__candidateHits > $__bestHits || ($__candidateHits === $__bestHits && $__candidatePosSum < $__bestPosSumLocal)) {
                        $__bestHits = $__candidateHits;
                        $__bestPosSumLocal = $__candidatePosSum;
                        $__dailyBestComboString = $__comboCandidate;
                        $__dailyBestComboDigits = $__comboDigits;
                    }
                }
                if (!empty($__dailyBestComboDigits)) {
                    $__predNums = array_values($__dailyBestComboDigits);
                }
                $__fbMainHits = max(0, (int)$__bestHits);
            } else {
                foreach ($__predNums as $__fn) {
                    if ($__fn !== 0 && in_array($__fn, $__grpDraw['drawMain'], true)) { $__fbMainHits++; }
                }
            }
            $__fbExtraHits = 0;
            if (!empty($__predExtraAll) && !empty($__grpDraw['drawExtra'])) {
                foreach ($__predExtraAll as $__pev) {
                    if ($__pev > 0 && in_array($__pev, $__grpDraw['drawExtra'], true)) {
                        $__fbExtraHits = 1;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            $__scored = array(
                'run_id'       => $__rid,
                'hits'         => $__fbMainHits,
                'extra_hits'   => $__fbExtraHits,
                'actual_main'  => $__grpDraw['drawMain'],
                'actual_extra' => $__grpDraw['drawExtra'],
            );
        }

        $__mainHits    = ($__scored !== null) ? (int)$__scored['hits']       : null;
        $__extraHits   = ($__scored !== null) ? (int)$__scored['extra_hits'] : null;
        $__actualMain  = ($__scored !== null) ? ($__scored['actual_main']  ?? array()) : array();
        $__actualExtra = ($__scored !== null) ? ($__scored['actual_extra'] ?? array()) : array();
        $__totalHits = (int)($__mainHits ?? 0) + (int)($__extraHits ?? 0);
        // pos_sum: sum of 1-based positions of hitting numbers in pred_main.
        // Lower = matched numbers appeared earlier in the ranked prediction list (more likely).
        $__posSum = 0;
        if ($__scored !== null && !empty($__grpDraw['drawMain']) && !empty($__predNums)) {
            $__hitLookup = array_flip($__grpDraw['drawMain']);
            foreach ($__predNums as $__pi => $__pn) {
                if (isset($__hitLookup[$__pn])) { $__posSum += ($__pi + 1); }
            }
        }
        // Update best run using the shared 7-tier comparator.
        // Build a minimal run array for the comparator before the full row is appended.
        $__candidateRun = array(
            'run_id'             => $__rid,
            'draw_date'          => (string)($__g['draw_date'] ?? ''),
            'has_draw'           => ($__scored !== null),
            'hits_main'          => $__mainHits,
            'hits_extra'         => $__extraHits,
            'is_daily'           => $__isDailyPr,
            'pred_combo_strings' => $__predComboStrings,
            'pred_extra_all'     => $__predExtraAll,
            'actual_main'        => $__actualMain,
            'actual_extra'       => $__actualExtra,
            'pos_sum'            => $__posSum,
        );
        $__curBestRid = $__runSummary[$__lid]['best_run_id'];
        if ($__curBestRid === 0) {
            // First run for this lottery
            $__runSummary[$__lid]['max_hits']     = $__totalHits;
            $__runSummary[$__lid]['best_run_id']  = $__rid;
            $__runSummary[$__lid]['best_pos_sum'] = $__posSum;
        } else {
            // Find current best row in the runs array to compare
            $__curBestRow = null;
            foreach ($__runSummary[$__lid]['runs'] as $__existingRun) {
                if ((int)$__existingRun['run_id'] === $__curBestRid) {
                    $__curBestRow = $__existingRun;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if ($__curBestRow !== null
                && mylottoexpertCompareCompletedRuns($__candidateRun, $__curBestRow) < 0) {
                $__runSummary[$__lid]['max_hits']     = $__totalHits;
                $__runSummary[$__lid]['best_run_id']  = $__rid;
                $__runSummary[$__lid]['best_pos_sum'] = $__posSum;
            }
        }
        $__runSummary[$__lid]['runs'][] = array(
            'run_id'         => $__rid,
            'draw_date'      => (string)($__g['draw_date'] ?? ''),
            'source'         => (string)$__pred->source,
            'pred_main'      => $__predNums,
            'pred_combo_strings' => $__predComboStrings,
            'daily_best_combo_string' => $__dailyBestComboString,
            'is_daily'       => $__isDailyPr,
            'pred_extra'     => $__predExtra,
            'pred_extra_all' => $__predExtraAll,
            'actual_main'    => $__actualMain,
            'actual_extra'   => $__actualExtra,
            'hits_main'      => $__mainHits,
            'hits_extra'     => $__extraHits,
            'has_draw'       => ($__scored !== null),
            'pos_sum'        => $__posSum,
            'disp'           => isset($__runDispInfo[$__rid]) ? $__runDispInfo[$__rid] : array('base_label'=>'','mode'=>'','label'=>'','source'=>$__pred->source),
            'diag'           => (array)($__grpDraw['diag'] ?? array()),
        );
    }
}

// Sort each lottery's runs using the shared 7-tier comparator:
// total hits -> main hits -> extra hits -> successful combo count ->
// combo quality score -> pos_sum -> run_id (newest last-resort tiebreak).
// Unscored rows are always placed below scored rows.
foreach ($__runSummary as $__lid => &$__lsRef) {
    usort($__lsRef['runs'], 'mylottoexpertCompareCompletedRuns');
}
unset($__lsRef);

// --------------------------------------------------------------
// SKAI Learning performance: calculate and persist metrics
// for every completed (has_draw = true) run in $__runSummary.
// This uses the pred_main (ranked list) and actual_main (drawn numbers)
// that were already computed above. No additional DB reads needed.
// --------------------------------------------------------------
foreach ($__runSummary as $__lpLid => $__lpLottery) {
    $__lpLotteryName = (string)($__lpLottery['lottery_name'] ?? '');
    foreach ($__lpLottery['runs'] as $__lpRun) {
        if (empty($__lpRun['has_draw'])) {
            continue; // skip runs without a validated draw
        }
        $__lpPredMain   = (array)($__lpRun['pred_main'] ?? array());
        $__lpActualMain = (array)($__lpRun['actual_main'] ?? array());
        if (empty($__lpActualMain)) {
            continue; // no actual draw data
        }

        $__lpMetrics = skaiCalcWinningRankMetrics($__lpPredMain, $__lpActualMain);

        // Extract learning module flags from saved settings (if available)
        $__lpRunId  = (int)($__lpRun['run_id'] ?? 0);
        $__lpSource = (string)($__lpRun['source'] ?? '');
        $__lpSettings = array();
        $__lpSavedRow = array();
        if ($__lpRunId > 0 && isset($__savedSetsById[$__lpRunId])) {
            $__lpSavedRow = (array)$__savedSetsById[$__lpRunId];
            // Try to decode settings_json for extended flags
            foreach (array('settings_json','settings','params_json','params') as $__lpSKey) {
                if (!empty($__lpSavedRow[$__lpSKey])) {
                    $__lpDec = json_decode((string)$__lpSavedRow[$__lpSKey], true);
                    if (is_array($__lpDec)) {
                        $__lpSettings = $__lpDec;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        $__lpTargetMeta = mylottoexpertResolvePredictionTargetMeta($__lpSavedRow);
        $__lpLineageMeta = mylottoexpertResolveRunLineageMeta($__lpSavedRow);
        // Derive learning module flags from settings fields that exist in the schema
        $__lpRunMode   = strtolower((string)($__lpSettings['skai_run_mode'] ?? ''));
        $__lpPureMode  = (int)($__lpSettings['pure_mode'] ?? 0);
        $__lpAutoTune  = !empty($__lpSettings['auto_tune']) && (string)$__lpSettings['auto_tune'] !== '0';
        // Map known run modes to module flags
        // 'pairwise' mode signals pairwise correlation engine
        // 'gibbs' or 'mcmc' signals Gibbs/MCMC sampler
        // 'skai' mode signals full SKAI blend (live tuning active)
        $__lpPairwise   = (strpos($__lpRunMode, 'pairwise') !== false) ? 1 : 0;
        $__lpGibbs      = (strpos($__lpRunMode, 'gibbs') !== false || strpos($__lpRunMode, 'mcmc') !== false) ? 1 : 0;
        $__lpSkaiMode   = (strpos($__lpRunMode, 'skai') !== false) ? 1 : 0;
        $__lpSkaiSource = ($__lpSource === 'skai_prediction' || $__lpSkaiMode) ? 1 : 0;
        $__lpLiveTune   = ($__lpAutoTune || $__lpSkaiMode) ? 1 : 0;

        // Tail Recovery:
        // The old logic only marked Tail Recovery active when pure_mode=0 and
        // skai_window_size existed. That missed many real blended SKAI runs.
        $__lpHasBlendSignal = (
            !empty($__lpSettings['skai_blend_ai_pct']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['blend_ai_pct']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['ai_pct']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['skai_blend_skip_pct']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['blend_skip_pct']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['skip_pct']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['strategy']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['blend']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['profile'])
        ) ? 1 : 0;
        $__lpHasWindowSignal = (
            !empty($__lpSettings['skai_window_size']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['best_window']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['tuned_window']) ||
            !empty($__lpSettings['skip_window'])
        ) ? 1 : 0;

        $__lpTailEnabled = (
            $__lpPureMode === 0 ||
            $__lpSkaiSource ||
            $__lpHasBlendSignal ||
            $__lpHasWindowSignal
        ) ? 1 : 0;

        $__lpTailActive = (
            $__lpTailEnabled &&
            ($__lpSkaiSource || $__lpHasBlendSignal || $__lpHasWindowSignal)
        ) ? 1 : 0;

        // Calibration: flagged when auto_tune is on or tune_used is set
        $__lpCalibEnabled = (!empty($__lpSettings['tune_used']) || $__lpAutoTune) ? 1 : 0;
        $__lpCalibActive  = (!empty($__lpSettings['tune_used'])) ? 1 : 0;
        // Shared learning: flagged when draws_analyzed >= 20 (broad historical window)
        $__lpShared = ((int)($__lpSettings['draws_analyzed'] ?? 0) >= 20) ? 1 : 0;

        // Draw date and run date
        $__lpDrawDate = (string)($__lpRun['draw_date'] ?? '');
        $__lpRunDate  = '';
        if (isset($__savedSetsById[$__lpRunId])) {
            $__lpSR = (array)$__savedSetsById[$__lpRunId];
            $__lpRunDate = (string)($__lpSR['generated_at'] ?? $__lpSR['date_saved'] ?? '');
        }
        if ($__lpDrawDate !== '') {
            $__lpDrawTs = strtotime($__lpDrawDate);
            if ($__lpDrawTs) {
                $__lpDrawDate = date('Y-m-d', $__lpDrawTs);
            }
        }

        // Combo hit summary (regular lotteries only; daily lotteries use digit combos)
        $__lpComboSummary = array();
        if (empty($__lpRun['is_daily'])) {
            $__lpComboSummary = array(
                'hits_main'  => (int)($__lpRun['hits_main']  ?? 0),
                'hits_extra' => (int)($__lpRun['hits_extra'] ?? 0),
            );
        }

        // Derive the actual run setting (AI share used %, strategy family) from the
        // saved run's settings for persistence in notes_json.  This is what the
        // KPI panel surfaces as the "run setting" - the real slider value used.
        $__lpSavedRowForBlend = $__lpSavedRow;
        $__lpBlendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($__lpSavedRowForBlend, $__lpSettings);

        $__lpData = array(
            'lottery_id'            => (int)$__lpLid,
            'lottery_name'          => $__lpLotteryName,
            'draw_date'             => $__lpDrawDate,
            'run_date'              => $__lpRunDate,
            'run_id'                => $__lpRunId,
            'run_uuid'              => (string)($__lpLineageMeta['run_uuid'] ?? ''),
            'snapshot_run_uuid'     => (string)($__lpLineageMeta['snapshot_run_uuid'] ?? ''),
            'run_identity_key'      => (string)($__lpLineageMeta['run_identity_key'] ?? ''),
            'prediction_target_id'  => (string)($__lpTargetMeta['prediction_target_id'] ?? ''),
            'prediction_target_key' => (string)($__lpTargetMeta['prediction_target_key'] ?? ''),
            'target_game_id'        => (string)($__lpTargetMeta['target_game_id'] ?? ''),
            'target_lottery_id'     => (int)($__lpTargetMeta['target_lottery_id'] ?? 0),
            'target_draw_date'      => (string)($__lpTargetMeta['target_draw_date'] ?? ''),
            'target_draw_at'        => (string)($__lpTargetMeta['target_draw_at'] ?? ''),
            'target_draw_session'   => (string)($__lpTargetMeta['target_draw_session'] ?? ''),
            'target_timezone_id'    => (string)($__lpTargetMeta['target_timezone_id'] ?? ''),
            'target_prediction_family' => (string)($__lpTargetMeta['target_prediction_family'] ?? ''),
            'target_prediction_type'   => (string)($__lpTargetMeta['target_prediction_type'] ?? ''),
            'source'                => $__lpSource,
            'actual_numbers'        => $__lpActualMain,
            'predicted_ranking'     => $__lpPredMain,
            'avg_winning_rank'      => $__lpMetrics['avg_rank'],
            'best_winning_rank'     => $__lpMetrics['best_rank'],
            'worst_winning_rank'    => $__lpMetrics['worst_rank'],
            'median_winning_rank'   => $__lpMetrics['median_rank'],
            'weighted_quality_score'=> $__lpMetrics['weighted_score'],
            'top10_hits'            => $__lpMetrics['top10_hits'],
            'top20_hits'            => $__lpMetrics['top20_hits'],
            'top30_hits'            => $__lpMetrics['top30_hits'],
            'top50_hits'            => $__lpMetrics['top50_hits'],
            'missing_hits_count'    => $__lpMetrics['missing_count'],
            'combo_hit_summary'     => $__lpComboSummary,
            'tail_enabled'          => $__lpTailEnabled,
            'tail_active'           => $__lpTailActive,
            'tail_promoted_count'   => 0,
            'tail_promoted_hit_count' => 0,
            'calibration_enabled'   => $__lpCalibEnabled,
            'calibration_active'    => $__lpCalibActive,
            'shared_learning_enabled' => $__lpShared,
            'pairwise_enabled'      => $__lpPairwise,
            'gibbs_enabled'         => $__lpGibbs,
            'live_tuning_enabled'   => $__lpLiveTune,
            'confidence_level'      => 'scored',
            'trend_bucket'          => 'pending',
            // Run configuration snapshot persisted for the KPI panel.
            // Stored in notes_json so existing schema is unchanged.
            // Legacy rows with null/[] notes_json are handled gracefully at render time.
            'notes'                 => array(
                'run_ai_pct'          => $__lpBlendInfo['ai'],
                'run_skip_pct'        => $__lpBlendInfo['skip'],
                'run_strategy_family' => $__lpBlendInfo['strategy_label'],
                'prediction_target_id'=> (string)($__lpTargetMeta['prediction_target_id'] ?? ''),
                'run_uuid'            => (string)($__lpLineageMeta['effective_run_uuid'] ?? ''),
            ),
        );
        if ($workspaceUserId > 0) {
            skaiUpsertPerformanceRecord($db, $workspaceUserId, $__lpData);
        }
    }
}

unset($__lpLottery, $__lpRun, $__lpMetrics, $__lpData);


// PRL uses the shared 7-tier ranking model: total hits -> main hits -> extra hits ->
// successful combo count -> combo quality score -> pos_sum -> run_id.
// This ensures both the "best" highlight and the sort order always agree.
foreach ($__runSummary as $__rscLid => $__rscLsData) {
    if (!isset($bestOpps[$__rscLid]['best_avg_hits'])) { continue; }
    $__rscBestRid = (int)$__rscLsData['best_run_id'];
    if (0 >= $__rscBestRid) { continue; }

    // Look up the saved-set row for the PRL-identified best run.
    // Prefer the DB-fetched row; fall back to the in-memory savedSets lookup.
    if (isset($__winnerRows[$__rscBestRid])) {
        $__rscWinnerRow = $__winnerRows[$__rscBestRid];
    } elseif (isset($__savedSetsById[$__rscBestRid])) {
        $__rscWinnerRow = $__savedSetsById[$__rscBestRid];
    } else {
        continue;
    }

    $__rscDispInfo    = mylottoexpertResolveRunDisplayInfo((array)$__rscWinnerRow, $__methodLabels);
    $__rscDisplayName = $__rscDispInfo['label'];
    $__rscRunMode     = $__rscDispInfo['mode'];

    // Find the last draw date for this specific run in the PRL run list.
    // Runs are sorted by hits desc (not date), so we scan all to find the max date.
    $__rscLastDate = '';
    foreach ($__rscLsData['runs'] as $__rscRun) {
        if ((int)$__rscRun['run_id'] === $__rscBestRid && $__rscRun['has_draw']
            && (string)$__rscRun['draw_date'] > $__rscLastDate) {
            $__rscLastDate = (string)$__rscRun['draw_date'];
        }
    }

    $bestOpps[$__rscLid]['best_avg_hits']['run_id']       = $__rscBestRid;
    $bestOpps[$__rscLid]['best_avg_hits']['max_hits']     = (int)$__rscLsData['max_hits'];
    $bestOpps[$__rscLid]['best_avg_hits']['display_name'] = $__rscDisplayName;
    $bestOpps[$__rscLid]['best_avg_hits']['run_mode']     = $__rscRunMode;
    if ($__rscLastDate !== '') {
        $bestOpps[$__rscLid]['best_avg_hits']['last_scored_date'] = $__rscLastDate;
    }
}

// 5) Analysis types used to render per-method prediction columns.
$modules = array(
    array('key' => 'skip_hit',        'label' => 'SKIP Model',           'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Analyzes historical draw patterns'),
    array('key' => 'ai_prediction',   'label' => 'Neural Network',        'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Deep learning model trained on draw history'),
    array('key' => 'mcmc_prediction', 'label' => 'MCMC',                  'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Statistical sampling method'),
    array('key' => 'heatmap',         'label' => 'Frequency Map',         'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Visual frequency analysis'),
    array('key' => 'skai_prediction', 'label' => 'SKAI Model',            'icon' => '', 'tooltip' => 'Combines multiple analytical methods'),
);

?>

<!-- ==================================================
     CSS Styles (Sorcerer style block)
     ================================================== -->

<?php
// Workspace decision summary metrics
$__intelligenceCards = array();
$__intelligenceTotalRuns = 0;
$__intelligenceActionableLotteries = 0;
$__intelligenceHighConfidenceLotteries = 0;
$__intelligenceActiveLotteries = count($bestOpps);

foreach ($bestOpps as $__dLid => $__dOpp) {
    $__lotteryName = (string)($__dOpp['lottery_name'] ?? 'Lottery');
    $__totalRuns = (int)($__dOpp['total_runs'] ?? 0);
    $__scoredRuns = count((array)($__dOpp['all_scored_runs'] ?? array()));
    $__agreementScore = (int)($__dOpp['best_agreement']['score'] ?? 0);
    $__agreementNumbers = array_values(array_unique(array_map('intval', (array)($__dOpp['best_agreement']['numbers'] ?? array()))));
    $__bestSetupName = (string)($__dOpp['best_avg_hits']['display_name'] ?? 'No validated setup yet');
    $__bestSetupHits = (int)($__dOpp['best_avg_hits']['max_hits'] ?? 0);
    $__bestSetupScoredRuns = (int)($__dOpp['best_avg_hits']['scored_runs'] ?? 0);
    $__bestSetupRunId = (int)($__dOpp['best_avg_hits']['run_id'] ?? 0);
    $__bestSetupRow = ($__bestSetupRunId > 0 && isset($__savedSetsById[$__bestSetupRunId])) ? (array)$__savedSetsById[$__bestSetupRunId] : array();
    $__bestSetupSource = (string)($__bestSetupRow['source'] ?? ($__dOpp['best_rank']['source'] ?? ''));
    $__drawDates = array();
    $__numberCounts = array();
    $__modeStats = array();
    $__topHitCount = 0;

    foreach ((array)($__dOpp['all_scored_runs'] ?? array()) as $__scoredRun) {
        $__drawDate = (string)($__scoredRun['draw_date'] ?? '');
        if ($__drawDate !== '') {
            $__drawDates[$__drawDate] = true;
        }
        foreach ((array)($__scoredRun['pred_main'] ?? array()) as $__num) {
            $__num = (int)$__num;
            if ($__num <= 0) {
                continue;
            }
            if (!isset($__numberCounts[$__num])) {
                $__numberCounts[$__num] = 0;
            }
            $__numberCounts[$__num]++;
            if ($__numberCounts[$__num] > $__topHitCount) {
                $__topHitCount = $__numberCounts[$__num];
            }
        }

        $__runId = (int)($__scoredRun['run_id'] ?? 0);
        if ($__runId > 0 && isset($__savedSetsById[$__runId])) {
            $__runRow = (array)$__savedSetsById[$__runId];
            if ((string)($__runRow['source'] ?? '') === 'skai_prediction') {
                $__runDisp = mylottoexpertResolveRunDisplayInfo($__runRow, $__methodLabels);
                $__modeLabel = $__runDisp['mode'] !== '' ? $__runDisp['mode'] : 'Default';
                $__modeRankScore = (float)($__scoredRun['rank_score'] ?? 0);
                $__modeHitScore = (int)($__scoredRun['hits'] ?? 0);
                $__modeBlendInfo = mylottoexpertBuildBlendDisplayInfo($__runRow, (array)($__runDisp['settings'] ?? array()));
                $__modeBlendValue = '';
                if (isset($__modeBlendInfo['ai']) && $__modeBlendInfo['ai'] !== null && $__modeBlendInfo['ai'] !== '') {
                    $__modeAiText = mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($__modeBlendInfo['ai']);
                    if ($__modeAiText !== '') {
                        $__modeBlendValue = $__modeAiText . '%';
                    }
                }

                if (!isset($__modeStats[$__modeLabel])) {
                    $__modeStats[$__modeLabel] = array(
                        'count' => 0,
                        'best_rank_score' => -1,
                        'best_hits' => -1,
                        'best_run_id' => 0,
                        'blend_value' => ''
                    );
                }

                $__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['count']++;

                $__modeIsBetter = (
                    $__modeRankScore > (float)$__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['best_rank_score']
                    || ($__modeRankScore === (float)$__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['best_rank_score']
                        && $__modeHitScore > (int)$__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['best_hits'])
                    || ($__modeRankScore === (float)$__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['best_rank_score']
                        && $__modeHitScore === (int)$__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['best_hits']
                        && $__runId > (int)$__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['best_run_id'])
                );
                if ($__modeIsBetter) {
                    $__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['best_rank_score'] = $__modeRankScore;
                    $__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['best_hits'] = $__modeHitScore;
                    $__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['best_run_id'] = $__runId;
                    $__modeStats[$__modeLabel]['blend_value'] = $__modeBlendValue;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    arsort($__numberCounts);
    $__repeatPool = array_slice(array_keys($__numberCounts), 0, 6);
    $__repeatPoolDisplay = !empty($__repeatPool) ? implode(', ', $__repeatPool) : 'No repeat pool yet';
    $__repeatSupportLabel = $__topHitCount > 0 ? $__topHitCount . ' run' . ($__topHitCount === 1 ? '' : 's') : 'No repeated support yet';

    $__drawCount = count($__drawDates);
    $__evidenceStage = 'Exploratory';
    $__evidenceNote = 'Recommendations are still early. Keep building the sample before treating any pattern as durable.';
    $__stageScore = 1;
    if ($__totalRuns >= 20 || $__scoredRuns >= 10) {
        $__evidenceStage = 'Strong guidance';
        $__evidenceNote = 'You now have enough sample to let repeatability drive decisions instead of isolated wins.';
        $__stageScore = 4;
        $__intelligenceHighConfidenceLotteries++;
    } elseif ($__totalRuns >= 10 || $__scoredRuns >= 5) {
        $__evidenceStage = 'Watch next';
        $__evidenceNote = 'The pattern is strong enough to narrow your choices, but you should still compare it with your best setup and your past results.';
        $__stageScore = 3;
        $__intelligenceActionableLotteries++;
    } elseif ($__totalRuns >= 5 || $__scoredRuns >= 3) {
        $__evidenceStage = 'Early sign';
        $__evidenceNote = 'You can start seeing a direction, but this is still the stage for careful testing, not full trust.';
        $__stageScore = 2;
    }

    $__signalStrength = 'Weak';
    $__signalNote = 'This lottery still needs more repeated numbers or more scored history before the page can give stronger guidance.';
    $__signalScore = 1;
    if ($__agreementScore >= 3 && $__topHitCount >= 3 && $__bestSetupHits > 0 && $__scoredRuns >= 3) {
        $__signalStrength = 'High';
        $__signalNote = 'Repeated numbers and past results are all pointing in the same direction.';
        $__signalScore = 4;
    } elseif (($__agreementScore >= 2 && $__scoredRuns >= 3) || ($__topHitCount >= 3 && $__bestSetupHits > 0)) {
        $__signalStrength = 'Moderate';
        $__signalNote = 'There is enough alignment to build a smaller set of numbers, but not enough to skip checking.';
        $__signalScore = 3;
    } elseif ($__agreementScore >= 2 || $__scoredRuns >= 2 || $__topHitCount >= 2) {
        $__signalStrength = 'Developing';
        $__signalNote = 'Useful clues are appearing, but the page should still be treated as a narrowing tool.';
        $__signalScore = 2;
    }

    $__dominantModeText = 'No dominant SKAI mode yet';
    $__dominantModeEntries = array();
    if (!empty($__modeStats)) {
        $__modeTotal = 0;
        foreach ($__modeStats as $__modeStatTotal) {
            $__modeTotal += (int)($__modeStatTotal['count'] ?? 0);
        }
        uasort($__modeStats, function ($a, $b) {
            $aRank = (float)($a['best_rank_score'] ?? -1);
            $bRank = (float)($b['best_rank_score'] ?? -1);
            if ($bRank > $aRank) { return 1; }
            if ($bRank < $aRank) { return -1; }

            $aHits = (int)($a['best_hits'] ?? -1);
            $bHits = (int)($b['best_hits'] ?? -1);
            if ($bHits > $aHits) { return 1; }
            if ($bHits < $aHits) { return -1; }

            $aCount = (int)($a['count'] ?? 0);
            $bCount = (int)($b['count'] ?? 0);
            if ($bCount > $aCount) { return 1; }
            if ($bCount < $aCount) { return -1; }
