        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
    <div style="margin-top:.35rem; font-size:.85rem; color:#444;">
      <span style="display:inline-block; width:16px; height:10px; background:#d97706; margin-right:.35rem;"></span>
      <?php echo htmlspecialchars($__extraLabel, ENT_QUOTES); ?> hit at that prediction rank &nbsp;&bull;&nbsp; 0 = no match yet
    </div>
  </div>
  <?php endif; ?>
  
  <?php
  // ===== Dynamic takeaway: best method, tie-break by earliest (lowest) hit rank =====
  // We scan each method's placement row, count total hits, and track how early
  // (low rank) the first hit appears. Ties in total hits are broken by who hits earlier.
  $best = [
      'method'   => null,
      'total'    => -1,
      'bestRank' => PHP_INT_MAX,
  ];
  $perMethodSummaries = [];

  foreach ($methodKeys as $__m) {
      // Main placement row for this method
      $row       = $placementStats[$__m]['main'] ?? [];
      $totalHits = array_sum($row);

      // Find earliest (lowest) rank where this method has at least one hit
      $earliest = PHP_INT_MAX;
      for ($r = 1; $__maxRankMain >= $r; $r++) {
          if (!empty($row[$r])) {
              $earliest = $r;
              break;
          }
      }

      // Find latest (highest) rank where this method has a hit
      $latest = 0;
      for ($r = $__maxRankMain; $r >= 1; $r--) {
          if (!empty($row[$r])) {
              $latest = $r;
              break;
          }
      }

      // Update "best" method:
      // 1) Highest total hits wins
      // 2) If tied, the method that hits earlier (lower rank) wins
      if (
          $totalHits > $best['total']
          || ($totalHits === $best['total'] && $earliest < $best['bestRank'])
      ) {
          $best['method']   = $__m;
          $best['total']    = $totalHits;
          $best['bestRank'] = $earliest;
      }

      // Human-friendly range text, e.g. "#2 - #11" or " - " if no hits
      $rangeText = ($earliest !== PHP_INT_MAX && $latest > 0)
          ? ('#' . $earliest . ' - #' . $latest)
          : ' - ';

      $label = $labelShort[$__m] ?? $__m;
      $perMethodSummaries[] = $label . ': total ' . (int) $totalHits . ' hits, range ' . $rangeText;
  }

  // Compose the headline + advice based on how early the best method hits
  $bestLabel    = $best['method'] ? ($labelShort[$best['method']] ?? $best['method']) : ' - ';
  $bestTotal    = max(0, (int) $best['total']);
  $bestRankText = ($best['bestRank'] === PHP_INT_MAX) ? 'n/a' : '#' . $best['bestRank'];

  // SDI: compute range for 'Best performing rank range' display
  $bestLatestRank = 0;
  if ($best['method']) {
    $__bestRow = $placementStats[$best['method']]['main'] ?? [];
    for ($__r = $__maxRankMain; $__r >= 1; $__r--) {
      if (!empty($__bestRow[$__r])) {
        $bestLatestRank = $__r;
        break;
      }
    }
  }
  if ($best['bestRank'] !== PHP_INT_MAX && $bestLatestRank > 0) {
    $bestRangeText = '#' . $best['bestRank'] . ' - #' . $bestLatestRank;
  } else {
    $bestRangeText = 'n/a';
  }

  if ($best['bestRank'] !== PHP_INT_MAX && 5 >= $best['bestRank']) {
      $advice = 'Great: your best method is hitting in the red zone (#1 - #5). Keep tuning to push more hits into #1 - #3.';
  } elseif ($best['bestRank'] !== PHP_INT_MAX && 10 >= $best['bestRank']) {
      $advice = 'Decent: hits are appearing mid-rank. Try adjusting settings to pull more into #1 - #5.';
  } else {
      $advice = 'Heads-up: hits are mostly late (blue side). Explore other settings to improve early-rank placement.';
  }
  ?>

<div class="helper" style="margin-top:.75rem; padding:.85rem 1.05rem; background:#f7fbff; border:1px solid #dfe6f2; border-radius:8px;">
  <div style="font-weight:700; margin-bottom:0.25rem; font-size:0.95rem; color:#1f2a3a; letter-spacing:0.01em;">
    Best takeaway for this draw
  </div>

  <div style="font-size:0.9rem; margin-bottom:0.35rem;">
    <strong>Best performer:</strong>
    <strong><?php echo htmlspecialchars($bestLabel, ENT_QUOTES); ?></strong>
    with <strong><?php echo $bestTotal; ?> total hits</strong>
    (earliest winning rank <strong><?php echo htmlspecialchars($bestRankText, ENT_QUOTES); ?></strong>).
  </div>

  <div style="font-size:0.9rem; margin-bottom:0.4rem; color:#34495e; line-height:1.45;">
    <?php echo htmlspecialchars($advice, ENT_QUOTES); ?>
  </div>

  <div style="font-size:0.85rem; color:#4a5568; line-height:1.4;">
    <strong>Pattern by method:</strong>
    <em><?php echo htmlspecialchars(implode(' | ', $perMethodSummaries), ENT_QUOTES); ?></em>
    <br>
    <span style="opacity:0.9;">
      Tip: Aim to stack more of your chosen numbers where methods hit early (ranks #1 - #5), and use later ranks as light support numbers.
    </span>
  </div>
</div>

  <!-- SDI: best performing rank range -->
  <div class="sdi-best-range">
    Best rank range: <strong><?php echo htmlspecialchars($bestRangeText, ENT_QUOTES); ?></strong>
  </div>

  <?php
  // Run Selector: list all saved runs so user can click to see each run on the heatmap
  $__runList = [];
  foreach ($g['preds'] as $__pr) {
    $__src = $__pr->source;
    if (!in_array($__src, $methodKeys, true)) { $__src = 'skip_hit'; }
    $__rMainNums  = array_slice(array_map('intval', explode(',', (string)($__pr->main_numbers ?? ''))), 0, $__maxRankMain);
    $__rExtraNums = array_slice(array_map('intval', explode(',', (string)($__pr->extra_ball_numbers ?? ''))), 0, $__maxRankExtra);
    $__rPosMain   = []; foreach ($__rMainNums  as $ri => $rn) { if (!isset($__rPosMain[$rn]))  $__rPosMain[$rn]  = $ri+1; }
    $__rPosExtra  = []; foreach ($__rExtraNums as $ri => $re) { if (!isset($__rPosExtra[$re])) $__rPosExtra[$re] = $ri+1; }
    $__rMainData  = array_fill(1, $__maxRankMain,  0);
    $__rExtraData = array_fill(1, $__maxRankExtra, 0);
    $__rMainHits = 0; $__rExtraHits = 0;
    foreach ($__drawMain  as $dh) { if (isset($__rPosMain[$dh]))  { $r=$__rPosMain[$dh];  if ($r>=1&&$__maxRankMain>=$r)  { $__rMainData[$r]++;  $__rMainHits++;  } } }
    foreach ($__drawExtra as $de) { if (isset($__rPosExtra[$de])) { $r=$__rPosExtra[$de]; if ($r>=1&&$__maxRankExtra>=$r) { $__rExtraData[$r]++; $__rExtraHits++; } } }
    $__rDisp = mylottoexpertResolveRunDisplayInfo($__pr, $__methodLabels);
    $__runList[] = [
      'id'        => (int)$__pr->id,
      'source'    => $__src,
      'label'     => $__rDisp['label'] !== '' ? $__rDisp['label'] : ($labelShort[$__src] ?? $__src),
      'mode'      => $__rDisp['mode'],
      'ts'        => (string)($__pr->generated_at ?: $__pr->date_saved),
      'mainNums'  => $__rMainNums,
      'extraNums' => $__rExtraNums,
      'mainData'  => array_values($__rMainData),
      'extraData' => array_values($__rExtraData),
      'mainHits'  => $__rMainHits,
      'extraHits' => $__rExtraHits,
    ];
  }

<?php
// == SKAI Learning performance Panel - Decision Intelligence ==============
// Upgraded panel: performance grading, consistency, trend intelligence,
// DUAL best-run model (system quality vs hit opportunity), and recommendations.
$__lpGroupLid     = (int)$g['lottery_id'];
$__lpGroupHistory = isset($__skaiPerfByLottery[$__lpGroupLid]) ? (array)$__skaiPerfByLottery[$__lpGroupLid] : array();
$__lpGroupTrend   = skaiComputeTrend($__lpGroupHistory);
$__lpGroupCard    = skaiDeriveScorecard($__lpGroupTrend);

// -- Grading (based on last-10 avg rank; fall back to lifetime) ------------
$__lpGradeAvg     = ($__lpGroupTrend['last10_avg'] !== null) ? $__lpGroupTrend['last10_avg'] : $__lpGroupTrend['lifetime_avg'];
$__lpGrade        = skaiLpGrade($__lpGradeAvg);

// -- Consistency / variance ------------------------------------------------
$__lpConsistency  = skaiLpConsistency($__lpGroupHistory);

// -- Trend intelligence (direction + strength) -----------------------------
$__lpTrendIntel   = skaiLpTrendIntelligence($__lpGroupTrend['delta_10vs20']);

// -- Confidence level (tiered, by run count) -------------------------------
$__lpConfidence   = skaiLpConfidenceLabel((int)$__lpGroupTrend['sample_count']);

// -- Insight paragraph -----------------------------------------------------
$__lpInsightText  = skaiLpInsight($__lpGrade, $__lpTrendIntel, $__lpConsistency, $__lpConfidence);

// -- DUAL BEST-RUN MODEL ---------------------------------------------------
// Best ranking setup example: run with strongest ranking quality (sys composite score)
$__lpBestSystem   = skaiLpSelectBestSystemRun($__lpGroupHistory);
// Best Hit Run: run with strongest hit-oriented outcome (hit composite score)
$__lpBestHit      = skaiLpSelectBestHitRun($__lpGroupHistory);
// Recommended run (Balanced): 60% system quality + 40% hit opportunity
$__lpRecommended  = skaiLpSelectRecommendedRun($__lpGroupHistory, 'balanced');
// "Why these results differ" interpretation text
$__lpDualInsight  = skaiLpDualRunInsight($__lpBestSystem, $__lpBestHit, (int)$__lpGroupTrend['sample_count']);

// -- Setting-context helpers: training style + same-setting trend ----------
$__lpBuildRunContext = function(array $__lpRunCard) use ($__savedSetsById, $__lpGroupHistory) {
    $__ctx = array(
        'training_style' => '',
        'setting_signature' => '',
        'same_setting_runs' => 0,
        'same_setting_trend' => null,
    );

    $__runId = (int)($__lpRunCard['run_id'] ?? 0);
    $__settings = array();
    if ($__runId > 0 && isset($__savedSetsById[$__runId])) {
        $__savedRow = (array)$__savedSetsById[$__runId];
        foreach (array('settings_json','settings','params_json','params') as $__ctxKey) {
            if (!empty($__savedRow[$__ctxKey])) {
                $__decoded = json_decode((string)$__savedRow[$__ctxKey], true);
                if (is_array($__decoded)) {
                    $__settings = $__decoded;
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    $__trainingStyleRaw = '';
    if (!empty($__settings['training_style'])) {
        $__trainingStyleRaw = (string)$__settings['training_style'];
    } elseif (!empty($__settings['profile'])) {
        $__trainingStyleRaw = (string)$__settings['profile'];
    } elseif (!empty($__settings['risk_profile'])) {
        $__trainingStyleRaw = (string)$__settings['risk_profile'];
    }
    $__ctx['training_style'] = skaiLpFormatTrainingStyleLabel($__trainingStyleRaw);

    $__settingLabel = trim((string)($__lpRunCard['run_setting_label'] ?? ''));
    $__ctx['setting_signature'] = strtolower(trim($__ctx['training_style'] . ' | ' . $__settingLabel, ' |'));

    if ($__ctx['setting_signature'] !== '') {
        $__subset = array();
        foreach ((array)$__lpGroupHistory as $__lpHistRec) {
            $__histRun = skaiLpExtractRunRecord(array($__lpHistRec), 0);
            $__histRunId = (int)($__histRun['run_id'] ?? 0);
            $__histSettings = array();
            if ($__histRunId > 0 && isset($__savedSetsById[$__histRunId])) {
                $__histSavedRow = (array)$__savedSetsById[$__histRunId];
                foreach (array('settings_json','settings','params_json','params') as $__histKey) {
                    if (!empty($__histSavedRow[$__histKey])) {
                        $__histDecoded = json_decode((string)$__histSavedRow[$__histKey], true);
                        if (is_array($__histDecoded)) {
                            $__histSettings = $__histDecoded;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            $__histTrainingRaw = '';
            if (!empty($__histSettings['training_style'])) {
                $__histTrainingRaw = (string)$__histSettings['training_style'];
            } elseif (!empty($__histSettings['profile'])) {
                $__histTrainingRaw = (string)$__histSettings['profile'];
            } elseif (!empty($__histSettings['risk_profile'])) {
                $__histTrainingRaw = (string)$__histSettings['risk_profile'];
            }
            $__histTraining = skaiLpFormatTrainingStyleLabel($__histTrainingRaw);
            $__histSignature = strtolower(trim($__histTraining . ' | ' . trim((string)($__histRun['run_setting_label'] ?? '')), ' |'));

            if ($__histSignature !== '' && $__histSignature === $__ctx['setting_signature']) {
                $__subset[] = $__lpHistRec;
            }
        }

        $__ctx['same_setting_runs'] = count($__subset);
        if (!empty($__subset)) {
            $__ctx['same_setting_trend'] = skaiComputeTrend($__subset);
        }
    }

    return $__ctx;
};

$__lpBestSystemCtx  = ($__lpBestSystem !== null) ? $__lpBuildRunContext($__lpBestSystem) : null;
$__lpBestHitCtx     = ($__lpBestHit !== null) ? $__lpBuildRunContext($__lpBestHit) : null;
$__lpRecommendedCtx = ($__lpRecommended !== null) ? $__lpBuildRunContext($__lpRecommended) : null;


// -- Row indexes for table badges ------------------------------------------
// Each role maps to the array index of the corresponding record in $__lpGroupHistory
$__lpSysRowIdx = ($__lpBestSystem   !== null) ? (int)$__lpBestSystem['idx']  : null;
$__lpHitRowIdx = ($__lpBestHit      !== null) ? (int)$__lpBestHit['idx']     : null;
$__lpRecRowIdx = ($__lpRecommended  !== null) ? (int)$__lpRecommended['idx'] : null;

// Worst row (highest avg rank) - uses dedicated helper to stay DRY
$__lpWorstRowIdx = skaiLpSelectWorstRun($__lpGroupHistory);

// -- Module flag summary (most recent 10 scored runs) ---------------------
$__lpModFlags = array(
    'tail_enabled' => 0, 'tail_active' => 0,
    'calibration_enabled' => 0, 'calibration_active' => 0,
    'shared_learning_enabled' => 0, 'pairwise_enabled' => 0,
    'gibbs_enabled' => 0, 'live_tuning_enabled' => 0,
);
$__lpModSampleCount = 0;
foreach (array_slice($__lpGroupHistory, 0, 10) as $__lpHRec) {
    $__lpModSampleCount++;
    foreach (array_keys($__lpModFlags) as $__lpMKey) {
        $__lpModFlags[$__lpMKey] += (int)($__lpHRec[$__lpMKey] ?? 0);
    }
}

// Latest accumulated draw-context signals.
// We use the most recent scored group row as the current state for this draw context,
// then combine it with historical support from the scored history above.
$__lpCurrentSignals = array(
    'tail' => 0,
    'calibration' => 0,
    'shared' => 0,
    'pairwise' => 0,
    'gibbs' => 0,
    'live_tuning' => 0,
);
if (!empty($__lpGroupHistory[0]) && !empty($__lpGroupHistory[0]['run_id'])) {
    $__lpCurrentRunId = (int)$__lpGroupHistory[0]['run_id'];
    $__lpCurrentSource = (string)($__lpGroupHistory[0]['source'] ?? '');
    $__lpCurrentSettings = array();
    if ($__lpCurrentRunId > 0 && isset($__savedSetsById[$__lpCurrentRunId])) {
        $__lpCurrentSavedRow = (array)$__savedSetsById[$__lpCurrentRunId];
        foreach (array('settings_json','settings','params_json','params') as $__lpCurrentSKey) {
            if (!empty($__lpCurrentSavedRow[$__lpCurrentSKey])) {
                $__lpCurrentDec = json_decode((string)$__lpCurrentSavedRow[$__lpCurrentSKey], true);
                if (is_array($__lpCurrentDec)) {
                    $__lpCurrentSettings = $__lpCurrentDec;
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    $__lpCurrentRunMode = strtolower((string)($__lpCurrentSettings['skai_run_mode'] ?? ''));
    $__lpCurrentPureMode = (int)($__lpCurrentSettings['pure_mode'] ?? 0);
    $__lpCurrentAutoTune = (!empty($__lpCurrentSettings['auto_tune']) && (string)$__lpCurrentSettings['auto_tune'] !== '0') ? 1 : 0;
    $__lpCurrentHasBlendSignal = (
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['skai_blend_ai_pct']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['blend_ai_pct']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['ai_pct']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['skai_blend_skip_pct']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['blend_skip_pct']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['skip_pct']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['strategy']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['blend']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['profile'])
    ) ? 1 : 0;
    $__lpCurrentHasWindowSignal = (
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['skai_window_size']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['best_window']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['tuned_window']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['skip_window'])
    ) ? 1 : 0;

    $__lpCurrentSignals['tail'] = (
        $__lpCurrentPureMode === 0 ||
        $__lpCurrentSource === 'skai_prediction' ||
        strpos($__lpCurrentRunMode, 'skai') !== false ||
        $__lpCurrentHasBlendSignal ||
        $__lpCurrentHasWindowSignal
    ) ? 1 : 0;

    $__lpCurrentSignals['calibration'] = (
        $__lpCurrentAutoTune ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['tune_used'])
    ) ? 1 : 0;

    $__lpCurrentSignals['shared'] = ((int)($__lpCurrentSettings['draws_analyzed'] ?? 0) >= 20) ? 1 : 0;
    $__lpCurrentSignals['pairwise'] = (strpos($__lpCurrentRunMode, 'pairwise') !== false) ? 1 : 0;
    $__lpCurrentSignals['gibbs'] = (strpos($__lpCurrentRunMode, 'gibbs') !== false || strpos($__lpCurrentRunMode, 'mcmc') !== false) ? 1 : 0;
    $__lpCurrentSignals['live_tuning'] = (
        $__lpCurrentAutoTune ||
        strpos($__lpCurrentRunMode, 'skai') !== false ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['tune_used']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['best_window']) ||
        !empty($__lpCurrentSettings['tuned_window'])
    ) ? 1 : 0;
}

$__lpTailSignalCount = max((int)$__lpModFlags['tail_active'], (int)$__lpModFlags['tail_enabled']);
$__lpTailLabel   = skaiLpCurrentHybridStatus((int)$__lpCurrentSignals['tail'],        $__lpTailSignalCount,                     $__lpModSampleCount);
$__lpCalibLabel  = skaiLpCurrentHybridStatus((int)$__lpCurrentSignals['calibration'], (int)$__lpModFlags['calibration_active'], $__lpModSampleCount);
$__lpSharedLabel = skaiLpCurrentHybridStatus((int)$__lpCurrentSignals['shared'],      (int)$__lpModFlags['shared_learning_enabled'], $__lpModSampleCount);
$__lpPairLabel   = skaiLpCurrentHybridStatus((int)$__lpCurrentSignals['pairwise'],    (int)$__lpModFlags['pairwise_enabled'],  $__lpModSampleCount);
$__lpGibbsLabel  = skaiLpCurrentHybridStatus((int)$__lpCurrentSignals['gibbs'],       (int)$__lpModFlags['gibbs_enabled'],     $__lpModSampleCount);
$__lpLiveTuneLabel = skaiLpCurrentHybridStatus(
    (int)$__lpCurrentSignals['live_tuning'],
    (int)$__lpModFlags['live_tuning_enabled'],
    $__lpModSampleCount
);

// -- Display helpers -------------------------------------------------------
$__lpFmtNum = function($v, $decimals = 1) {
    if ($v === null || $v === '') { return '<span style="color:#cbd5e1;">&#8212;</span>'; }
    return htmlspecialchars((string)round((float)$v, $decimals), ENT_QUOTES);
};
$__lpFmtRankColor = function($v) {
    if ($v === null || $v === '') { return '<span style="color:#cbd5e1;">&#8212;</span>'; }
    $f = round((float)$v, 1);
    if ($f <= 5)  { $c = '#b45309'; }
    elseif ($f <= 10) { $c = '#059669'; }
    elseif ($f <= 20) { $c = '#d97706'; }
    else { $c = '#dc2626'; }
    return '<span style="font-weight:700;color:' . $c . ';">' . htmlspecialchars((string)$f, ENT_QUOTES) . '</span>';
};

  <!-- -- Metric definitions (expanded with dual-model concepts) ----------- -->
  <div class="skai-lp-definitions">
    <details>
      <summary>&#x2139;&#xFE0F; How these measures work</summary>
      <div class="skai-lp-def-grid">
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Performance grade</strong>
          Based on Average winning rank: Elite (1&#8211;5), Strong (6&#8211;10),
          Moderate (11&#8211;20), Weak (21+). Lower rank = better.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Average winning rank</strong>
          The average position at which actual drawn numbers appeared in SKAI's
          ranked prediction list. Rank 1 = top prediction. Lower is better.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Setting used</strong>
          The exact AI share used percentage that was active when the run was generated.
          Shown as &ldquo;55% &bull; Balanced Mix&rdquo; - the number is the real slider value.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Strategy family</strong>
          The behavior group associated with the slider setting.
          AI&#8209;Forward (65%+): AI-driven weighting.
          Balanced Mix (41&#8211;64%): Balanced SKAI mix.
          Skip Pattern Boost (0&#8211;40%): More skip-pattern emphasis.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Best ranking setup example</strong>
          The run with the strongest ranking quality. Selected by a composite score:
          45% avg rank + 30% weighted score + 15% best rank + 10% missing count.
          Measures overall ranking quality.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Best hit setup example</strong>
          The run with the strongest hit-oriented outcome. Selected by:
          45% Top-20 hits + 30% Top-10 hits + 15% missing + 10% avg rank.
          Measures strongest hit potential.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Recommended setting</strong>
          The exact run configuration that performed best across both ranking quality
          and hit coverage. Shown as the real slider percentage and strategy family used.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Why the ranking result and hit result can differ</strong>
          A run can rank winning numbers better overall (lower avg rank) without
          producing the highest hit count in a specific threshold - and vice versa.
          Both measures are valid for different evaluation goals.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Consistency</strong>
          Standard deviation of avg ranks across all runs.
          Low (&sigma;&lt;3) = High. Medium (&sigma;3&#8211;7) = Moderate. High (&sigma;&ge;7) = Volatile.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Overall trend direction</strong>
          Compares your newest 10 scored runs against the 10 before them across all saved runs for this lottery.
          Positive delta means the rank improved. This is your broad overall trend.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Same-setting trend</strong>
          Measures only runs that used the same training style and blend together.
          This helps answer whether one specific strategy is improving over time instead of mixing every strategy into one trend.
        </div>
        <div class="skai-lp-def-item">
          <strong>Weighted quality score</strong>
          Sum of 1&#x2215;rank for each winning number found. Rewards numbers near
          the top of the list much more heavily than those lower down.
        </div>
      </div>
    </details>
  </div>

  <hr class="skai-lp-divider">

  <div class="skai-lp-history">
    <details>
      <summary style="cursor:pointer;font-size:0.82rem;font-weight:700;color:#475569;
                      text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.04em;padding:0.4rem 0;
                      list-style:none;display:-webkit-flex;display:flex;

              <th>Top 20</th>
              <th>Weighted score</th>
              <th>Missing</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            <?php foreach ($__lpGroupHistory as $__lpHIdx => $__lpHR): ?>
            <?php
              $__lpHTS    = strtotime((string)($__lpHR['draw_date'] ?? ''));
              $__lpHDStr  = $__lpHTS ? date('M j, Y', $__lpHTS) : htmlspecialchars((string)($__lpHR['draw_date'] ?? ''), ENT_QUOTES);
              $__lpHAvg   = (isset($__lpHR['avg_winning_rank']) && $__lpHR['avg_winning_rank'] !== null && $__lpHR['avg_winning_rank'] !== '')
                              ? round((float)$__lpHR['avg_winning_rank'], 1) : null;
              $__lpHBest  = ($__lpHR['best_winning_rank'] !== null) ? (int)$__lpHR['best_winning_rank'] : null;
              $__lpHWSc   = (isset($__lpHR['weighted_quality_score']) && $__lpHR['weighted_quality_score'] !== null && $__lpHR['weighted_quality_score'] !== '')
                              ? round((float)$__lpHR['weighted_quality_score'], 3) : null;
              $__lpHGrade = skaiLpGrade($__lpHAvg);

              // Decode run setting from notes_json and build label via shared helper
              $__lpHNotes   = array();
              if (!empty($__lpHR['notes_json'])) {
                  $__lpHNotesD = json_decode((string)$__lpHR['notes_json'], true);
                  if (is_array($__lpHNotesD)) { $__lpHNotes = $__lpHNotesD; }
              }
              $__lpHAiPct  = (isset($__lpHNotes['run_ai_pct']) && $__lpHNotes['run_ai_pct'] !== null && $__lpHNotes['run_ai_pct'] !== '')
                               ? (float)$__lpHNotes['run_ai_pct'] : null;
              $__lpHStratF = (isset($__lpHNotes['run_strategy_family']) && $__lpHNotes['run_strategy_family'] !== '')
                               ? (string)$__lpHNotes['run_strategy_family'] : '';
              $__lpHSettingRaw = skaiLpFormatRunSettingLabel($__lpHAiPct, $__lpHStratF);
              $__lpHSetting = ($__lpHSettingRaw !== '')
                  ? htmlspecialchars($__lpHSettingRaw, ENT_QUOTES)
                  : '<span style="color:#cbd5e1;font-size:0.75rem;">&#8212;</span>';

              // Determine row role class (sys best has priority for row tint)
              $__lpHRowCls  = '';
              if ($__lpHIdx === $__lpSysRowIdx)  { $__lpHRowCls = ' lp-row-best'; }
              elseif ($__lpHIdx === $__lpWorstRowIdx) { $__lpHRowCls = ' lp-row-worst'; }

              // Build stacked role badges
              $__lpHBadges = '';
              if ($__lpHIdx === $__lpSysRowIdx)  { $__lpHBadges .= '<span class="lp-run-badge lp-run-badge--sys">Rank best</span>'; }
              if ($__lpHIdx === $__lpHitRowIdx)  { $__lpHBadges .= '<span class="lp-run-badge lp-run-badge--hit">Hit best</span>'; }
              if ($__lpHIdx === $__lpRecRowIdx)  { $__lpHBadges .= '<span class="lp-run-badge lp-run-badge--rec">Rec</span>'; }
              if ($__lpHIdx === $__lpWorstRowIdx){ $__lpHBadges .= '<span style="font-size:0.9rem;" title="Worst overall avg rank">&#x1F534;</span>'; }
              if ($__lpHBadges === '')            { $__lpHBadges = '<span style="color:#cbd5e1;font-size:0.75rem;">&#8212;</span>'; }
            ?>
            <tr class="<?php echo $__lpHRowCls; ?>">
              <td><?php echo $__lpHDStr; ?></td>
              <td class="lp-role-cell"><?php echo $__lpHBadges; ?></td>
              <td style="font-size:0.78rem;white-space:nowrap;"><?php echo $__lpHSetting; ?></td>
              <td>
                <span class="lp-tier-badge lp-tier-badge--<?php echo htmlspecialchars($__lpHGrade['grade'], ENT_QUOTES); ?>">
                  <?php echo htmlspecialchars($__lpHGrade['label'], ENT_QUOTES); ?>
                </span>
              </td>
              <td><?php echo $__lpFmtRankColor($__lpHAvg); ?></td>
              <td><?php echo ($__lpHBest !== null) ? htmlspecialchars((string)$__lpHBest, ENT_QUOTES) : '&#8212;'; ?></td>
              <td><?php echo (int)$__lpHR['top10_hits']; ?></td>
              <td><?php echo (int)$__lpHR['top20_hits']; ?></td>
              <td><?php echo ($__lpHWSc !== null) ? htmlspecialchars((string)$__lpHWSc, ENT_QUOTES) : '&#8212;'; ?></td>
              <td><?php echo (int)$__lpHR['missing_hits_count']; ?></td>
            </tr>
            <?php endforeach; ?>
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
    </details>
  </div>

  <?php endif; ?>

  <!-- METHODS TAB -->
  <div class="sdi-panel" data-sdi-panel="methods" role="tabpanel" style="display:none;">

      <!-- Narrative: What Stands Out -->
      <div class="narrative-header" style="margin:1.5rem 1rem 1rem; padding:1rem; background:linear-gradient(135deg, #f8fafc 0%, #e7f3ff 100%); border-left:3px solid #3b82f6; border-radius:8px;">

        </p>
      </div>

            <!-- Prediction cards: max 3 per row, wrapping grid layout -->
      <div class="predictions-row">

        <?php
          // 1) Group saved runs by source
          $predsBySource = [];
          foreach ($g['preds'] as $s) {
            $predsBySource[$s->source][] = $s;
          }
        ?>

        <?php foreach ($modules as $mod):
          $moduleKey     = $mod['key'];
          $moduleLabel   = $mod['label'];
          $moduleIcon    = $mod['icon'];
          $moduleTooltip = $mod['tooltip'] ?? '';
          $runs          = $predsBySource[$moduleKey] ?? [];
        ?>
        <div class="prediction-column">

          <?php if (!empty($runs)): ?>

            <?php foreach ($runs as $s):

<?php
// Load user's saved settings templates
$q = $db->getQuery(true)
    ->select([
        's.*',
        'l.name AS lottery_name',
        'l.game_id AS lottery_game_id',
        'l.lottery_urls AS lottery_page_url',
        'st.name AS state_name'
    ])
    ->from($db->quoteName('#__user_saved_settings', 's'))
    ->join('LEFT', $db->quoteName('#__lotteries', 'l') . ' ON s.lottery_id = l.lottery_id')
    ->join('LEFT', $db->quoteName('#__states', 'st') . ' ON l.state_id = st.state_id')
    ->where('s.user_id = ' . $workspaceUserId)
    ->order('s.created_at DESC');

$db->setQuery($q);
$savedSettings = $db->loadAssocList() ?: [];

?>
<?php if (!empty($savedSettings)): ?>
  <div class="card" style="margin-top:2rem;">
    <div class="card-header">
      <h3 class="title">Saved configurations</h3>
      <p style="margin:0; color:var(--skai-text-secondary); font-size:0.9rem;">Reuse your saved settings for future predictions</p>
    </div>
    <ul style="list-style:none; margin:0; padding:1rem;">
      <?php foreach ($savedSettings as $set):
        // Decode JSON params - support both new structured format and legacy flat format.
        $params = json_decode($set['params'], true) ?: [];

        // Normalize: resolve Training Style from multiple legacy keys.
        $__trainingStyle = '';
        foreach (['training_style', 'profile', 'risk_profile'] as $__tsk) {
            if (!empty($params[$__tsk])) { $__trainingStyle = (string)$params[$__tsk]; break; }
        }
        // Normalize: resolve Strategy from multiple legacy keys.
        $__strategy = '';
        foreach (['strategy', 'blend'] as $__sk) {
            if (!empty($params[$__sk])) { $__strategy = (string)$params[$__sk]; break; }
        }
        // Normalize: resolve Mode.
        $__mode = '';
        foreach (['skai_run_mode', 'mode', 'run_mode'] as $__mk) {
            if (!empty($params[$__mk])) { $__mode = ucwords(str_replace('_', ' ', (string)$params[$__mk])); break; }
        }
        // Normalize: resolve Blend percentages.
        $__blendSkip = null; $__blendAi = null;
        foreach (['skai_blend_skip_pct', 'blend_skip_pct', 'skip_pct'] as $__bsk) {
            if (isset($params[$__bsk]) && $params[$__bsk] !== '') { $__blendSkip = (float)$params[$__bsk]; break; }
        }
        foreach (['skai_blend_ai_pct', 'blend_ai_pct', 'ai_pct'] as $__bak) {
            if (isset($params[$__bak]) && $params[$__bak] !== '') { $__blendAi = (float)$params[$__bak]; break; }
        }
        $__blendDisplay = '';
        if ($__blendSkip !== null && $__blendAi !== null) {
            $__blendDisplay = 'Skip ' . mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($__blendSkip) . '% / AI ' . mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($__blendAi) . '%';
        } elseif ($__blendAi !== null) {
            $__blendDisplay = 'AI ' . mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($__blendAi) . '%';
        } elseif ($__blendSkip !== null) {
            $__blendDisplay = 'Skip ' . mylottoexpertFormatPercentForLabel($__blendSkip) . '%';
        }
        $__pageSavedFrom = !empty($params['page_saved_from']) ? (string)$params['page_saved_from'] : '';
      ?>
        <li style="margin-bottom:1.75rem; border-bottom:1px solid #e2e8f0; padding-bottom:1.25rem;">
          <div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;align-items:baseline;gap:6px;margin-bottom:4px;">
            <strong style="font-size:1rem;"><?php echo htmlspecialchars($set['setting_name'], ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8'); ?></strong>
            <span style="font-size:0.8rem;color:#64748b;">
              <?php
                $sourceLabel = ucfirst(str_replace('_', ' ', $set['source']));
                $__setDisplayMeta = mylottoexpertResolveDisplayLocationMeta(
                    (string)($set['state_name'] ?? ''),
                    '',
                    (string)($set['lottery_name'] ?? ''),
                    ''
                );
                $state       = htmlspecialchars((string)$__setDisplayMeta['state'], ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8');
                $lotteryName = htmlspecialchars((string)$__setDisplayMeta['lottery'], ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8');
                $__locParts  = array_filter([$state, $lotteryName], static function($v) { return $v !== ''; });
                echo htmlspecialchars($sourceLabel, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8');
                if (!empty($__locParts)) { echo ' &mdash; ' . implode(' &bull; ', $__locParts); }
                if ($__pageSavedFrom !== '') { echo ' &mdash; saved from: ' . htmlspecialchars($__pageSavedFrom, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8'); }
              ?>
            </span>
          </div>
          <div style="font-size:0.78rem;color:#94a3b8;margin-bottom:8px;">

          </div>

              </span>

          <?php if ($params): ?>
            <div class="settings-params" style="font-size:0.82rem; color:#475569; margin-top:0.3rem;">
              <?php
                // Human-friendly labels - identity fields already shown above, exclude from flat list.
                $__skipParamsDisplay = ['training_style','profile','risk_profile','strategy','blend',
                                        'skai_run_mode','mode','run_mode',
                                        'skai_blend_skip_pct','skai_blend_ai_pct','blend_skip_pct',
                                        'blend_ai_pct','skip_pct','ai_pct','page_saved_from'];
                $labels = [
                  'draws_analyzed'      => 'Draws',
                  'freq_weight'         => 'Freq Wt',
                  'skip_weight'         => 'Skip Wt',
                  'hist_weight'         => 'Hist Wt',
                  'epochs'              => 'Epochs',
                  'batch_size'          => 'Batch',
                  'dropout_rate'        => 'Dropout',
                  'learning_rate'       => 'LR',
                  'activation_function' => 'ActFn',

                  'laplace_k'           => 'Laplace K',
                  'decay'               => 'Decay',
                  'chain_len'           => 'Chain Len',
                ];
                $parts = [];
                foreach ($params as $key => $val) {
                  if (in_array($key, $__skipParamsDisplay, true)) { continue; }
                  $lbl = $labels[$key] ?? ucwords(str_replace('_', ' ', $key));
                  $parts[] = htmlspecialchars($lbl, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8') . ': ' . htmlspecialchars((string)$val, ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8');
                }
                if (!empty($parts)) { echo implode(' | ', $parts); }
              ?>
            </div>
          <?php endif; ?>

          <?php
            // [[MLE_RECALL_DATA_ATTR]]
            // Encode params in a data attribute to avoid JSON_HEX_QUOT \u0022 SyntaxError.
            // JSON_HEX_QUOT converts " to \u0022; embedded directly in onclick="..." that
            // causes SyntaxError: missing ) after argument list (my-dashboard:2:2).
            // htmlspecialchars with ENT_QUOTES stores " as &quot; in the attribute; the
            // browser decodes it back to " when getAttribute() is called, so JSON.parse
            // receives valid JSON.
            $__mleParamsAttr = htmlspecialchars(
                json_encode($params, JSON_HEX_TAG | JSON_HEX_AMP | JSON_HEX_APOS | JSON_UNESCAPED_UNICODE),
                ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8'
            );
            $__mleNoteAttr = htmlspecialchars((string)($set['user_notes'] ?? ''), ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8');
          ?>
          <!-- User note display -->
          <?php if ($__mleNoteAttr !== ''): ?>

                        rows="3"

                        ><?php echo htmlspecialchars((string)($set['user_notes'] ?? ''), ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8'); ?></textarea>

<div id="favorite-lotteries" class="favorite-lotteries-grid">

<details open class="card favorites-wrapper">
  <summary class="card-header favorite-lotteries-header">
    <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; justify-content:space-between; width:100%; flex-wrap:wrap;">
      <div style="display:flex; align-items:center; gap:10px;">
        <span class="title">Your favorite lotteries</span>
        <span class="section-badge"><?php echo count($favoriteLotteries); ?></span>
      </div>
      <a href="/select-favorite-lotteries" class="btn-primary">+ Edit</a>
    </div>
  </summary>

  <p class="mle-section-explainer" style="margin:0.75rem 1rem 0;">Track your selected lotteries in one place. Use this section to confirm each lottery context and quickly open official results.</p>

  <div id="favorites-list">
 
    <?php if (!empty($favoriteLotteries)): ?>
      <div class="favorites-grid">
        <?php foreach ($favoriteLotteries as $lotto): ?>
          <?php
            // Latest completed draw + next scheduled draw are loaded separately.
            $drawingInfo  = getLatestDrawing($lotto['game_id'], $db);
            $nextDrawInfo = getNextScheduledDrawing($lotto['game_id'], $db);

            // Sanitize the URL for "View Results"
            $url = htmlspecialchars(trim($lotto['lottery_urls']), ENT_QUOTES, 'UTF-8');

            // Default placeholders
            $lastDraw      = 'N/A';
            $lastDrawHeld  = 'N/A';
            $nextDraw      = 'N/A';
            $nextDrawHeld  = 'N/A';
            $drawnStr      = 'N/A';

            if (!empty($drawingInfo)) {
                $lastDraw = !empty($drawingInfo['draw_date'])
                    ? date('M j, Y', strtotime($drawingInfo['draw_date']))
                    : 'N/A';
                $lastDrawHeld = mylottoexpertFormatDrawHeldLabel($drawingInfo);

                $drawParts = mylottoexpertExtractDrawNumbersFromRow($lotto['game_id'], $drawingInfo);
                $drawnAll  = array_merge(
                    isset($drawParts['main']) && is_array($drawParts['main']) ? $drawParts['main'] : array(),
                    isset($drawParts['extra']) && is_array($drawParts['extra']) ? $drawParts['extra'] : array()
                );

                $drawnStr = !empty($drawnAll)
                    ? implode(', ', array_map('strval', $drawnAll))
                    : 'N/A';
            }

            if (!empty($nextDrawInfo['draw_date'])) {
                $nextDraw = date('M j, Y', strtotime($nextDrawInfo['draw_date']));
                $nextDrawHeld = mylottoexpertFormatDrawHeldLabel($nextDrawInfo);

            }

            $nameLower = mb_strtolower($lotto['lottery_name'], 'UTF-8');

                (string)($lotto['state_name'] ?? ''),
                (string)($lotto['country_name'] ?? ''),
                (string)($lotto['lottery_name'] ?? ''),
                (string)($lotto['game_id'] ?? '')
            );
            $lottoDisplayTitle = mylottoexpertFormatLotteryLocationLine(
                (string)$lottoDisplayMeta['state'],
                (string)$lottoDisplayMeta['country'],
                (string)$lottoDisplayMeta['lottery'],
                (string)($lotto['game_id'] ?? '')
            );
            $lottoDisplayLocation = mylottoexpertFormatLotteryLocationLine(
                (string)$lottoDisplayMeta['state'],
                (string)$lottoDisplayMeta['country'],
                '',
                (string)($lotto['game_id'] ?? ''),
                ', '
            );
            if (strpos($nameLower, 'pick 3') !== false) {
                $typeBadge = 'Pick 3';
            } elseif (strpos($nameLower, 'pick 4') !== false) {
                $typeBadge = 'Pick 4';
            } elseif (strpos($nameLower, 'powerball') !== false) {
                $typeBadge = 'Powerball';
            } elseif (strpos($nameLower, 'mega') !== false) {
                $typeBadge = 'Mega Millions';
            }
          ?>
