      t.setAttribute('aria-selected', active ? 'true' : 'false');
      t.tabIndex = active ? 0 : -1;
    });
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(panel.querySelectorAll('.sdi-panel'), function(p) {
      p.style.display = (p.getAttribute('data-sdi-panel') === tabId) ? '' : 'none';
    });
  }
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
    var t = ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('.sdi-tab') : null;
    if (t) activateTab(t);
  });
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(ev) {
    if (ev.key !== 'ArrowLeft' && ev.key !== 'ArrowRight') return;
    var t = ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('.sdi-tab') : null;
    if (!t) return;
    var all = Array.prototype.slice.call(t.parentElement.querySelectorAll('.sdi-tab'));
    var idx = all.indexOf(t);
    var next = ev.key === 'ArrowRight' ? all[(idx+1)%all.length] : all[(idx-1+all.length)%all.length];
    if (next) { next.focus(); activateTab(next); }
    ev.preventDefault();
  });
  // Initialize tab visibility on page load for every lottery group
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.sdi-tab-bar'), function(bar) {
    var active = bar.querySelector('.sdi-tab[aria-selected="true"]') ||
                 bar.querySelector('.sdi-tab');
    if (active) activateTab(active);
  });
}());

// Overview tab-chip navigation: clicking [data-skai-goto-tab] activates the named tab
// within the nearest lottery collapsible content ancestor.
// targetTabId is validated against a known allowlist before use in selector.
document.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
  var chip = ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('[data-skai-goto-tab]') : null;
  if (!chip) return;
  var targetTabId = chip.getAttribute('data-skai-goto-tab') || '';
  // Allowlist: only known tab IDs are accepted (prevents selector injection)
  var allowedTabs = { overview: 1, performance: 1, methods: 1, settings: 1 };
  if (!allowedTabs[targetTabId]) return;
  var content = chip.closest ? chip.closest('.lottery-collapsible-content') : null;
  if (!content) return;
  var targetTab = content.querySelector('.sdi-tab[data-sdi-tab="' + targetTabId + '"]');
  if (targetTab) {
    var bar = targetTab.parentElement;
    if (!bar) return;
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(bar.querySelectorAll('.sdi-tab'), function(t) {
      var active = (t === targetTab);
      t.setAttribute('aria-selected', active ? 'true' : 'false');
      t.tabIndex = active ? 0 : -1;
    });
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(content.querySelectorAll('.sdi-panel'), function(p) {
      p.style.display = (p.getAttribute('data-sdi-panel') === targetTabId) ? '' : 'none';
    });
    targetTab.focus();
  }
});

// Convert all timestamps to user's local timezone
// This runs after the DOM is loaded to convert ISO timestamps to local time
function convertTimestampsToLocal() {
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.local-time'), function(el) {
    var container = el.closest('[data-timestamp]');
    if (!container) return;
    
    var isoTime = container.getAttribute('data-timestamp');
    if (!isoTime) return;
    
    try {
      var date = new Date(isoTime);
      if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return;
      
      // Format: "Dec 30, 2025, 3:45pm"
      var options = {
        month: 'short',
        day: 'numeric',
        year: 'numeric',
        hour: 'numeric',
        minute: '2-digit',
        hour12: true
      };
      
      var localTime = date.toLocaleString('en-US', options);
      el.textContent = localTime;
    } catch (e) {
      // If conversion fails, leave the original timestamp
      console.error('Failed to convert timestamp:', isoTime, e);
    }
  });
}

// Run timestamp conversion after DOM is ready
convertTimestampsToLocal();

function initOuterLotteryCollapse() {
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.mle-lottery-outer'), function(outerEl) {
    var lid = outerEl.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-id') || '';
    var storageKey = lid ? ('mle_outer_collapsed_' + lid) : '';
    try {
      if (storageKey && localStorage.getItem(storageKey) === 'true') {
        outerEl.classList.add('body-collapsed');
        var btn = outerEl.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle');
        if (btn) { btn.textContent = '\u25b6 Expand'; }
      }
    } catch (e) {}
  });
}

initOuterLotteryCollapse();

// Lottery section collapse/expand: restore initial state from localStorage.
// Click handling is done by data-lottery-toggle-btn="1" on the button.
function initLotteryCollapse() {
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group'), function(group) {
    var toggle = group.querySelector('.lottery-collapse-toggle');
    if (!toggle) return;

    var lotteryId = group.getAttribute('data-lottery-id');
    var baseLid    = lotteryId ? lotteryId.split('-')[0] : '';
    if (!lotteryId) return;

    // Restore collapsed state from localStorage
    try {
      if (localStorage.getItem('lottery_collapsed_' + (baseLid || lotteryId)) === 'true') {
        group.classList.add('collapsed');
        toggle.textContent = '\u25b6 Expand';
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Expand lottery section');
      }
    } catch (e) {}
  });
}

// Initialize lottery collapse functionality
initLotteryCollapse();

// Set the initial label of the "Collapse All / Expand All" global button.
(function() {
  var allBtn = document.getElementById('mle-lottery-toggle-all-btn');
  if (!allBtn) { return; }
  var groups = document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group');
  var anyExpanded = false;
  for (var i = 0; i < groups.length; i++) {
    if (!groups[i].classList.contains('collapsed')) { anyExpanded = true; break; }
  }
  allBtn.textContent = anyExpanded ? '\u25bc Collapse All' : '\u25b6 Expand All';
}());

// Restore Prediction Results section collapse state from localStorage.
(function() {
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('.prc-section'), function(sec) {
    var sectionId = sec.id;
    if (!sectionId) { return; }
    try {
      if (localStorage.getItem('prc_collapsed_' + sectionId) === 'true') {
        skaiPrcSetCollapsed(sec, true);
      }
    } catch (e) { /* localStorage unavailable (private browsing / quota) */ }
  });
})();

// ============================================================
// Strategy Workspace -- Overview tab, PRE-DRAW mode (ES5, no deps)
// ============================================================
(function() {
  'use strict';

  function esc(s) {
    // FIX: all replacements use valid quoted strings (no stray apostrophes)
    // ES5-safe; outputs HTML entities; UTF-8-safe.
    return String(s || '')
      .replace(/&/g, '\u0026amp;')
      .replace(/\u003c/g, '\u0026lt;')
      .replace(/\u003e/g, '\u0026gt;')
      .replace(/\u0022/g, '\u0026quot;')
      .replace(/\u0027/g, '\u0026#39;');
  }
  function initWorkspace(ws) {
    var lid      = ws.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
    var hasExtra = ws.getAttribute('data-sw-has-extra') === '1';
    var mainMax  = parseInt(ws.getAttribute('data-sw-main-max')  || '99', 10) || 99;
    var extraMax = parseInt(ws.getAttribute('data-sw-extra-max') || '9',  10) || 9;
    var predsRaw   = ws.getAttribute('data-sw-preds')   || '[]';
    var modulesRaw = ws.getAttribute('data-sw-modules') || '[]';
    var allPreds, modList;
    try { allPreds = JSON.parse(predsRaw); }   catch(e) { allPreds = []; console.warn('[SW] preds parse error:', e); }
    try { modList  = JSON.parse(modulesRaw); } catch(e) { modList  = []; console.warn('[SW] modules parse error:', e); }
    var srcTag = {skip_hit:'SK',ai_prediction:'NN',mcmc_prediction:'MC',heatmap:'FM',skai_prediction:'SKAI'};
    var activeSources = {}, builderMains = [], builderExtras = [], consensusSet = {};
    var toggles      = ws.querySelectorAll('.sw-source-toggle');
    var candidatesEl = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-candidates]');
    var poolEl       = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-pool]');
    var counterEl    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-counter]');
    var countMains   = counterEl ? counterEl.querySelector('[data-sw-count-mains]')  : null;
    var countExtras  = counterEl ? counterEl.querySelector('[data-sw-count-extras]') : null;
    var addInput     = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-add-input]');
    var addBtn       = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-add-btn]');
    var rmWeakBtn    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-remove-weak]');
    var clearBtn     = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-clear]');
    var saveSection  = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-save-section]');
    var saveMainsEl  = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-save-mains]');
    var saveExtrasEl = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-save-extras]');
    var saveSrcsEl   = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-save-sources]');
    var confLabel    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-conf-label]');
    var confDetail   = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-conf-detail]');
    var confDots     = ws.querySelectorAll('[data-sw-dot]');
    var covList      = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-coverage-list]');
    var covTip       = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-cov-tip]');
    var balLabel     = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-bal-label]');
    var balDetail    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-bal-detail]');
    var whlLabel     = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-wheel-label]');
    var whlDetail    = ws.querySelector('[data-sw-wheel-detail]');

    Array.prototype.forEach.call(toggles, function(cb) {
      activeSources[cb.getAttribute('data-sw-source')] = !!cb.checked;
    });

    function computeCandidates() {
      var bySource = {};
      allPreds.forEach(function(p) {
        if (!activeSources[p.source]) return;
        if (!bySource[p.source]) bySource[p.source] = {mains:[],extras:[]};
        p.mains.forEach(function(n) { if (bySource[p.source].mains.indexOf(n)===-1) bySource[p.source].mains.push(n); });
        p.extras.forEach(function(n){ if (bySource[p.source].extras.indexOf(n)===-1) bySource[p.source].extras.push(n); });
      });
      var sources = Object.keys(bySource), mainCount = {}, mainSrcs = {};
      sources.forEach(function(src) {
        bySource[src].mains.forEach(function(n) {
          mainCount[n] = (mainCount[n]||0)+1;
          mainSrcs[n]  = mainSrcs[n]||[];
          mainSrcs[n].push(srcTag[src]||src.substring(0,2).toUpperCase());
        });
      });
      consensusSet = {};
      Object.keys(mainCount).forEach(function(n){ if (mainCount[n]>=2) consensusSet[parseInt(n,10)]=true; });
      var all = Object.keys(mainCount).map(Number).sort(function(a,b){
        return mainCount[b]!==mainCount[a] ? mainCount[b]-mainCount[a] : a-b;
      });
      return {consensusNums:all.filter(function(n){return mainCount[n]>=2;}),
              supportingNums:all.filter(function(n){return 2 > mainCount[n];}),
              mainCount:mainCount, mainSrcs:mainSrcs, sources:sources};
    }

    function chipHtml(n,count,srcs){
      var c=count>=2, cls='sw-chip'+(c?' sw-chip--consensus':'');
      var bdg=c?'\u003cspan class="sw-chip-badge"\u003e'+count+'+\u003c/span\u003e':'';
      var tgs=srcs&&srcs.length?'\u003cspan class="sw-chip-srcs"\u003e['+srcs.join('][')+']\u003c/span\u003e':'';
      return '\u003cbutton class="'+cls+'" type="button" data-sw-chip-num="'+n+'"'+
             ' aria-label="Add '+n+' to strategy builder"\u003e'+esc(String(n))+bdg+tgs+'\u003c/button\u003e';
    }

    function renderCandidates(d) {
      if (!candidatesEl) return;
      if (!d.sources.length){candidatesEl.innerHTML='\u003cdiv class="sw-empty-state"\u003eSelect a source above.\u003c/div\u003e';return;}
      var h='';
      if (d.consensusNums.length){
        h+='\u003cdiv class="sw-candidate-group-label"\u003eConsensus ('+d.consensusNums.length+')\u003c/div\u003e\u003cdiv class="sw-chips"\u003e';
        d.consensusNums.forEach(function(n){h+=chipHtml(n,d.mainCount[n],d.mainSrcs[n]);});
        h+='\u003c/div\u003e';
      }
      if (d.supportingNums.length){
        h+='\u003cdiv class="sw-candidate-group-label" style="margin-top:.5rem;"\u003eSupporting ('+d.supportingNums.length+')\u003c/div\u003e\u003cdiv class="sw-chips"\u003e';
        d.supportingNums.forEach(function(n){h+=chipHtml(n,d.mainCount[n],d.mainSrcs[n]);});
        h+='\u003c/div\u003e';
      }
      candidatesEl.innerHTML=h||'\u003cdiv class="sw-empty-state"\u003eNo prediction numbers found.\u003c/div\u003e';
    }

    function renderPool(){
      if (!poolEl) return;
      if (!builderMains.length&&!builderExtras.length){
        poolEl.innerHTML='\u003cdiv class="sw-pool-empty"\u003eClick a candidate above to add numbers here.\u003c/div\u003e';
        if (saveSection) saveSection.style.display='none'; return;
      }
      var h='';
      builderMains.forEach(function(n){
        h+='\u003cbutton class="sw-pool-chip" type="button" data-sw-pool-num="'+n+'" data-sw-pool-type="main" aria-label="Remove '+n+'"\u003e'+esc(String(n))+'\u003cspan class="sw-pool-chip-x"\u003e\u00d7\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/button\u003e';
      });
      builderExtras.forEach(function(n){
        h+='\u003cbutton class="sw-pool-chip" style="background:#7c3aed;" type="button" data-sw-pool-num="'+n+'" data-sw-pool-type="extra" aria-label="Remove extra '+n+'"\u003e'+esc(String(n))+'(e)\u003cspan class="sw-pool-chip-x"\u003e\u00d7\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/button\u003e';
      });
      poolEl.innerHTML=h;
      if (saveSection) saveSection.style.display='';
    }

    function updateCounters(){
      if (countMains)  countMains.textContent=String(builderMains.length);
      if (countExtras) countExtras.textContent=String(builderExtras.length);
    }

    function updateSaveFields(){
      var ks=Object.keys(activeSources).filter(function(k){return activeSources[k];});
      if (saveMainsEl)  saveMainsEl.value=builderMains.join(',');
      if (saveExtrasEl) saveExtrasEl.value=builderExtras.join(',');
      if (saveSrcsEl)   saveSrcsEl.value=ks.join(',');
    }

    function updateIntelligence(){
      var tot=builderMains.length, con=builderMains.filter(function(n){return!!consensusSet[n];}).length;
      var rat=tot>0?con/tot:0;
      // Confidence
      var d=0,cs='\u2014',cc='';
      if(tot>0){if(rat>=0.8){cs='Strong';cc='sw-pos';d=5;}else if(rat>=0.5){cs='Moderate';cc='sw-pos';d=3;}else{cs='Low';cc='sw-caut';d=1;}}
      if(confLabel){confLabel.textContent=cs;confLabel.className='sw-intel-label '+cc;}
      if(confDetail)confDetail.textContent=tot>0?'Consensus: '+con+' of '+tot+' ('+Math.round(rat*100)+'%).':'Add numbers to see how strong the agreement is.';
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(confDots,function(dot){
        var i=parseInt(dot.getAttribute('data-sw-dot')||'0',10),on=d >= i;
        dot.classList.toggle('active',on);dot.classList.toggle('high',on&&d>=4);
        dot.classList.toggle('caution',on&&d>0&&2>=d); // 2>=d avoids [..] Joomla filter match
      });
      // Coverage
      if(covList){
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(covList.querySelectorAll('.sw-coverage-item'),function(li){
          var m=li.getAttribute('data-sw-cov-method')||'',cv=false;
          if(tot>0)allPreds.forEach(function(p){if(p.source!==m)return;p.mains.forEach(function(n){if(builderMains.indexOf(n)!==-1)cv=true;});});
          li.classList.toggle('covered',cv);
          var chk=li.querySelector('.sw-coverage-check');if(chk)chk.innerHTML=cv?'\u2713':'\u2717';
        });
        var cc2=covList.querySelectorAll('.sw-coverage-item.covered').length;
        if(covTip)covTip.style.display=(tot>0&&2 > cc2)?'':'none';
      }
      // Balance
      if(tot===0){
        if(balLabel){balLabel.textContent='\u2014';balLabel.className='sw-intel-label';}
        if(balDetail)balDetail.textContent='Add numbers to check balance.';
      }else{
        var ht=false,hm=false;
        builderMains.forEach(function(n){allPreds.forEach(function(p){
          var ri=p.mains.indexOf(n);if(ri===-1)return;var rk=ri+1;
          if(3>=rk)ht=true;if(rk>=4&&10>=rk)hm=true; // >=forms avoid [..] Joomla filter match
        });});
        var bs,bc;
        if(ht&&hm){bs='Balanced';bc='sw-pos';}else if(ht){bs='Top-heavy';bc='sw-caut';}else if(hm){bs='Mid-heavy';bc='sw-caut';}else{bs='Unknown';bc='';}
        if(balLabel){balLabel.textContent=bs;balLabel.className='sw-intel-label '+bc;}
        if(balDetail)balDetail.textContent=(ht&&hm)?'Good mix of top and mid-rank numbers.':(ht?'Mostly top-rank. Try adding mid-rank numbers (#4\u201310).':'Mostly mid-rank. Try adding a top-rank number (#1\u20133).');
      }
      // Wheel readiness
      var ws2,wc,wn;
      if(tot===0){ws2='\u2014';wc='';wn='Add at least 10 main numbers.';}
      else if(tot>=15){ws2='Wheel-ready: Yes';wc='sw-pos';wn=tot===15?'15 numbers is a common wheel base.':'Large enough for most wheeling systems.';}
      else if(tot>=10){ws2='Wheel-ready: Maybe';wc='sw-caut';wn='Small set ('+tot+' mains). Add more for a larger wheel.';}
      else{ws2='Wheel-ready: No';wc='sw-warn';wn='Need at least 10 main numbers ('+tot+' so far).';}
      if(whlLabel){whlLabel.textContent=ws2;whlLabel.className='sw-intel-label '+wc;}
      if(whlDetail)whlDetail.textContent=wn;
    }

    function refresh(){
      var d=computeCandidates();
      renderCandidates(d);renderPool();updateCounters();updateSaveFields();updateIntelligence();
    }

    function addTo(n,isE){
      n=parseInt(n,10);if(!(typeof (n) === 'number' && isFinite(n))||1 > n)return;
      if(isE){if(n>extraMax)return;if(builderExtras.indexOf(n)===-1)builderExtras.push(n);builderExtras.sort(function(a,b){return a-b;});}
      else{if(n>mainMax)return;if(builderMains.indexOf(n)===-1)builderMains.push(n);builderMains.sort(function(a,b){return a-b;});}
      refresh();
    }
    function rmFrom(n,isE){
      n=parseInt(n,10);
      if(isE)builderExtras=builderExtras.filter(function(x){return x!==n;});
      else   builderMains=builderMains.filter(function(x){return x!==n;});
      refresh();
    }

    Array.prototype.forEach.call(toggles,function(cb){
      cb.addEventListener('change',function(){activeSources[cb.getAttribute('data-sw-source')]=!!cb.checked;refresh();});
    });
    if(candidatesEl)candidatesEl.addEventListener('click',function(ev){
      var b=ev.target.closest?ev.target.closest('[data-sw-chip-num]'):null;
      if(b)addTo(b.getAttribute('data-sw-chip-num'),false);
    });
    if(poolEl)poolEl.addEventListener('click',function(ev){
      var b=ev.target.closest?ev.target.closest('[data-sw-pool-num]'):null;
      if(!b)return;rmFrom(b.getAttribute('data-sw-pool-num'),b.getAttribute('data-sw-pool-type')==='extra');
    });
    if(addBtn&&addInput){
      addBtn.addEventListener('click',function(){addTo(addInput.value,false);addInput.value='';addInput.focus();});
      addInput.addEventListener('keydown',function(ev){if(ev.key==='Enter'){ev.preventDefault();addTo(addInput.value,false);addInput.value='';}});
    }
    if(rmWeakBtn)rmWeakBtn.addEventListener('click',function(){builderMains=builderMains.filter(function(n){return!!consensusSet[n];});refresh();});
    if(clearBtn)clearBtn.addEventListener('click',function(){builderMains=[];builderExtras=[];refresh();});
    refresh();
  }

  function bootSW(){
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('[data-sw-workspace]'),initWorkspace);
  }
  if(document.readyState==='loading'){document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',bootSW);}
  else{bootSW();}
}());
// close the top-level DOMContentLoaded wrapper opened at the start of this script
});

/* ===== merged script section ===== */

// ============================================================
// Outer lottery group collapse (mle-lottery-outer)
// Persists state per lottery in localStorage.
// ============================================================
function mleOuterLotteryToggle(outerEl) {
  if (!outerEl) return;
  var lid = outerEl.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-id') || '';
  var storageKey = lid ? ('mle_outer_collapsed_' + lid) : '';
  var btn = outerEl.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle');
  var isCollapsed = outerEl.classList.contains('body-collapsed');
  if (isCollapsed) {
    outerEl.classList.remove('body-collapsed');
    if (btn) { btn.textContent = '\u25bc Collapse'; }
    outerEl.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
    if (storageKey) { try { localStorage.setItem(storageKey, 'false'); } catch(e) {} }
  } else {
    outerEl.classList.add('body-collapsed');
    if (btn) { btn.textContent = '\u25b6 Expand'; }
    outerEl.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
    if (storageKey) { try { localStorage.setItem(storageKey, 'true'); } catch(e) {} }
  }
}

  function scrollToFavorites() {
    var el = document.getElementById('favorite-lotteries');
    if (!el) {
      return;
    }

    // Respect users who prefer reduced motion
    var prefersReduced =
      window.matchMedia &&
      window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches;

    if (prefersReduced) {
      // Jump without animation
      el.scrollIntoView(true);
    } else if (el.scrollIntoView) {
      try {
        el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
      } catch (e) {
        // Fallback for older browsers
        el.scrollIntoView(true);
      }
    }

    // Make the region programmatically focusable and move focus for screen readers
    if (!el.hasAttribute('tabindex')) {
      el.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
    }
    try {
      el.focus();
    } catch (e) {}

    el.classList.add('highlighted-scroll');
    setTimeout(function () {
      el.classList.remove('highlighted-scroll');
    }, 2000);
  }

/* ===== merged script section ===== */

// ============================================================
// Best Setup Snapshot: jump handlers
// "View best" scrolls to a prediction card; "All runs" scrolls
// to the lottery group. ES5-compatible.
// ============================================================
(function initSnapshotJumps() {
  var snap = document.getElementById('skai-global-snapshot');
  if (!snap) { return; }

  snap.addEventListener('click', function (ev) {
    var btn = ev.target;
    if (!btn || btn.tagName !== 'BUTTON') { return; }

    // Helper: smooth scroll with fallback for older browsers
    function scrollTo(el) {
      if (!el) { return; }
      try {
        el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
      } catch (e) {
        el.scrollIntoView(true);
      }
    }

    // "View best"  -  jump to the prediction card for this run
    if (btn.classList.contains('skai-bss-view-btn')) {
      var runId = btn.getAttribute('data-jump-run-id') || '';
      var lid   = btn.getAttribute('data-jump-lottery-id') || '';
      if (runId) {
        // Look for the card by data-set-id first
        var card = document.querySelector('[data-set-id="' + runId + '"]');
        if (card) {
          scrollTo(card);
          return;
        }
      }
      // Fallback: scroll to the lottery group
      if (lid) {
        var grps = document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group');
        for (var i = 0; i < grps.length; i++) {
          var grpLid = (grps[i].getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '').split('-')[0];
          if (grpLid === String(lid)) {
            scrollTo(grps[i]);
            return;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // "All runs"  -  jump to the lottery group for this lottery
    if (btn.classList.contains('skai-bss-all-link')) {
      var crrId = btn.getAttribute('data-jump-crr-id') || '';
      if (crrId) {
        var grps2 = document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group');
        for (var j = 0; j < grps2.length; j++) {
          var grpLid2 = (grps2[j].getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '').split('-')[0];
          if (grpLid2 === String(crrId)) {
            scrollTo(grps2[j]);
            return;
          }
        }
      }
    }
  });
})();

/* ===== merged script section ===== */

// ============================================================
// DEBUG: Prediction Results section diagnostics.
// Set to true to log draw-lookup details to the console.
// ES5-compatible; safe to leave in production (false = silent).
// ============================================================
var DEBUG_PRED_RESULTS = false;
// Override via URL query string: append ?debug_pred_results=1 to enable without redeployment
if (window.location.search && window.location.search.indexOf('debug_pred_results=1') !== -1) {
  DEBUG_PRED_RESULTS = true;
}

(function () {
  if (!DEBUG_PRED_RESULTS) { return; }
  var sections = document.querySelectorAll('.prc-section');
  for (var i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
    var sec = sections[i];
    var pending = sec.querySelectorAll('.prc-row-pending');
    var total   = sec.querySelectorAll('tbody tr:not(.prc-section-subhead)');
    console.log('[PRED-RESULTS] section:', sec.id,
      '| total rows:', total.length,
      '| upcoming rows:', pending.length);
    var upcomingRows = sec.querySelectorAll('tr.prc-row-pending');
    for (var j = 0; j < upcomingRows.length; j++) {
      var cells = upcomingRows[j].querySelectorAll('td');
      console.log('  [UPCOMING] draw date:', cells[1] ? cells[1].textContent.trim() : '?',
        'method:', cells[2] ? cells[2].textContent.trim() : '?');
    }
  }
}());

// ============================================================
// skaiLotteryToggle: Collapse / expand a lottery-group section.
// Called via onclick so it works even if initLotteryCollapse()
// did not run (e.g. due to an earlier JS error in the page).
// ES5-compatible; no dependencies.
// ============================================================
function skaiLotteryToggle(btn) {
  // Find the parent .lottery-group (use closest() with fallback for old browsers)
  var group = btn.closest ? btn.closest('.lottery-group') : (function() {
    var el = btn;
    while (el && !(el.classList && el.classList.contains('lottery-group'))) { el = el.parentElement; }
    return el;
  }());
  if (!group) return;

  var lotteryId  = group.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
  var baseLid    = lotteryId ? lotteryId.split('-')[0] : '';
  var storageKey = baseLid ? ('lottery_collapsed_' + baseLid) : '';
  var isCollapsed = group.classList.contains('collapsed');

  if (isCollapsed) {
    group.classList.remove('collapsed');
    btn.textContent = '\u25bc Collapse';
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Collapse lottery section');
    if (storageKey) { try { localStorage.setItem(storageKey, 'false'); } catch(e) {} }
  } else {
    group.classList.add('collapsed');
    btn.textContent = '\u25b6 Expand';
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
    btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Expand lottery section');
    if (storageKey) { try { localStorage.setItem(storageKey, 'true'); } catch(e) {} }
  }
}

// ============================================================
// skaiLotteryToggleAll: Collapse / expand ALL lottery-group sections
// AND all outer mle-lottery-outer wrappers.
// Updates each group's localStorage key and syncs per-group toggle buttons.
// ES5-compatible; no dependencies.
// ============================================================
function skaiLotteryToggleAll(btn) {
  var groups = document.querySelectorAll('.lottery-group');
  var outers = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-lottery-outer');
  var shouldCollapse = false;
  for (var i = 0; i < groups.length; i++) {
    if (!groups[i].classList.contains('collapsed')) { shouldCollapse = true; break; }
  }
  if (!shouldCollapse) {
    for (var oi = 0; oi < outers.length; oi++) {
      if (!outers[oi].classList.contains('body-collapsed')) { shouldCollapse = true; break; }
    }
  }
  for (var j = 0; j < groups.length; j++) {
    var group      = groups[j];
    var toggle     = group.querySelector('.lottery-collapse-toggle');
    var lotteryId  = group.getAttribute('data-lottery-id') || '';
    var baseLid    = lotteryId ? lotteryId.split('-')[0] : '';
    var storageKey = baseLid ? ('lottery_collapsed_' + baseLid) : '';
    if (shouldCollapse) {
      group.classList.add('collapsed');
      if (toggle) {
        toggle.textContent = '\u25b6 Expand';
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Expand lottery section');
      }
      if (storageKey) { try { localStorage.setItem(storageKey, 'true'); } catch(e) {} }
    } else {
      group.classList.remove('collapsed');
      if (toggle) {
        toggle.textContent = '\u25bc Collapse';
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
        toggle.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Collapse lottery section');
      }
      if (storageKey) { try { localStorage.setItem(storageKey, 'false'); } catch(e) {} }
    }
  }
  // Also toggle outer lottery wrappers
  for (var ok = 0; ok < outers.length; ok++) {
    var outerEl   = outers[ok];
    var outerLid  = outerEl.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-id') || '';
    var outerKey  = outerLid ? ('mle_outer_collapsed_' + outerLid) : '';
    var outerBtn  = outerEl.querySelector('.mle-lottery-outer-toggle');
    if (shouldCollapse) {
      outerEl.classList.add('body-collapsed');
      if (outerBtn) { outerBtn.textContent = '\u25b6 Expand'; }
      if (outerKey) { try { localStorage.setItem(outerKey, 'true'); } catch(e) {} }
    } else {
      outerEl.classList.remove('body-collapsed');
      if (outerBtn) { outerBtn.textContent = '\u25bc Collapse'; }
      if (outerKey) { try { localStorage.setItem(outerKey, 'false'); } catch(e) {} }
    }
  }
  if (btn) {
    btn.textContent = shouldCollapse ? '\u25b6 Expand All' : '\u25bc Collapse All';
  }
}

// ============================================================
// initRunSelector: handles checkbox-based multi-run overlay
// on the run-selector table. Also supports keyboard activation.
// Standalone -- works even if DOMContentLoaded handler errors out.
// ============================================================
(function initRunSelector() {

  // ---- shared helper: rebuild the live heatmap from all checked rows ----
  function refreshLiveHeatmap(wrap) {
    var liveWrap  = wrap.querySelector('.run-live-heatmap-wrap');
    var liveTitle = wrap.querySelector('.run-live-title');
    var liveGrid  = wrap.querySelector('.run-live-grid');
    if (!liveWrap || !liveGrid) return;

    // Collect data from checked rows
    var checkedData = [];
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(wrap.querySelectorAll('.run-selector-check:checked'), function(cb) {
      var row = cb.closest ? cb.closest('.run-selector-row') : null;
      if (!row) return;
      var jsonStr = row.getAttribute('data-run-json');
      if (!jsonStr) return;
      try { checkedData.push(JSON.parse(jsonStr)); } catch(e) {}
    });

    // Sync .run-selected class to checkboxes
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(wrap.querySelectorAll('.run-selector-row'), function(row) {
      var cb = row.querySelector('.run-selector-check');
      if (cb && cb.checked) { row.classList.add('run-selected'); }
      else                  { row.classList.remove('run-selected'); }
    });

    if (checkedData.length === 0) {
      liveWrap.style.display = 'none';
      return;
    }

    var maxRankMain  = checkedData[0].maxRankMain  || 20;
    var maxRankExtra = checkedData[0].maxRankExtra || 5;
    var hasExtra     = !!checkedData[0].hasExtra;
    var extraLabel   = checkedData[0].extraLabel   || 'Extra';

    // Global max across all selected runs (for consistent colour scaling)
    var globalMax = 1;
    checkedData.forEach(function(d) {
      (d.mainData || []).forEach(function(v) { if (v > globalMax) globalMax = v; });
    });

    function buildRow(rowLabel, rankData, maxRank, altHue, gMax) {
      // Escape rowLabel for safe HTML insertion
      var safeLabel = String(rowLabel).replace(/&/g,'\u0026amp;').replace(/\u003c/g,'\u0026lt;').replace(/\u003e/g,'\u0026gt;').replace(/\u0022/g,'\u0026quot;');
      var html = '\u003ctr\u003e';
      html += '\u003ctd style="text-align:left;font-weight:700;white-space:nowrap;" title="' + safeLabel + '"\u003e' + safeLabel + '\u003c/td\u003e';
      var total = 0;
      var peakRank = -1, peakVal = -1;
      for (var ci = 0; ci < maxRank; ci++) {
        var vi = rankData[ci] || 0;
        total += vi;
        if (vi > peakVal) { peakVal = vi; peakRank = ci + 1; }
      }
      for (var c = 1; maxRank >= c; c++) {
        var v = rankData[c - 1] || 0;
        var cellStyle = '';
        var isPeak = (c === peakRank && v > 0);
        if (v > 0) {
          var hue = (altHue !== undefined)
            ? altHue
            : Math.round(240 * (c - 1) / Math.max(1, maxRank - 1));
          var intensity = v / gMax;
          var light = Math.round(52 - intensity * 8);
          cellStyle = 'background:hsl(' + hue + ',90%,' + light + '%);color:#fff;font-weight:700;';
          if (isPeak) cellStyle += 'outline:2px solid #f59e0b;outline-offset:-2px;';
        }
        html += '\u003ctd style="' + cellStyle + '" title="Rank #' + c + ': ' + v + ' hit(s)"\u003e' + (v || '') + '\u003c/td\u003e';
      }
      html += '\u003ctd style="font-weight:700;"\u003e' + (total || 0) + '\u003c/td\u003e';
      html += '\u003c/tr\u003e';
      return html;
    }

    // Build mains table
    var html = '\u003ctable\u003e';
    html += '\u003cthead\u003e\u003ctr\u003e\u003cth style="text-align:left;"\u003eRun\u003c/th\u003e';
    for (var c2 = 1; maxRankMain >= c2; c2++) html += '\u003cth\u003e' + c2 + '\u003c/th\u003e';
    html += '\u003cth\u003eTotal\u003c/th\u003e\u003c/tr\u003e\u003c/thead\u003e\u003ctbody\u003e';
    checkedData.forEach(function(d) {
      html += buildRow(d.label + ' (Mains)', d.mainData || [], maxRankMain, undefined, globalMax);
    });
    html += '\u003c/tbody\u003e\u003c/table\u003e';

    // Build extra-ball table when relevant
    if (hasExtra) {
      var globalMaxExtra = 1;
      var anyExtraHit = false;
      checkedData.forEach(function(d) {
        (d.extraData || []).forEach(function(v) {
          if (v > globalMaxExtra) globalMaxExtra = v;
          if (v > 0) anyExtraHit = true;
        });
      });
      if (anyExtraHit || checkedData.some(function(d){ return (d.extraData||[]).length > 0; })) {
        html += '\u003cdiv style="margin-top:0.75rem;font-weight:700;font-size:0.85rem;color:#92400e;"\u003e' + extraLabel + '\u003c/div\u003e';
        html += '\u003ctable style="margin-top:0.25rem;"\u003e';
        html += '\u003cthead\u003e\u003ctr\u003e\u003cth style="text-align:left;"\u003eRun\u003c/th\u003e';
        for (var e2 = 1; maxRankExtra >= e2; e2++) html += '\u003cth\u003e#' + e2 + '\u003c/th\u003e';
        html += '\u003cth\u003eTotal\u003c/th\u003e\u003c/tr\u003e\u003c/thead\u003e\u003ctbody\u003e';
        checkedData.forEach(function(d) {
          html += buildRow(d.label + ' (' + extraLabel + ')', d.extraData || [], maxRankExtra, 45, globalMaxExtra);
        });
        html += '\u003c/tbody\u003e\u003c/table\u003e';
      }
    }

    liveGrid.innerHTML = html;
    if (liveTitle) {
      var cnt = checkedData.length;
      liveTitle.textContent = cnt === 1
        ? checkedData[0].label + ' -- Placement vs Actual Draw'
        : cnt + ' predictions -- Comparative Placement vs Actual Draw';
    }
    liveWrap.style.display = 'block';
    try { liveWrap.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' }); } catch(e2) {}
  } // end refreshLiveHeatmap

  // ---- checkbox change handler (handles the heatmap) ----
  document.addEventListener('change', function(ev) {
    var cb = ev.target;
    if (!cb || !cb.classList || !cb.classList.contains('run-selector-check')) return;
    var wrap = cb.closest ? cb.closest('.run-selector-wrap') : null;
    if (!wrap) return;
    refreshLiveHeatmap(wrap);
  });

  // ---- row click handler: toggles the row's checkbox ----
  document.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
    // Only handle clicks on the TR row itself (not on the checkbox directly)
    var row = ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('.run-selector-row') : null;
    if (!row) return;
    // If the click was directly on the checkbox, let it handle itself
    if (ev.target.classList && ev.target.classList.contains('run-selector-check')) return;
    var cb = row.querySelector('.run-selector-check');
    if (!cb) return;
    cb.checked = !cb.checked;
    // Manually dispatch change event since programmatic changes don't fire it
    try { cb.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true })); } catch(e) {}
  });

  // ---- keyboard: Enter or Space on a focused row toggles checkbox ----
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(ev) {
    if (ev.key !== 'Enter' && ev.key !== ' ') return;
    var row = ev.target.closest ? ev.target.closest('.run-selector-row') : null;
    if (!row) return;
    // Prevent page scroll for Space BEFORE any early return
    ev.preventDefault();
    var cb = row.querySelector('.run-selector-check');
    if (!cb) return;
    cb.checked = !cb.checked;
    try { cb.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true })); } catch(e) {}
  });

}());

// ============================================================
// skaiPrcToggle: Collapse / expand a prediction-results table section.
// ES5-compatible; no dependencies.
// ============================================================
function skaiPrcSetCollapsed(sec, collapsed) {
  var body = document.getElementById(sec.id + '-body');
  var hdr  = sec.querySelector('.prc-header');
  var btn  = sec.querySelector('.prc-toggle-btn');
  if (!body) { return; }
  if (collapsed) {
    body.style.display = 'none';
    if (btn) { btn.textContent = '\u25BA Expand'; }
    if (hdr) { hdr.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false'); }
  } else {
    body.style.display = '';
    if (btn) { btn.textContent = '\u25BC Collapse'; }
    if (hdr) { hdr.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true'); }
  }
}

function skaiPrcToggle(sectionId) {
  var sec  = document.getElementById(sectionId);
  if (!sec) { return; }
  var body = document.getElementById(sectionId + '-body');
  if (!body) { return; }

  var isOpen = body.style.display !== 'none';
  skaiPrcSetCollapsed(sec, isOpen);
  try {
    if (isOpen) { localStorage.setItem('prc_collapsed_' + sectionId, 'true'); }
    else { localStorage.removeItem('prc_collapsed_' + sectionId); }
  } catch (e) { /* localStorage unavailable (private browsing / quota) */ }
}

// ============================================================
// skaiPrcConfirmDelete: collect checkbox selections then confirm.
// Populates the hidden delete_set_selected input (CSV) before submit.
// ES5-compatible; no dependencies.
// ============================================================
function skaiPrcConfirmDelete(form, sectionId) {
  // Collect all checked checkboxes in this section
  var checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="prc_del_' + sectionId + '"]');
  var selectedIds = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < checkboxes.length; i++) {
    if (checkboxes[i].checked) { selectedIds.push(checkboxes[i].value); }
  }
  if (selectedIds.length === 0) {
    alert('Please select at least one prediction row to delete.');
    return false;
  }
  // Populate the hidden field  -  guard against missing element
  var hiddenField = document.getElementById('prc-del-val-' + sectionId);
  if (!hiddenField) {
    alert('Could not find the delete field. Please refresh the page and try again.');
    return false;
  }
  hiddenField.value = selectedIds.join(',');
  var msg = selectedIds.length === 1
    ? 'Delete 1 prediction? This cannot be undone.'
    : 'Delete ' + selectedIds.length + ' predictions? This cannot be undone.';
  return confirm(msg);
}

// ============================================================
// skaiPrcClearCheckboxes: Deselect all checkboxes in a PRC table section.
// ES5-compatible; no dependencies.
// ============================================================
function skaiPrcClearCheckboxes(sectionId) {
  var checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="prc_del_' + sectionId + '"]');
  for (var i = 0; i < checkboxes.length; i++) {
    checkboxes[i].checked = false;
  }
}

// ============================================================
// skaiPrcSelectUpcoming: Select only checkboxes whose table row is an
// upcoming (not-yet-scored) prediction.  Past draws are left untouched.
// Upcoming rows carry the CSS class "prc-row-pending" on the <tr>.
// ES5-compatible; no dependencies.
// ============================================================
function skaiPrcSelectUpcoming(sectionId) {
  var checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="prc_del_' + sectionId + '"]');
  for (var i = 0; i < checkboxes.length; i++) {
    var cb = checkboxes[i];
    // Walk up to the closest <tr> and check whether it is an upcoming row
    var row = cb.parentNode;
    while (row && row.nodeName.toUpperCase() !== 'TR') { row = row.parentNode; }
    if (row && row.className && row.className.indexOf('prc-row-pending') !== -1) {
      cb.checked = true;
    }
  }
}

/* ===== merged script section ===== */

// ============================================================
// MyLottoExpert  -  Per-card and per-lottery-group print
// ES5-compatible; no external dependencies.
// ============================================================

// Joomla's text filter strips HTML tags from script-block content before the
// JavaScript reaches the browser.  Writing < and > as their Unicode escapes
// (\u003c / \u003e) prevents the filter from recognising them as HTML while
// still producing the correct characters at JavaScript runtime.
var _LT = '\u003c'; // < angle bracket  -  Joomla-safe
var _GT = '\u003e'; // > angle bracket  -  Joomla-safe

/**
 * HTML-escape helper (XSS-safe output into print window)
 */
function _mleEsc(str) {
  return String(str || '')
    .replace(/&/g, '\u0026amp;')
    .replace(/\u003c/g, '\u0026lt;')
    .replace(/\u003e/g, '\u0026gt;')
    .replace(/\u0022/g, '\u0026quot;');
}

/**
 * Print a single prediction card.
 * Called from the  button on each card.
 */
function mlePrintCard(btn) {
  var card = btn && btn.closest ? btn.closest('.prediction-card') : null;
  if (!card) { return; }
  _mleOpenPrintWindow([card], btn);
}

/**
 * Print all prediction cards in a lottery group.
 * Called from the "Print All" button in the lottery header.
 */
function mlePrintGroup(btn) {
  var group = btn && btn.closest ? btn.closest('.lottery-group') : null;
  if (!group) { return; }
  var cards = group.querySelectorAll(
    '.prediction-card:not(.common-card):not(.prediction-placeholder)'
  );
  _mleOpenPrintWindow(Array.prototype.slice.call(cards), btn, group);
}


function mleHistoricalBuildPrintHtml(sourceNode) {
  if (!sourceNode) {
    return '';
  }

  var wrapper = document.createElement('div');
  var clone = sourceNode.cloneNode(true);
  var i;
  var nodes;

  wrapper.appendChild(clone);

  nodes = wrapper.querySelectorAll('.prc-body');
  for (i = 0; i < nodes.length; i++) {
    nodes[i].style.display = 'block';
    nodes[i].style.visibility = 'visible';
    nodes[i].style.height = 'auto';
    nodes[i].style.maxHeight = 'none';
    nodes[i].style.overflow = 'visible';
  }

  nodes = wrapper.querySelectorAll('.prc-toggle-btn, .btn-secondary, .prc-delete-bar, .prc-del-col, input[type="checkbox"]');
  for (i = nodes.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (nodes[i] && nodes[i].parentNode) {
      nodes[i].parentNode.removeChild(nodes[i]);
    }
  }

  nodes = wrapper.querySelectorAll('th.prc-del-col, td.prc-del-col');
  for (i = nodes.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (nodes[i] && nodes[i].parentNode) {
      nodes[i].parentNode.removeChild(nodes[i]);
    }
  }

  return wrapper.innerHTML;
}

function mleHistoricalPrintShell(title, bodyHtml) {
  var __p = [];
  var __body = String(bodyHtml || '');
  var fullHtml = '';
  var win = null;
  var MLE_HIST_WIN_CLOSE_MS = 120000;

  __p.push(_LT + '!DOCTYPE html' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'html lang="en"' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'head' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'meta charset="UTF-8"' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'meta name="color-scheme" content="light only"' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1"' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'title' + _GT + _mleEsc(String(title || 'Historical Validation')) + _LT + '/title' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'style' + _GT);
  __p.push('html,body{background:#ffffff !important;color:#111111 !important;margin:0;padding:0;color-scheme:light only;}');
  __p.push('body{font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;background:#ffffff !important;color:#111111 !important;margin:0;line-height:1.45;}');
  __p.push('.mle-print-toolbar{position:sticky;top:0;z-index:9999;display:block;padding:12px 16px;background:#0A1A33;color:#ffffff;border-bottom:1px solid #d1d5db;}');
  __p.push('.mle-print-toolbar-title{display:inline-block;font-size:16px;font-weight:700;vertical-align:middle;}');
  __p.push('.mle-print-toolbar-actions{float:right;}');
  __p.push('.mle-print-toolbar-btn{display:inline-block;margin-left:8px;padding:8px 12px;border:0;border-radius:6px;background:#1C66FF;color:#ffffff;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;}');
  __p.push('.mle-print-toolbar-btn-secondary{background:#4b5563;}');
  __p.push('.mle-print-doc{padding:20px;}');
  __p.push('h1,h2,h3{margin:0 0 10px 0;color:#111;}');
  __p.push('.prc-wrap{display:block !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-section{display:block !important;border:1px solid #ccc;border-radius:8px;margin:0 0 18px 0;overflow:visible;page-break-inside:avoid;background:#fff !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-header{display:block !important;padding:10px 12px;background:#f3f4f6 !important;color:#111 !important;border-bottom:1px solid #d1d5db;}');
  __p.push('.prc-header *{color:#111 !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-title{display:block !important;font-size:18px;font-weight:700;color:#111 !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-badge{display:inline-block;margin-left:8px;padding:2px 8px;border:1px solid #bbb;border-radius:999px;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:#111 !important;background:#fff !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-body{display:block !important;padding:0;overflow:visible !important;visibility:visible !important;height:auto !important;max-height:none !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:12px;background:#fff !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-table th,.prc-table td{border:1px solid #d1d5db;padding:6px 8px;text-align:left;vertical-align:top;color:#111 !important;background:#fff !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-table th{background:#f8fafc !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-legend,.prc-toggle-btn,.btn-secondary,button,.prc-delete-bar,.prc-del-col,input[type="checkbox"]{display:none !important;}');
  __p.push('.mle-print-toolbar button{display:inline-block !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-row-best,.prc-row-best td{background:#fff8dc !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-row-hit2,.prc-row-hit2 td{background:#f0fff4 !important;}');
  __p.push('.prc-num,.prc-src{display:inline-block;margin:1px 2px;padding:2px 6px;border:1px solid #ccc;border-radius:999px;color:#111 !important;background:#fff !important;}');
  __p.push('@media print{html,body{background:#fff !important;}body{margin:0 !important;} .mle-print-toolbar{display:none !important;} .mle-print-doc{padding:12px !important;}}');
  __p.push(_LT + '/style' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + '/head' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'body' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'div class="mle-print-toolbar"' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'span class="mle-print-toolbar-title"' + _GT + _mleEsc(String(title || 'Historical Validation')) + _LT + '/span' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'span class="mle-print-toolbar-actions"' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'button type="button" class="mle-print-toolbar-btn" onclick="window.focus();window.print();"' + _GT + 'Print' + _LT + '/button' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'button type="button" class="mle-print-toolbar-btn mle-print-toolbar-btn-secondary" onclick="window.close();"' + _GT + 'Close' + _LT + '/button' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + '/span' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'div style="clear:both;"' + _GT + _LT + '/div' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + '/div' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'div class="mle-print-doc"' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'h1' + _GT + _mleEsc(String(title || 'Historical Validation')) + _LT + '/h1' + _GT);
  __p.push(__body);
  __p.push(_LT + '/div' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + 'script' + _GT);
  __p.push('(function(){');
  __p.push('var printed=false;');
  __p.push('function doPrint(){if(printed){return;} printed=true; window.focus(); window.setTimeout(function(){ try{ window.print(); }catch(e){} }, 250);}');
  __p.push('if(document.readyState==="complete"){window.setTimeout(doPrint, 250);}else if(window.addEventListener){window.addEventListener("load", function(){window.setTimeout(doPrint, 250);});}else if(window.attachEvent){window.attachEvent("onload", function(){window.setTimeout(doPrint, 250);});}');
  __p.push('if(window.addEventListener){window.addEventListener("afterprint", function(){window.close();});}');
  __p.push('window.setTimeout(function(){ try{ window.close(); }catch(e){} }, ' + String(MLE_HIST_WIN_CLOSE_MS) + ');');
  __p.push('})();');
  __p.push(_LT + '/script' + _GT);
  __p.push(_LT + '/body' + _GT + _LT + '/html' + _GT);

  fullHtml = __p.join('');

  try {
    win = window.open(
      '', '_blank',
      'width=1100,height=800,menubar=no,toolbar=yes,location=no,status=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes'
    );
  } catch (e) { win = null; }

  if (!win) {
    return;
  }

  try {
    win.document.open();
    win.document.write(fullHtml);
    win.document.close();
    win.focus();
  } catch (e) {
    try { win.close(); } catch (e2) {}
  }
}

function mleHistoricalHeaderKeydown(event, sectionId) {
  event = event || window.event;
  if (!event) { return true; }
  var key = event.key || event.keyCode;
  if (key === 'Enter' || key === ' ' || key === 13 || key === 32) {
    if (event.preventDefault) { event.preventDefault(); } else { event.returnValue = false; }
    skaiPrcToggle(sectionId);
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}

function mlePrintHistoricalAll() {
  var wrap = document.getElementById('mle-historical-validation-wrap');
  if (!wrap) {
    return;
  }
  mleHistoricalPrintShell('Completed Draw results by Date', mleHistoricalBuildPrintHtml(wrap));
}

function mlePrintHistoricalLottery(btn) {
  var node = btn;
  var section = null;

  while (node && node.nodeType === 1) {
    if (node.className && String(node.className).indexOf('prc-section') !== -1) {
      section = node;
      break;
    }
    node = node.parentNode;
  }

  if (!section) {
    return;
  }

  var lotteryName = section.getAttribute('data-historical-lottery') || 'Historical Validation';
  mleHistoricalPrintShell(String(lotteryName) + ' - Historical Validation', mleHistoricalBuildPrintHtml(section));
}

/**
 * Build a complete, self-contained HTML document containing the formatted
 * prediction report and print it.
 *
 * Strategy:
 *   1. PRIMARY  -  window.open('', '_blank') + win.document.write(html) + win.print()
 *      Opening a blank window synchronously from the click handler is allowed
 *      by popup blockers (the user gesture chain is still active).
 *      win.document.write() avoids blob:/data: URI CSP restrictions.
 *      win.print() definitively prints the NEW window  -  never the Joomla host page.
 *
 *   2. FALLBACK  -  if the popup is blocked, _mlePrintFallback() injects an
 *      in-page overlay and calls window.print() on the host page.
 *      _mlePrintStyles() now includes explicit display:table/table-row/table-cell
 *      overrides scoped to #mle-print-overlay so Bootstrap cannot interfere.
 *
 * @param {Element[]} cards      -  array of .prediction-card elements
 * @param {Element}   triggerEl  -  the button that was clicked
 * @param {Element}   [groupEl]  -  .lottery-group element (optional, for title)
 */
function _mleOpenPrintWindow(cards, triggerEl, groupEl) {
  if (!cards || !cards.length) { return; }

  // -- Resolve lottery title --
  var group = groupEl ||
    (triggerEl && triggerEl.closest ? triggerEl.closest('.lottery-group') : null);
  var lotteryTitle = '';
  if (group) {
    var titleEl = group.querySelector('.lottery-title');
    if (titleEl) { lotteryTitle = titleEl.textContent.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim(); }
  }

  var printDate = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
    year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric'
  });
  var cardCount = cards.length;

  // -- Build each card's HTML --
  var cardsHtml = '';
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(cards, function (card, idx) {
    cardsHtml += _mleBuildCardHtml(card, idx + 1, cardCount);
  });

  // -- Assemble a complete standalone HTML document --
  // The style-tag block is the ONLY stylesheet in the popup window  - 
  // no Joomla CSS, no Bootstrap, no theme overrides.
  // NOTE: _LT/_GT replace literal < > in HTML strings so Joomla's text filter
  // (which runs on script-block content) cannot strip HTML tags from these literals.
   // -- Assemble a complete standalone HTML document --
  // FIX: Use array join so no string literal can ever span lines (ES5-safe).
  var __p = [];
  __p.push(_LT+'!DOCTYPE html'+_GT+_LT+'html lang="en"'+_GT+_LT+'head'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'meta charset="UTF-8"'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'title'+_GT+'My LottoExpert \u2013 Prediction Report'+_LT+'/title'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'style'+_GT);

  // Hard reset: force standard table display values so nothing can override them.
  __p.push('*{box-sizing:border-box;margin:0;padding:0;}');
  __p.push('html,body{padding:24px;background:#fff;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;color:#1f2937;line-height:1.5;}');
  __p.push('table{display:table !important;border-collapse:collapse;border-spacing:0;width:auto;}');
  __p.push('thead{display:table-header-group !important;}');
  __p.push('tbody{display:table-row-group !important;}');
  __p.push('tr{display:table-row !important;}');
  __p.push('td,th{display:table-cell !important;padding:0;vertical-align:top;}');
  __p.push('div,p,span{display:revert;}');
  __p.push('@page{margin:1.8cm 1.5cm;size:auto;}');

  __p.push(_LT+'/style'+_GT+_LT+'/head'+_GT+_LT+'body'+_GT);

  // -- Report header --
  __p.push(_LT+'table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:24px;" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'tr'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'td style="background:#0A1A33;padding:18px 22px;vertical-align:middle;"'+_GT);

  // FIX: keep the whole style attribute in ONE string literal (no split across lines)
  __p.push(_LT+'div style="font-family:Georgia,serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:bold;color:#ffffff;letter-spacing:-0.01em;line-height:1.1;"'+_GT+'My LottoExpert'+_LT+'/div'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:normal;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.65);margin-top:4px;letter-spacing:0.08em;text-transform:uppercase;"'+_GT+'Prediction Report'+_LT+'/div'+_GT);

  __p.push(_LT+'/td'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'td style="background:#0A1A33;padding:18px 22px;vertical-align:middle;text-align:right;"'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;color:#ffffff;"'+_GT
    + 'Printed: '+_LT+'strong'+_GT + _mleEsc(printDate) + _LT+'/strong'+_GT+_LT+'/div'+_GT);

  __p.push(lotteryTitle
    ? (_LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:8.5pt;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.70);margin-top:4px;"'+_GT
        + 'Lottery: ' + _mleEsc(lotteryTitle) + _LT+'/div'+_GT)
    : '');

  __p.push(_LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:8.5pt;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.70);margin-top:4px;"'+_GT
    + cardCount + ' Prediction' + (cardCount !== 1 ? 's' : '') + ' Included'
    + _LT+'/div'+_GT);

  __p.push(_LT+'/td'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'/tr'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'/table'+_GT);

  __p.push(cardsHtml);

  // -- Disclaimer footer --
  __p.push(_LT+'table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-top:28px;" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'tr'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'td style="border-top:1px solid #e5e7eb;padding:10px 0;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:7.5pt;color:#9ca3af;text-align:center;"'+_GT);
  __p.push('Generated by My LottoExpert \u00a0\u2022\u00a0 For personal use only \u00a0\u2014\u00a0 Past results do not guarantee future outcomes.');
  __p.push(_LT+'/td'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'/tr'+_GT);
  __p.push(_LT+'/table'+_GT);

  __p.push(_LT+'/body'+_GT+_LT+'/html'+_GT);

  var fullHtml = __p.join('');

  // -- Try to open an isolated print popup --
  // Opening window.open('') synchronously from the click handler means the
  // browser treats it as a user-gesture-initiated popup -> not blocked.
  // Using document.write() bypasses blob:/data: URI CSP restrictions entirely.
  // win.print() prints the NEW window  -  it can never print the Joomla host page.
  var MLE_WIN_CLOSE_MS = 120000; // 2 minutes: safety-net close if afterprint never fires
  var win = null;
  try {
    win = window.open(
      '', '_blank',
      'width=900,height=700,menubar=no,toolbar=no,location=no,status=no,scrollbars=yes'
    );
  } catch (e) { win = null; }

  if (win) {
    try {
      win.document.open();
      win.document.write(fullHtml);
      win.document.close();
      win.focus();
      win.print();
      try { win.addEventListener('afterprint', function () { win.close(); }); } catch (e) {}
      setTimeout(function () { try { win.close(); } catch (e) {} }, MLE_WIN_CLOSE_MS);
    } catch (e) {
      try { win.close(); } catch (e2) {}
      _mlePrintFallback(cardsHtml, lotteryTitle, printDate, cardCount);
    }
    return;
  }

  // -- Popup blocked: fall back to in-page print overlay --
  _mlePrintFallback(cardsHtml, lotteryTitle, printDate, cardCount);
}

/**
 * In-page print fallback for when the popup is blocked.
 * Injects an overlay div + print CSS, hides the Joomla page,
 * and calls window.print() on the host page.
 */
function _mlePrintFallback(cardsHtml, lotteryTitle, printDate, cardCount) {
  var inner =
    _LT+'table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:24px;" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"'+_GT
    + _LT+'tr'+_GT
    + _LT+'td style="background:#0A1A33;padding:18px 22px;vertical-align:middle;"'+_GT
    +   _LT+'div style="font-family:Georgia,serif;font-size:18pt;font-weight:bold;'
    +         'color:#ffffff;letter-spacing:-0.01em;line-height:1.1;"'+_GT+'My LottoExpert'+_LT+'/div'+_GT
    +   _LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:normal;'
    +         'color:rgba(255,255,255,0.65);margin-top:4px;letter-spacing:0.08em;'
    +         'text-transform:uppercase;"'+_GT+'Prediction Report'+_LT+'/div'+_GT
    + _LT+'/td'+_GT
    + _LT+'td style="background:#0A1A33;padding:18px 22px;vertical-align:middle;text-align:right;"'+_GT
    +   _LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;color:#ffffff;"'+_GT
    +     'Printed: '+_LT+'strong'+_GT + _mleEsc(printDate) + _LT+'/strong'+_GT+_LT+'/div'+_GT
    +   (lotteryTitle
          ? _LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:8.5pt;'
            + 'color:rgba(255,255,255,0.70);margin-top:4px;"'+_GT+'Lottery: '
            + _mleEsc(lotteryTitle) + _LT+'/div'+_GT
          : '')
    +   _LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:8.5pt;'
    +         'color:rgba(255,255,255,0.70);margin-top:4px;"'+_GT
    +     cardCount + ' Prediction' + (cardCount !== 1 ? 's' : '') + ' Included'
    +   _LT+'/div'+_GT
    + _LT+'/td'+_GT
    + _LT+'/tr'+_GT
    + _LT+'/table'+_GT
    + cardsHtml
    + _LT+'table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-top:28px;" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"'+_GT
    + _LT+'tr'+_GT
    + _LT+'td style="border-top:1px solid #e5e7eb;padding:10px 0;'
    +     'font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:7.5pt;'
    +     'color:#9ca3af;text-align:center;"'+_GT
    +   'Generated by My LottoExpert \u00a0\u2022\u00a0 '
    +   'For personal use only \u00a0\u2014\u00a0 '
    +   'Past results do not guarantee future outcomes.'
    + _LT+'/td'+_GT
    + _LT+'/tr'+_GT
    + _LT+'/table'+_GT;

  var overlay = document.createElement('div');
  overlay.setAttribute('id', 'mle-print-overlay');
  overlay.innerHTML = inner;
  document.body.appendChild(overlay);

  var styleEl = document.createElement('style');
  styleEl.setAttribute('id', 'mle-print-css');
  styleEl.textContent = _mlePrintStyles();
  document.head.appendChild(styleEl);

  function _mleAfterPrint() {
    var s = document.getElementById('mle-print-css');
    var o = document.getElementById('mle-print-overlay');
    if (s && s.parentNode) { s.parentNode.removeChild(s); }
    if (o && o.parentNode) { o.parentNode.removeChild(o); }
    window.removeEventListener('afterprint', _mleAfterPrint);
  }
  window.addEventListener('afterprint', _mleAfterPrint);
  window.print();
}

/**
 * Return the minimal CSS injected into the page head during printing.
 * Card layout relies entirely on inline styles  -  only the @media print
 * visibility trick lives here so the rest of the Joomla page is hidden.
 */
function _mlePrintStyles() {
  return '@page{margin:1.8cm 1.5cm;size:auto;}'
    // During print: hide all Joomla page content; show only our overlay.
    // Using display:none (not visibility:hidden) so hidden elements take NO
    // space and don't generate blank pages.
    // body > *:not(#mle-print-overlay) hides every sibling; our overlay is
    // excluded and forced back to static flow so it fills pages naturally.
    + '@media print{'
    + 'body \u003e *:not(#mle-print-overlay){display:none !important;}'
    + '#mle-print-overlay{'
    + 'display:block !important;'
    + 'position:static !important;'
    + 'visibility:visible !important;'
    + 'width:100%;background:#fff;'
    + '}'
    // Force correct table display regardless of Bootstrap/Joomla CSS resets.
    // These rules are injected AFTER all page stylesheets and use !important,
    // so they win over any framework rules that might collapse tables to block/flex.
    + '#mle-print-overlay table{display:table !important;border-collapse:collapse !important;}'
    + '#mle-print-overlay tbody{display:table-row-group !important;}'
    + '#mle-print-overlay tr{display:table-row !important;}'
    + '#mle-print-overlay td,#mle-print-overlay th{display:table-cell !important;vertical-align:top !important;}'
    + '#mle-print-overlay div{display:block !important;}'
    + '#mle-print-overlay span{display:inline !important;}'
    + '#mle-print-overlay *{visibility:visible !important;}'
    + '}'
    // Hidden on screen until print triggers the @media print rules above.
    + '#mle-print-overlay{'
    + 'display:none;'
    + 'font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;'
    + 'font-size:10pt;'
    + 'color:#1f2937;'
    + 'line-height:1.5;'
    + '}';
}

/**
 * Format a NodeList of number elements as a dash-separated string with
 * inline-styled color spans (hits = bold green, misses = gray, drawn = navy).
 * Single-digit numbers are zero-padded for clean visual alignment.
 * @param {NodeList} nodes    -  e.g. querySelectorAll('.match-pill:not(.extra)')
 * @param {boolean}  isExtra  -  true for bonus/powerball ball (uses red palette)
 */
function _mleFormatNums(nodes, isExtra) {
  var parts = [];
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(nodes, function (n) {
    var val = (n.textContent || '').trim();
    if (!val) { return; }
    // Zero-pad single digits for clean column alignment (e.g. "07" not "7")
    if (/^\d$/.test(val)) { val = '0' + val; }
    var inlineStyle;
    if (n.classList.contains('drawn-pill')) {
      inlineStyle = 'font-weight:bold;color:' + (isExtra ? '#991b1b' : '#0A1A33') + ';';
    } else if (n.classList.contains('match-pill')) {
      inlineStyle = 'font-weight:bold;color:' + (isExtra ? '#dc2626' : '#16a34a') + ';';
    } else {
      inlineStyle = 'color:#6b7280;';
    }
    parts.push(_LT+'span style="' + inlineStyle + '"'+_GT + _mleEsc(val) + _LT+'/span'+_GT);
  });
  // Em-dash separator keeps each number visually distinct
  return parts.join(_LT+'span style="color:#d1d5db;padding:0 5px;font-weight:normal;"'+_GT+'\u2014'+_LT+'/span'+_GT);
}

/**
 * Extract data from a .prediction-card DOM node and return professional
 * print HTML using stacked full-width sections + 100% inline styles.
 * Each labeled section occupies its own row (label header + content below),
 * so no side-by-side column squishing occurs.
 * @param {Element} card        -  the .prediction-card DOM element
 * @param {number}  cardIndex   -  1-based index for "Prediction #N of M" label
 * @param {number}  totalCards  -  total card count for the label
 */
function _mleBuildCardHtml(card, cardIndex, totalCards) {

  // -- Method badge --
  var badgeEl = card.querySelector('.source-badge');
  var method  = badgeEl ? badgeEl.textContent.trim() : 'Prediction';

  // -- Run label: walk direct TEXT_NODE children to skip nested .local-time ISO string --
  var runLabel = '';
  var tsLabelEl = card.querySelector('.timestamp-label');
  if (tsLabelEl) {
    var labelParts = [];
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(tsLabelEl.childNodes, function (node) {
      if (node.nodeType === 3) { labelParts.push(node.nodeValue); }
    });
    runLabel = labelParts.join('').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').replace(/\s*[\u2013-]\s*$/, '').trim();
  }

  // -- Saved-at timestamp: prefer data-timestamp attribute (ISO) for accuracy --
  var savedAt = '';
  var savedAtContainer = card.querySelector('.timestamp-container');
  if (savedAtContainer) {
    var iso = savedAtContainer.getAttribute('data-timestamp') || '';
    if (iso) {
      try {
        var d = new Date(iso);
        savedAt = isNaN(d.getTime()) ? iso : d.toLocaleString();
      } catch (e) { savedAt = iso; }
    } else {
      var savedAtEl = savedAtContainer.querySelector('.local-time');
      savedAt = savedAtEl ? savedAtEl.textContent.trim() : '';
    }
  }

  // -- Settings rows --
  var settingRowEls = card.querySelectorAll('.settings-panel .setting-row');
  var settingItems  = [];
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(settingRowEls, function (row) {
    var strong = row.querySelector('strong');
    var lbl    = strong ? strong.textContent.replace(':', '').trim() : '';
    var val    = '';
    Array.prototype.forEach.call(row.childNodes, function (node) {
      if (node === strong) { return; }
      val += (node.nodeType === 3 ? node.nodeValue : node.textContent);
    });
    val = val.trim();
    if (lbl && val) { settingItems.push({ lbl: lbl, val: val }); }
  });

  // -- Hit counts --
  var mainHits  = card.querySelectorAll('.match-pill:not(.extra)').length;
  var extraHits = card.querySelectorAll('.match-pill.extra').length;

  // -- Number sets --
  var drawnMain  = card.querySelectorAll('.drawn-pill:not(.extra)');
  var drawnExtra = card.querySelectorAll('.drawn-pill.extra');
  var predMain   = card.querySelectorAll('.match-pill:not(.extra),.no-match:not(.extra)');
  var predExtra  = card.querySelectorAll('.match-pill.extra,.no-match.extra');

  var hasDrawn   = drawnMain.length > 0 || drawnExtra.length > 0;
  // isUpcoming: empty card with no prediction numbers at all (placeholder)
  var isUpcoming = !hasDrawn && predMain.length === 0 && predExtra.length === 0;
  // isPending: has predicted numbers but the draw hasn't happened yet
  var isPending  = !hasDrawn && (predMain.length > 0 || predExtra.length > 0);

  // -- Build matched-number list for the Match Result section --
  var matchedNums = [];
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(predMain, function (n) {
    if (n.classList.contains('match-pill')) {
      var v = (n.textContent || '').trim();
      if (/^\d$/.test(v)) { v = '0' + v; }
      matchedNums.push(v);
    }
  });
  var matchedExtras = [];
  Array.prototype.forEach.call(predExtra, function (n) {
    if (n.classList.contains('match-pill')) {
      var v = (n.textContent || '').trim();
      if (/^\d$/.test(v)) { v = '0' + v; }
      matchedExtras.push(v);
    }
  });

  // -- Status badge --
  var badgeHtml = '';
  if (isUpcoming) {
    badgeHtml = _LT+'span style="background:#e0f2fe;color:#0369a1;border-radius:3px;padding:3px 10px;'
              + 'font-size:8pt;font-weight:bold;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"'+_GT
              + 'UPCOMING DRAW'+_LT+'/span'+_GT;
  } else if (isPending) {
    badgeHtml = _LT+'span style="background:#fef9c3;color:#854d0e;border-radius:3px;padding:3px 10px;'
              + 'font-size:8pt;font-weight:bold;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"'+_GT
              + 'PENDING DRAW'+_LT+'/span'+_GT;
  } else if (hasDrawn) {
    var hLabel = mainHits + (mainHits === 1 ? ' HIT' : ' HITS');
    if (extraHits > 0) { hLabel += ' + ' + extraHits + ' BONUS'; }
    var hBg = mainHits >= 3 ? '#dcfce7' : (mainHits >= 1 ? '#fef9c3' : '#f3f4f6');
    var hFg = mainHits >= 3 ? '#14532d' : (mainHits >= 1 ? '#854d0e' : '#6b7280');
    badgeHtml = _LT+'span style="background:' + hBg + ';color:' + hFg + ';border-radius:3px;padding:3px 10px;'
              + 'font-size:8pt;font-weight:bold;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"'+_GT
              + _mleEsc(hLabel) + _LT+'/span'+_GT;
  }

  // -- Prediction counter label --
  var counterLabel = (totalCards > 1)
    ? 'PREDICTION #' + cardIndex + ' OF ' + totalCards
    : 'PREDICTION';

  // -- Meta line (run label + saved date) --
  var metaLine = runLabel || '';
  if (savedAt) { metaLine += (metaLine ? '  \u2022  Saved: ' : 'Saved: ') + savedAt; }

  // -- Helper: build a section label row (full-width shaded header) --
  function secLabel(text, bg, fg) {
    return _LT+'tr'+_GT+_LT+'td style="padding:7px 16px;background:' + (bg || '#e8edf5')
      + ';border-top:1.5px solid #c7d2e6;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;'
      + 'font-size:7pt;font-weight:bold;color:' + (fg || '#0A1A33')
      + ';text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;"'+_GT + text + _LT+'/td'+_GT+_LT+'/tr'+_GT;
  }

  // -- Helper: build a section content row (full-width white content area) --
  function secContent(innerHtml, bg) {
    return _LT+'tr'+_GT+_LT+'td style="padding:12px 16px 14px;background:' + (bg || '#ffffff')
      + ';border-bottom:1px solid #e5e9f0;"'+_GT + innerHtml + _LT+'/td'+_GT+_LT+'/tr'+_GT;
  }

  // -- Helper: render a NodeList as a large bold number line with dash separators --
  //    extraNodes is optional (bonus ball, rendered smaller + labeled)
  function numLine(mainNodes, extraNodes) {
    var mainStr = _mleFormatNums(mainNodes, false);
    var html    = _LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:16pt;'
                + 'font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:3px;line-height:1.5;color:#1f2937;"'+_GT
                + (mainStr || _LT+'span style="font-style:normal;font-size:9pt;color:#9ca3af;"'+_GT+'N/A'+_LT+'/span'+_GT)
                + _LT+'/div'+_GT;
    if (extraNodes && extraNodes.length) {
      var extraStr = _mleFormatNums(extraNodes, true);
      if (extraStr) {
        html += _LT+'div style="margin-top:8px;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;'
              + 'font-size:9pt;color:#6b7280;letter-spacing:0;"'+_GT
              + _LT+'span style="font-weight:bold;color:#991b1b;text-transform:uppercase;'
              + 'letter-spacing:0.06em;font-size:7pt;"'+_GT+'Bonus Ball:\u00a0'+_LT+'/span'+_GT
              + _LT+'span style="font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;letter-spacing:2px;"'+_GT
              + extraStr + _LT+'/span'+_GT
              + _LT+'/div'+_GT;
      }
    }
    return html;
  }

// -- Assemble card HTML --
var S_TBL = 'style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"';

// FIX: Build with array join to prevent any possibility of newline-in-string-literal (ES5-safe).
var __h = [];

// Card wrapper
__h.push(_LT+'div style="margin-bottom:28px;page-break-inside:avoid;border:1.5px solid #c7d2e6;border-radius:6px;overflow:hidden;"'+_GT);

// -- Card header: dark navy bar --
__h.push(_LT+'table ' + S_TBL + _GT);
__h.push(_LT+'tr'+_GT);

// Left header cell
__h.push(_LT+'td style="background:#0A1A33;padding:12px 16px;vertical-align:middle;"'+_GT);

// Left label
__h.push(_LT+'span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:7pt;font-weight:bold;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.5);letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase;"'+_GT);
__h.push(_mleEsc(counterLabel));
__h.push(_LT+'/span'+_GT);

// Method title
__h.push(_LT+'span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:13pt;font-weight:bold;color:#ffffff;margin-left:12px;"'+_GT);
__h.push(_mleEsc(method.toUpperCase()));
__h.push(_LT+'/span'+_GT);

__h.push(_LT+'/td'+_GT);

// Right badge cell
__h.push(_LT+'td style="background:#0A1A33;padding:12px 16px;vertical-align:middle;text-align:right;white-space:nowrap;"'+_GT);
__h.push(badgeHtml);
__h.push(_LT+'/td'+_GT);

__h.push(_LT+'/tr'+_GT);

// Optional meta row (KEEP INSIDE SAME TABLE)
if (metaLine) {
  __h.push(_LT+'tr'+_GT);
  __h.push(_LT+'td colspan="2" style="background:#0f2340;padding:5px 16px;"'+_GT);
  __h.push(_LT+'span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:8pt;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.65);"'+_GT);
  __h.push(_mleEsc(metaLine));
  __h.push(_LT+'/span'+_GT);
  __h.push(_LT+'/td'+_GT);
  __h.push(_LT+'/tr'+_GT);
}

__h.push(_LT+'/table'+_GT);

// Commit assembled header HTML to string
var html = __h.join('');
  // -- Section rows --
  html += _LT+'table ' + S_TBL + _GT;

  // 1. YOUR PREDICTED NUMBERS
  if (predMain.length > 0 || predExtra.length > 0) {
    html += secLabel('Your Predicted Numbers');
    html += secContent(numLine(predMain, predExtra));
  }

  // 2. OFFICIAL DRAWN NUMBERS (always shown so users understand the draw status)
  html += secLabel('Official Drawn numbers');
  if (hasDrawn) {
    html += secContent(numLine(drawnMain, drawnExtra));
  } else {
     // FIX: Avoid any chance of a literal newline being injected into a quoted string
    // by keeping message text in short, safe literals and escaping the em dash.
    var _mleDrawMsg = isPending
      ? ('Draw results not yet available \u2014 check back after the draw date.')
      : ('Upcoming draw.');

    var drawStatus =
      _LT+'span style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-style:italic;color:#9ca3af;"'+_GT
      + _mleDrawMsg
      + _LT+'/span'+_GT;
    html += secContent(drawStatus);
  }

  // 3. MATCH RESULT (only shown when there are actual drawn numbers to compare)
  if (hasDrawn) {
    html += secLabel('Match Result', '#f0fdf4', '#166534');
    var matchLines = '';

    // Primary summary line
    var matchCount = mainHits + ' of ' + predMain.length + ' main number'
                   + (predMain.length !== 1 ? 's' : '') + ' matched';
    matchLines += _LT+'div style="font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10.5pt;'
                + 'font-weight:bold;color:#15803d;"'+_GT + matchCount + _LT+'/div'+_GT;

    // Matching numbers line
    if (matchedNums.length > 0) {
      matchLines += _LT+'div style="margin-top:5px;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;'
                  + 'font-size:9pt;color:#374151;"'+_GT
                  + _LT+'span style="font-weight:bold;color:#0A1A33;"'+_GT+'Matching Numbers:\u00a0'+_LT+'/span'+_GT
                  + matchedNums.join('\u00a0 \u2022 \u00a0')
                  + _LT+'/div'+_GT;
    } else {
      matchLines += _LT+'div style="margin-top:5px;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;'
                  + 'font-size:9pt;color:#9ca3af;font-style:italic;"'+_GT+'No main numbers matched.'+_LT+'/div'+_GT;
    }

    // Bonus ball line
    if (predExtra.length > 0) {
      var bonusLine = extraHits + ' of ' + predExtra.length + ' bonus ball'
                    + (predExtra.length !== 1 ? 's' : '') + ' matched';
      if (matchedExtras.length > 0) {
        bonusLine += ' \u2014 ' + matchedExtras.join(', ');
      }
      matchLines += _LT+'div style="margin-top:5px;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;'
                  + 'font-size:9pt;color:#374151;"'+_GT
                  + _LT+'span style="font-weight:bold;color:#0A1A33;"'+_GT+'Bonus Ball:\u00a0'+_LT+'/span'+_GT
                  + bonusLine
                  + _LT+'/div'+_GT;
    }

    html += secContent(matchLines, '#f0fdf4');
  }

  // 4. SETTINGS USED (2-column mini-table; falls back to saved-date-only)
  if (settingItems.length > 0 || savedAt) {
    html += secLabel('Settings Used to Generate This Prediction');
    var settingsHtml = '';

    if (settingItems.length > 0) {
      // 2-column table: key: value pairs with room to breathe
      settingsHtml += _LT+'table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"'+_GT;
      var PER_ROW = 2;
      Array.prototype.forEach.call(settingItems, function (item, i) {
        if (i % PER_ROW === 0) { settingsHtml += _LT+'tr'+_GT; }
        settingsHtml += _LT+'td style="padding:4px 16px 4px 0;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;'
                      + 'font-size:9pt;color:#374151;vertical-align:top;width:50%;"'+_GT
                      + _LT+'span style="font-weight:bold;color:#0A1A33;"'+_GT + _mleEsc(item.lbl) + ':\u00a0'+_LT+'/span'+_GT
                      + _mleEsc(item.val) + _LT+'/td'+_GT;
        if ((i + 1) % PER_ROW === 0) { settingsHtml += _LT+'/tr'+_GT; }
      });
      if (settingItems.length % PER_ROW !== 0) {
        settingsHtml += _LT+'td'+_GT+_LT+'/td'+_GT+_LT+'/tr'+_GT;
      }
      settingsHtml += _LT+'/table'+_GT;
    }

    if (savedAt) {
      settingsHtml += _LT+'div style="margin-top:' + (settingItems.length > 0 ? '7' : '0')
                    + 'px;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:8.5pt;color:#6b7280;"'+_GT
                    + _LT+'span style="font-weight:bold;color:#374151;"'+_GT+'Saved:\u00a0'+_LT+'/span'+_GT
                    + _mleEsc(savedAt) + _LT+'/div'+_GT;
    }

    html += secContent(settingsHtml);
  }

  html += _LT+'/table'+_GT;  // end section rows
  html += _LT+'/div'+_GT;    // end card wrapper
  return html;
}

// What to focus on now collapse helpers
function skaiCiSetCollapsed(sectionId, collapsed) {
  var sec = document.getElementById(sectionId);
  if (!sec) { return; }
  var body = document.getElementById(sectionId + '-body');
  var header = sec.querySelector('.prc-header');
  var btn = sec.querySelector('.prc-toggle-btn');
  if (body) { body.style.display = collapsed ? 'none' : ''; }
