  if (header) { header.setAttribute('aria-expanded', collapsed ? 'false' : 'true'); }
  if (btn) {
    btn.innerHTML = collapsed ? '&#x25BA; Expand' : '&#x25BC; Collapse';
    btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', collapsed ? 'false' : 'true');
  }
  try { localStorage.setItem('mle_ci_collapsed_' + sectionId, collapsed ? 'true' : 'false'); } catch (e) {}
}
function mleCiHeaderKeydown(event, sectionId) {
  event = event || window.event;
  if (!event) { return true; }
  var key = event.key || event.keyCode;
  if (key === 'Enter' || key === ' ' || key === 13 || key === 32) {
    if (event.preventDefault) { event.preventDefault(); } else { event.returnValue = false; }
    skaiCiToggle(sectionId);
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}

function skaiCiToggle(sectionId) {
  var sec = document.getElementById(sectionId);
  if (!sec) { return; }
  var body = document.getElementById(sectionId + '-body');
  var isOpen = !body || body.style.display !== 'none';
  skaiCiSetCollapsed(sectionId, isOpen);
  skaiCiRefreshToggleAll();
}
function skaiCiRefreshToggleAll() {
  var sections = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-ci-section');
  var anyOpen = false;
  for (var i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
    var body = document.getElementById(sections[i].id + '-body');
    if (body && body.style.display !== 'none') { anyOpen = true; break; }
  }
  var allBtn = document.getElementById('mle-ci-toggle-all');
  if (allBtn) {
    allBtn.innerHTML = anyOpen ? '&#x25BC; Collapse all' : '&#x25BA; Expand all';
    allBtn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', anyOpen ? 'true' : 'false');
  }
}
function skaiCiToggleAll() {
  var sections = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-ci-section');
  var shouldCollapse = false;
  for (var i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
    var body = document.getElementById(sections[i].id + '-body');
    if (body && body.style.display !== 'none') { shouldCollapse = true; break; }
  }
  for (var j = 0; j < sections.length; j++) {
    skaiCiSetCollapsed(sections[j].id, shouldCollapse);
  }
  skaiCiRefreshToggleAll();
}
(function () {
  var sections = document.querySelectorAll('.mle-ci-section');
  for (var i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
    var sec = sections[i];
    var collapsed = false;
    try { collapsed = localStorage.getItem('mle_ci_collapsed_' + sec.id) === 'true'; } catch (e) {}
    skaiCiSetCollapsed(sec.id, collapsed);
  }
  skaiCiRefreshToggleAll();
})();

if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
  window.skaiCiToggle = skaiCiToggle;
  window.skaiCiToggleAll = skaiCiToggleAll;
  window.mleCiHeaderKeydown = mleCiHeaderKeydown;
  window.skaiPrcToggle = skaiPrcToggle;
  window.mleHistoricalHeaderKeydown = mleHistoricalHeaderKeydown;
  window.mlePrintHistoricalAll = mlePrintHistoricalAll;
  window.mlePrintHistoricalLottery = mlePrintHistoricalLottery;
  window.skaiLotteryToggle = skaiLotteryToggle;
  window.skaiLotteryToggleAll = skaiLotteryToggleAll;
  window.mleOuterLotteryToggle = mleOuterLotteryToggle;
  window.mlePrintCard = mlePrintCard;
  window.mlePrintGroup = mlePrintGroup;
}

document.addEventListener('click', function(evt) {
  var target = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  var node = target;

  while (node && node.nodeType === 1) {
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle')) {
      skaiCiToggle(node.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle-btn') === '1') {
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); } else { evt.cancelBubble = true; }
      skaiCiToggle(node.getAttribute('data-ci-id'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.id === 'mle-ci-toggle-all') {
      skaiCiToggleAll();
      return;
    }
    if (node.id === 'mle-print-historical-all') {
      mlePrintHistoricalAll();
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle')) {
      skaiPrcToggle(node.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle-btn') === '1') {
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); } else { evt.cancelBubble = true; }
      skaiPrcToggle(node.getAttribute('data-prc-id'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-print-lottery') === '1') {
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); } else { evt.cancelBubble = true; }
      mlePrintHistoricalLottery(node);
      return;
    }
    if (node.id === 'mle-go-to-favorites-btn') {
      if (typeof scrollToFavorites === 'function') { scrollToFavorites(); }
      return;
    }
    node = node.parentNode;
  }
});

document.addEventListener('keydown', function(evt) {
  evt = evt || window.event;
  var target = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  if (!target || !target.getAttribute) { return; }

  if (target.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle')) {
    mleCiHeaderKeydown(evt, target.getAttribute('data-ci-toggle'));
    return;
  }
  if (target.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle')) {
    mleHistoricalHeaderKeydown(evt, target.getAttribute('data-prc-toggle'));
    return;
  }
});


document.addEventListener('click', function(evt) {
  var target = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  var node = target;

  while (node && node.nodeType === 1) {
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-clear-btn') === '1') {
      skaiPrcClearCheckboxes(node.getAttribute('data-prc-section-id'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-prc-select-upcoming-btn') === '1') {
      skaiPrcSelectUpcoming(node.getAttribute('data-prc-section-id'));
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-lottery-toggle-all-btn') === '1') {
      skaiLotteryToggleAll(node);
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-lottery-toggle-btn') === '1') {
      skaiLotteryToggle(node);
      return;
    }
    // Outer lottery-group toggle (new two-level grouping)
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-toggle-btn') !== null) {
      var outerEl = node.closest ? node.closest('.mle-lottery-outer') : (function() {
        var el = node;
        while (el && !(el.classList && el.classList.contains('mle-lottery-outer'))) { el = el.parentElement; }
        return el;
      }());
      if (outerEl) { mleOuterLotteryToggle(outerEl); }
      if (evt.stopPropagation) { evt.stopPropagation(); } else { evt.cancelBubble = true; }
      return;
    }
    // Click on the outer header itself (anywhere except the inner button)
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-outer-lottery-toggle') !== null) {
      var outerEl2 = node.closest ? node.closest('.mle-lottery-outer') : (function() {
        var el = node;
        while (el && !(el.classList && el.classList.contains('mle-lottery-outer'))) { el = el.parentElement; }
        return el;
      }());
      if (outerEl2) { mleOuterLotteryToggle(outerEl2); }
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-print-group-btn') === '1') {
      mlePrintGroup(node);
      return;
    }
    if (node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('data-print-card-btn') === '1') {
      mlePrintCard(node);
      return;
    }
    node = node.parentNode;
  }
});

document.addEventListener('change', function(evt) {
  var target = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  if (!target || !target.getAttribute) { return; }
  if (target.getAttribute('data-auto-submit-select') === '1' && target.form && typeof target.form.submit === 'function') {
    target.form.submit();
  }
});

document.addEventListener('submit', function(evt) {
  evt = evt || window.event;
  var form = evt.target || evt.srcElement;
  if (!form || !form.getAttribute) { return; }

  if (form.getAttribute('data-prc-delete-form') === '1') {
    if (!skaiPrcConfirmDelete(form, form.getAttribute('data-prc-section-id'))) {
      if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); } else { evt.returnValue = false; }
    }
    return;
  }

  var msg = form.getAttribute('data-confirm-submit');
  if (msg) {
    if (!window.confirm(msg)) {
      if (evt.preventDefault) { evt.preventDefault(); } else { evt.returnValue = false; }
    }
  }
});

/**
 * mleToggleNoteEditor - show or hide the inline note editor for a saved settings card.
 * @param {number}  settingId - DB id of the saved settings row
 * @param {boolean} show      - true = open editor, false = close editor
 */
function mleToggleNoteEditor(settingId, show) {
  var editor  = document.getElementById('mle-note-editor-'  + settingId);
  var display = document.getElementById('mle-note-display-' + settingId);
  if (!editor) { return; }
  editor.style.display  = show ? 'block' : 'none';
  if (display) { display.style.display = show ? 'none' : (display.textContent.trim() ? 'block' : 'none'); }
  if (show) {
    var ta = editor.querySelector('textarea');
    if (ta) { ta.focus(); }
  }
}

/**
 * mleSaveNote - submit the note form via fetch so the page does not reload.
 * Falls back to normal form submit if fetch is unavailable.
 * @param {Event}  evt       - form submit event
 * @param {number} settingId - DB id of the saved settings row
 */
function mleSaveNote(evt, settingId) {
  evt.preventDefault();
  var form = evt.target;
  if (typeof fetch === 'undefined') { form.submit(); return false; }
  var data = new FormData(form);
  fetch(window.location.href, { method: 'POST', body: data, credentials: 'same-origin' })
    .then(function(r) { return r.ok ? r.text() : Promise.reject(r.status); })
    .then(function() {
      var ta      = form.querySelector('textarea[name="user_notes"]');
      var noteVal = ta ? ta.value.trim() : '';
      var display = document.getElementById('mle-note-display-' + settingId);
      if (display) {
        display.innerHTML = noteVal
          ? '<strong style="color:#334155;">Note:</strong> ' + noteVal.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/\n/g,'<br>')
          : '';
        display.style.display = noteVal ? 'block' : 'none';
      }
      // Update "Add Note / Edit Note" toggle buttons using data-note-toggle attribute
      var btns = document.querySelectorAll('[data-note-toggle="' + settingId + '"]');
      for (var i = 0; i < btns.length; i++) {
        btns[i].innerHTML = (noteVal ? '&#x1F4DD; Edit Note' : '&#x1F4DD; Add Note');
      }
      mleToggleNoteEditor(settingId, false);
    })
    .catch(function(err) {
      // Inform the user before falling back to a full-page submit
      var statusMsg = err ? ' (status ' + err + ')' : '';
      if (window.console) { console.warn('[MLE] Note save via fetch failed' + statusMsg + '; retrying via form submit.'); }
      form.submit();
    });
  return false;
}

/**
 * mleApplyRecallSettings - "Use these settings" button handler.
 * Stores the saved settings in sessionStorage under 'mle_recall_settings' so that the
 * SKAI page can read and apply them on load, then navigates to the lottery's SKAI page.
 * Falls back to the in-page CustomEvent approach (mylottoRecallSettings) if the user is
 * already on the SKAI page or no destination URL is stored for this lottery.
 * @param {HTMLElement} btn       - the button element that was clicked
 * @param {number}      settingId - DB id of the saved settings row
 * @param {number}      lotteryId - Lottery this template belongs to
 */
function mleApplyRecallSettings(btn, settingId, lotteryId) {
  var raw = btn ? btn.getAttribute('data-mle-params') : null;
  var params;
  try { params = raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null; } catch (e) { params = null; }
  if (!params) { return; }

  var destUrl  = (btn ? btn.getAttribute('data-mle-lottery-url') : null) || '';
  var gameId   = (btn ? btn.getAttribute('data-mle-game-id')     : null) || '';
  var source   = (btn ? btn.getAttribute('data-mle-source')       : null) || '';

  // Build the recall payload to hand off to the SKAI page
  var payload = {
    settingId : settingId,
    lotteryId : lotteryId,
    gameId    : gameId,
    source    : source,
    params    : params
  };

  // If there is a known destination URL for this lottery, navigate there.
  // The SKAI page will read the sessionStorage payload and auto-apply the settings.
  if (destUrl && destUrl !== '' && destUrl !== '#') {
    try {
      sessionStorage.setItem('mle_recall_settings', JSON.stringify(payload));
    } catch (ssErr) {
      if (window.console) { console.warn('[MLE] sessionStorage unavailable:', ssErr); }
    }
    // Navigate; append a flag so the SKAI page knows to look for recall data
    var sep = (destUrl.indexOf('?') === -1) ? '?' : '&';
    window.location.href = destUrl + sep + 'mle_recall=1';
    return;
  }

  // No destination URL - fall back to in-page fill (works if SKAI is on the same page)
  if (typeof mylottoRecallSettings === 'function') {
    mylottoRecallSettings(settingId, lotteryId, params);
  }
}

/**
 * mylottoRecallSettings - populate the active prediction form with a saved settings template.
 * Dispatches a custom event 'mylotto:recall-settings' with the params payload so that any
 * page-level handler (Sky, AI, SKAI, etc.) can apply the values to its own form fields.
 * Falls back to a console notice if no handler is registered.
 *
 * @param {number} settingId    - DB id of the saved settings template
 * @param {number} lotteryId    - Lottery this template belongs to
 * @param {Object} params       - Key/value map of the saved settings params
 */
function mylottoRecallSettings(settingId, lotteryId, params) {
  if (typeof params !== 'object' || params === null) { return; }
  var detail = { settingId: settingId, lotteryId: lotteryId, params: params };
  var evt = null;
  try {
    evt = new CustomEvent('mylotto:recall-settings', { bubbles: true, cancelable: true, detail: detail });
  } catch (e) {
    // IE11 fallback
    evt = document.createEvent('CustomEvent');
    evt.initCustomEvent('mylotto:recall-settings', true, true, detail);
  }
  var handled = document.dispatchEvent(evt);
  // dispatchEvent() returns false only if a handler called evt.preventDefault() to signal it took
  // exclusive ownership. When handled === true (no handler cancelled), do a best-effort form fill
  // by matching input/select elements by name attribute.
  if (handled) {
    var filled = 0;
    for (var k in params) {
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(params, k)) { continue; }
      var els = document.querySelectorAll('[name="' + k + '"], [data-setting-key="' + k + '"]');
      for (var i = 0; i < els.length; i++) {
        var el = els[i];
        if (el.tagName === 'SELECT') {
          for (var j = 0; j < el.options.length; j++) {
            if (String(el.options[j].value) === String(params[k])) { el.selectedIndex = j; filled++; break; }
          }
        } else if (el.type === 'checkbox') {
          el.checked = (String(params[k]) === '1' || String(params[k]).toLowerCase() === 'true');
          filled++;
        } else if (el.type !== 'hidden' && el.type !== 'submit' && el.type !== 'button') {
          el.value = params[k];
          filled++;
        }
      }
    }
    if (filled > 0) {
      // Trigger change events so reactive UI updates
      var allInputs = document.querySelectorAll('input,select,textarea');
      for (var i2 = 0; i2 < allInputs.length; i2++) {
        try { allInputs[i2].dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true })); } catch(e2) {}
      }
    }
  }
}

</script>
